### [38] [Evaluation Pitfalls and Challenges in Multimedia Event Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26775)
*Philipp Seeberger,Steffen Freisinger,Tobias Bocklet,Korbinian Riedhammer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次系统揭示了多模态事件抽取领域在评估标准上的三大缺陷，证明了不规范的评估设置会导致严重的性能偏差，呼吁建立统一且严谨的评估基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多模态事件抽取研究进展迅速，但目前领域内缺乏一致和严格的评估标准，导致不同研究结果之间难以比较，且可能高估了现有模型对现实世界多模态事件的抽取和定位能力。

Method: 通过对现有文献的系统性分析，识别出数据处理不一致、任务假设不统一以及评估设置过于宽松这三大问题。随后，研究者在严格的控制实验框架下，对比不同评估选择对模型性能的影响，量化了这些因素导致的性能差异。

Result: 研究发现，细微的评估选择偏差（如数据预处理、任务定义差异）会导致模型性能出现显著波动，证实了现有研究中普遍存在对模型能力的高估现象。

Conclusion: 多模态事件抽取领域当前缺乏统一且严格的评估标准。为了推动该领域的发展，必须建立更严谨、可比性更强的评估体系，以避免对模型性能的评估偏差和高估。

Abstract: Multimedia event extraction aims to jointly identify events and their arguments across multiple modalities, such as text and images, to support more comprehensive event understanding. While recent work reports steady and substantial progress, the reliability and comparability of these results critically depend on consistent and rigorous evaluation. In this work, we present the first systematic analysis of evaluation pitfalls in multimedia event extraction and identify three major sources of issues: inconsistent data processing, inconsistent task assumptions, and overly relaxed evaluation settings. We demonstrate, through a series of controlled experiments under a strict evaluation framework, that minor evaluation choices can cause large performance variations and lead to overestimation of a model's ability to ground real-world events across modalities. Our findings highlight the need for comparable evaluation standards and encourage a shift toward more rigorous evaluation in multimedia event extraction.

</details>


### [39] [OPID: On-Policy Skill Distillation for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26790)
*Shuo Yang,Jinyang Wu,Zhengxi Lu,Yuhao Shen,Fan Zhang,Lang Feng,Shuai Zhang,Haoran Luo,Zheng Lian,Zhengqi Wen,Jianhua Tao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: OPID 是一种创新的语言智能体训练框架，它通过从自身轨迹中提取分层技能，并结合关键优先的路由机制与上下文增强的自我蒸馏，在不依赖外部记忆的情况下，为智能体提供了分布匹配的高质量密集监督信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于结果的强化学习（RL）虽稳定但存在奖励稀疏问题，而现有的基于技能的自我蒸馏方法通常依赖昂贵的外部记忆或特权上下文，且在多步交互中容易出现分布不匹配的问题。作者旨在设计一种无需外部资源、能从自身轨迹实时获取密集监督信号的训练框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 OPID 的框架：1. 分层技能提取：将轨迹回顾为不同粒度的技能（片段级与步骤级）；2. 关键优先路由机制：根据决策的重要性动态选择技能类型；3. 上下文增强蒸馏：将选定技能注入上下文，通过对比原上下文与增强上下文的对数概率差异，计算出密集的 token 级自我蒸馏优势，并将其整合入强化学习目标中。

Result: 在 ALFWorld、WebShop 和基于搜索的问答任务中，OPID 相比仅使用结果奖励的强化学习方法以及现有的技能蒸馏基准，展现出了更高的任务完成性能、更强的样本效率和更好的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: OPID 通过将基于结果的强化学习与基于策略的自我蒸馏有效结合，成功解决了语言智能体训练中奖励稀疏与技能引导成本高昂的问题。该方法证明了从自身轨迹中提取的分层技能监督能显著提升智能体在复杂多步交互任务中的性能和样本效率。

Abstract: Outcome-based reinforcement learning provides a stable optimization backbone for language agents, but its sparse trajectory-level rewards provide little guidance on which intermediate decisions should be reinforced or suppressed. On-policy self-distillation offers dense token-level supervision, yet existing skill-conditioned variants often rely on external skill memories or retrieved privileged context, which are costly to maintain and can be mismatched with the state distribution induced by the current policy in multi-turn interaction. We propose \textbf{OPID} (\textbf{O}n-\textbf{P}olicy Sk\textbf{i}ll \textbf{D}istillation), a framework that extracts skill supervision directly from completed on-policy trajectories. OPID represents trajectory hindsight as hierarchical skills: episode-level skills capture global workflows or failure-avoidance rules, while step-level skills capture local decision knowledge at critical timesteps. A critical-first routing mechanism uses step-level skills when critical decisions are identified and falls back to episode-level skills as default guidance otherwise. The selected skill is injected into the interaction history, allowing the old policy to re-score the same sampled response under both original and skill-augmented contexts. The resulting log-probability shift yields a token-level self-distillation advantage, which is combined with the outcome advantage for policy optimization. OPID thus preserves RL as the primary training objective while introducing dense, distribution-matched hindsight supervision. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop and Search-based QA demonstrate that OPID generally improves agent performance, sample efficiency, and robustness over outcome-only RL and existing skill-distillation baselines. Our code is available at https://github.com/jinyangwu/OPID/tree/main.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了应对 IWSLT 2026 指令跟随任务，探索在受限环境下提升 SpeechLLMs 在短文本及长文本语音指令跟随中的性能表现及鲁棒性。

Method: 针对短文本任务，利用 SpeechLLMs 进行直接推理；针对长文本任务，对比了三种语音分段方法，并引入了 HIFS 指标以衡量长文本生成稳定性，最终确定固定 30 秒分段策略效果最优。

Result: 在短文本任务上，SIFS 得分为 2.0708；在长文本任务中，固定 30 秒分段策略实现了最优表现，HIFS 得分为 2.0663。分析表明长文本生成中的幻觉问题主要表现为重复插入，且长文本扩展后短文本能力基本未受损。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过合理的任务拆分与针对性的长文本评估指标，SpeechLLM 可以有效处理长短语音指令任务，并指出长文本生成中幻觉现象（特别是重复插入）是当前性能提升的主要瓶颈。

Abstract: This paper describes our submission to the IWSLT 2026 Instruction Following shared task. SpeechLLMs are developed for both short-form and long-form speech instruction following under constrained settings. For the short track, strong performance is achieved on MCIF, with a SIFS score of 2.0708. For the long track, three speech segmentation methods are explored, and the HIFS score is introduced to account for unstable long-form generation. Experimental results show that fixed 30-second segmentation provides the most robust long-form performance, achieving the highest HIFS score of 2.0663. Further analysis shows that hallucination mainly manifests as repetitive insertions in generated outputs, substantially affecting ASR and SSUM, while short-form capabilities are largely retained after long-form extension.

### [41] [Cascaded Multi-Granularity Pruning for On-Device LLM Inference in Industrial IoT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26861)
*Jinghan Wang,Yanjun Chen,Wei Zhang,Xiaotong Huang,Tianchen Liu,Gaoliang Peng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对工业物联网边缘侧大模型部署，本文提出了一种基于结构独立性假设（SIA）的级联多粒度剪枝框架，成功实现了高压缩比与高性能，并揭示了不同模型架构对剪枝稳健性的底层影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有结构化剪枝方法在极高压缩比下容易导致性能崩溃，且其在不同模型架构间的表现难以预测。针对工业物联网（IIoT）边缘设备对轻量化部署的迫切需求，亟需一种能够适应不同架构特征并实现高压缩比的稳健剪枝方案。

Method: 提出了一种级联多粒度剪枝框架，按“层-注意力头-前馈网络通道”的由粗到细顺序进行剪枝，并在各阶段间采用轻量级低秩恢复以重新评估组件重要性。同时，通过信息论分析形式化了“结构独立性假设”（SIA），用以预测特定模型架构剪枝标准的可行性。

Result: 在轴承故障诊断任务中，该框架在MHA+GELU架构上实现了13.8倍的压缩，精度提升3.7个百分点；在符合SIA的架构上验证了其有效性，并在实际工业平台上实现了高达67.2%的延迟降低与62.5%的内存节省。同时揭示了GQA+SwiGLU架构因违反SIA会导致高达74个百分点的精度崩溃。

Conclusion: 该研究通过“结构独立性假设”（SIA）为大型语言模型在工业物联网边缘侧的结构化剪枝提供了理论判据。研究表明，在满足SIA的架构（如MHA+GELU）上，级联多粒度剪枝能实现极高的压缩比与性能平衡，而在违反SIA的架构（如GQA+SwiGLU）上则会发生显著性能衰退，这为工业AI模型的定制化压缩提供了重要的设计指导。

Abstract: Deploying large language models (LLMs) on Industrial Internet of Things (IIoT) edge devices demands extreme compression, yet existing structured pruning methods collapse at high compression ratios due to one-shot importance estimation, and their cross-architecture behavior remains unpredictable. This article presents a cascaded multi-granularity pruning framework that removes layers, attention heads, and feed-forward channels in coarse-to-fine order, with lightweight low-rank recovery between stages to re-estimate component importance. An information-theoretic analysis motivates this ordering, and the Structural Independence Assumption (SIA) is formalized as a checkable condition predicting whether per-component pruning criteria are reliable for a given architecture: Multi-Head Attention (MHA)+GELU designs satisfy the SIA, whereas Grouped Query Attention (GQA)+SwiGLU designs violate it. On bearing fault diagnosis spanning 88M to 6.25B-parameter models, the framework extends achievable compression to 13.8 times on MHA+GELU architectures with 83.82% accuracy (+3.70 percentage points (pp) over the strongest baseline), while exposing a ~74pp accuracy collapse on GQA+SwiGLU architectures that violate the SIA. Deployed on an industrial slewing bearing fault diagnosis platform with NVIDIA DGX Spark, compressed models reduce inference latency by up to 67.2% and peak memory by 62.5%, demonstrating viability for IIoT edge inference.

### [42] [Information-Aware KV Cache Compression for Long Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26875)
*Jushi Kai,Zhuiri Xiao,Alexandra Birch,Zhouhan Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: InfoKV 是一种新型 KV cache 压缩框架，通过引入预测不确定性和表征演化等信息论指标，弥补了传统注意力机制在捕捉长距离依赖时的不足，提升了长文本推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 KV cache 压缩方法过度依赖注意力权重，忽略了对远距离上下文有重要影响的预测不确定性等信息论信号，导致在长文本任务中表现受限。

Method: 提出了“前向影响”（Forward Influence）度量指标，并基于此设计了 InfoKV 框架。该框架将 token 级别的预测不确定性（熵）、层级间的表征演化与传统的注意力评分相结合，实现更智能的 KV cache 压缩。

Result: 在 Llama-3.1、Llama-3.2 和 DeepSeek-R1 等模型上的实验表明，InfoKV 在长文本预填充和解码阶段均显著优于现有的注意力压缩方法。

Conclusion: InfoKV 证明了结合信息论信号（预测不确定性和表征演化）能够比单纯依赖注意力权重的压缩方法更有效地保留对长文本推理至关重要的 KV cache 信息。

Abstract: Reasoning capability has advanced rapidly in large language models (LLMs), leading to an increasing size of key-value (KV) cache in both prefilling and decoding stages. Existing KV cache compression methods mainly rely on attention weights to estimate token importance. While attention effectively captures contextual relevance, it overlooks complementary information-theoretic signals related to predictive uncertainty and token informativeness. In this paper, we revisit token importance from a forward-looking perspective and introduce \textit{Forward Influence}, a metric that measures how compressed tokens affect future contexts. Our analysis reveals that tokens selected by attention scores mainly influence nearby contexts, whereas tokens associated with high predictive uncertainty exhibit substantially stronger influence on distant future contexts. Based on the observation, we propose \textbf{InfoKV}, an entropy-aware KV cache compression framework that incorporates information-theoretic signals. It combines token-level predictive uncertainty with layer-wise representation evolution and integrates the resulting entropy scores with attention scores during reasoning. Experiments on long-context reasoning benchmarks with Llama-3.1, Llama-3.2, and DeepSeek-R1 demonstrate that InfoKV consistently outperforms existing attention-based KV compression methods in both long prefilling and decoding scenarios.

### [43] [Heterogeneous Neural Predictivity from Language Models During Naturalistic Comprehension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26880)
*Xiao Jia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过对多种神经影像数据集的严谨分析，验证了语言模型特征在自然语言理解任务中作为神经活动预测因子的有效性，并明确了预测的有效性与大脑真实计算机制之间的界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管语言模型在预测大脑神经活动方面显示出潜力，但目前尚不清楚这些预测性能是否反映了大脑真实的语言处理机制，还是仅仅因为模型特征捕获了某些相关的统计属性。因此，研究旨在通过严格的控制实验，定量评估语言模型特征作为神经预测因子的有效性及其边界。

Method: 研究团队使用了八种预训练语言模型，结合“分块编码模型”（blocked encoding models），并引入了针对时间、干扰项和表征容量的匹配控制组。通过对Brain Treebank、MEG-MASC和Podcast ECoG数据集进行分析，验证了模型特征对神经信号的预测能力，并通过特征消融实验（ablation studies）评估了预测的特异性。

Result: 分析结果显示，语言模型在大多数源级摘要中展现出了优于低级基准的预测能力。在Brain Treebank和Podcast ECoG数据集中，有67个评估行符合严格的预测控制标准。特征消融实验进一步证实了预测评分对模型特定特征的依赖性，且这种优势在不同参与者间具有局部化特征。

Conclusion: 研究表明，语言模型特征是预测自然语言理解过程中神经活动的有效指标。然而，预测的有效性并不等同于证明模型与人类大脑在处理机制或表征方式上的本质一致性，未来需要更高精度的跨模态数据整合来深入解释二者的联系。

Abstract: Language-model representations provide structured, high-dimensional annotations of naturalistic language stimuli and can serve as informative neural predictors during comprehension. We analyzed locked derived data from Brain Treebank, MEG-MASC, and Podcast ECoG with eight frozen language models, blocked encoding models, and matched temporal, nuisance, and representation-capacity controls. Positive held-out prediction and gains over low-level baselines were widespread in source-level summaries. Across Brain Treebank and Podcast ECoG, 67 of 432 evaluable rows met a controlled predictive-only criterion, and model-side feature ablations changed prediction scores in most evaluable source rows. Brain-derived, timing-linked, acoustic, and implanted-signal controls confirmed component-level sensitivity of the analysis pipeline. These findings show that language-model-derived quantities can annotate neural activity during natural speech and text comprehension. Participant-level matched-control advantages were localized rather than uniform, response-profile and feature-specificity contrasts bounded representational or computational interpretations, and complete co-indexed integrated interpretation will require future jointly indexed coverage. Together, the analyses identify language-model features as useful neural predictors and separate predictive usefulness from claims about shared neural organization or language-processing computations.

### [44] [SamaVaani: Auditing and Debiasing Multilingual Clinical ASR for Indian Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26901)
*Subham Kumar,Prakrithi Shivaprakash,Abhishek Manoharan,Astut Kurariya,Diptadhi Mukherjee,Prabhat Chand,Pratima Murthy,Koustav Rudra,Lekhansh Shukla,Animesh Mukherjee*

Abstract: Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) is increasingly used to document clinical encounters, yet its reliability in multilingual and demographically diverse Indian healthcare context remains largely unknown. With this, we uncover systematic performance gaps tied to speaker role and gender, raising concerns about equitable deployment in clinical settings, which are further mitigated by fairness-aware fine-tuning. To this end, we propose SamaVaani, a unified debiasing technique that simultaneously improves ASR performance and improves fairness across demographic groups.

### [47] [RedVox: Safety and Fairness Gaps in Speech Models Across Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26968)
*Beatrice Savoldi,Sara Papi,Wafa Aissa,Matteo Negri,Luisa Bentivogli*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RedVox是一项针对多语言语音模型安全性与公平性的研究。该研究发现主流语音模型在非英语语种及现实语音输入下表现出更高的安全风险，并发布了多语言语音安全基准以弥补该领域的研究空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语音模型在全球范围内的应用日益广泛，但针对英语以外语种及自然环境下的安全性与公平性研究严重匮乏，且现有模型的安全文档披露率极低。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了多语言语音模型在安全性方面的严重不足，强调了跨语言评估与现实语音数据对于构建安全人工智能的重要性，并呼吁在语音数据收集过程中更加关注参与者的隐私与伦理问题。

Abstract: Speech-capable models are increasingly deployed in real-world applications across languages. Yet their safety and fairness beyond English settings and under naturalistic conditions remain understudied. We survey safety reporting practices across state-of-the-art speech model releases, finding that only 8% document any multilingual analysis. To address this gap, we introduce RedVox, a multilingual safety and fairness benchmark for audio and speech built on real voices, covering unsafe and unfair stereotypical requests across five languages (English, French, Italian, Spanish, and German). Evaluating eight state-of-the-art models, we find that vulnerabilities persist even under non-adversarial conditions, worsen in non-English languages, and are amplified when the request comes from a spoken input. Finally, by surveying the participants who contributed to RedVox, we document the unique personal and privacy challenges of collecting speech data with human participants, pointing to broader sociotechnical challenges in naturalistic speech safety research.

### [48] [Auditing Framing-Sensitive Behavioral Instability in Large Language Models for Mental Health Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26982)
*Abla Bedoui,Ashley L. Greene,Mohammed Cherkaoui*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型在处理心理健康等敏感任务时，对不同上下文语境表述的敏感性问题。研究发现，语境框架不仅会影响模型行为，还能在模型内部表征中被清晰解码，甚至可以通过干预内部激活状态来调节输出，这对提升AI系统的鲁棒性和可信度具有重要参考价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在心理健康等敏感领域的应用日益增多，模型行为的一致性和稳定性至关重要。然而，语义相同但表述方式不同的上下文可能会导致模型输出产生偏差（框架效应）。目前学术界对这种行为差异在模型内部表征层面的具体体现机制缺乏深入理解，因此研究其如何影响模型的解释倾向与可靠性具有重要意义。

Method: 1. 使用受控的匹配提示词集，涵盖多种上下文语境框架，并应用于多个指令微调模型系列；2. 采用层级探针分析（Layer-wise probing analysis）技术，探究模型内部表征与行为之间的关联；3. 实施激活引导（Activation steering）实验，验证模型内部特定的表征方向是否能调节最终的输出行为。

Result: 1. 语境框架系统性地改变了模型的解释性响应趋势；2. 与行为相关的信息在整个Transformer层级中均可解码，且解码强度因架构而异；3. 即便排除词汇基线的影响，语境框架信息在模型内部依然具有高度可预测性；4. 实验证明，通过干预模型内部相关的表征方向，可以部分调节或改变模型的最终输出行为。

Conclusion: 上下文语境对大语言模型的行为和内部表征具有系统性影响。模型对提示词的表述方式（语境框架）非常敏感，这构成了AI在心理健康等敏感领域应用时的可靠性挑战。研究表明，需要开发更稳健的对齐方法来缓解这种不一致性，以提升人机交互的信任度。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly being integrated into mental health support tools and other psychologically sensitive conversational applications. In such settings, behavioral stability and consistency are important for trustworthy human-AI interaction. However, semantically similar concerns can be presented through different contextual framings, potentially eliciting different model responses. Such framing-sensitive variability may challenge user expectations regarding system behavior and complicate the assessment of AI reliability. While prior studies have primarily examined such effects at the behavioral level, less is known about how framing-related variation is reflected in the internal representations of aligned language models. In this work, we investigate these effects using controlled matched prompts spanning multiple contextual framing conditions across several instruction-tuned model families. Across architectures, framing systematically alters interpretive response tendencies. Layer-wise probing analyses show that behavior-associated information remains decodable throughout transformer depth, with architecture-dependent variation in decoding strength. Moreover, held-out framing probes remained consistently above chance across architectures despite strong lexical baselines. Activation steering experiments further suggest that framing-associated representational directions can partially modulate downstream behavioral outcomes. Finally, these findings indicate that robustness to contextual variation may represent an important consideration when evaluating the consistency and trustworthiness of conversational AI systems deployed in mental-health-oriented interactions.

### [49] [ReaORE: Reasoning-Guided Progressive Open Relation Extraction Empowered by Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26986)
*Xin Lin,Liang Zhang,Guoqi Ma,Hongyao Tu,Jinsong Su*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对开放关系抽取中难以处理未见关系且对易混淆关系判别力不足的问题，本文提出了 ReaORE 框架，通过从粗到细的推理策略（过滤与细粒度对比预测）显著提升了关系抽取的准确性和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放关系抽取（OpenRE）方法存在两类主要缺陷：一是基于聚类的方法无法生成语义化的关系标签且泛化性较差；二是基于大语言模型（LLM）直接生成标签的方法往往缺乏足够的判别力，难以区分语义相近或易混淆的关系。

Method: 提出了一种名为“推理引导的渐进式开放关系抽取”（ReaORE）框架，包含两个阶段：首先是“关系过滤”阶段，通过多维推理理解实例并结合基于嵌入的相似度计算生成初始关系集合；其次是“关系预测”阶段，通过细粒度的对比推理，从初始集合中准确识别出目标关系，从而提高对易混淆关系的判别能力。

Result: 在两个广泛使用的 OpenRE 数据集上的实验结果表明，ReaORE 在性能上优于现有的基准模型。

Conclusion: ReaORE 通过引入从粗到细的推理机制，有效地克服了传统聚类方法泛化能力弱以及现有大模型直接生成标签时区分度不足的问题，为开放关系抽取提供了一个更精准、稳健的框架。

Abstract: Open Relation Extraction (OpenRE) requires a model to extract unseen relations between head and tail entities from unstructured text for real-world applications. The core challenge of OpenRE lies in achieving reliable generalization to unseen relation types. Current OpenRE approaches either employ clustering techniques, which cannot generate relation labels and suffer from poor generalization, or rely on direct relation label generation via Large Language Models (LLMs), which lack sufficient discriminative capacity to distinguish easily confused relations. To address these limitations, we propose Reasoning-guided progressive OpenRE (ReaORE), a framework for performing relation extraction through coarse-to-fine relation reasoning. Specifically, ReaORE consists of two key stages: (i) relation filtering, which reasons over multiple aspects to understand relations and instances, yielding an initial relation set, and further supplements and filters relations via embedding-based similarity to ensure the target relation is included; (ii) relation prediction, which aims to predict the target relations from the above set via fine-grained comparative reasoning to better distinguish easily confused relations. Extensive experiments on two widely used OpenRE datasets demonstrate that ReaORE outperforms existing baselines.

### [50] [Where Do Models Find Happiness? Emotion Vectors in Open-Source LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26987)
*Sinie van der Ben,Raphaël Baur,Yannick Metz,Mennatallah El-Assady*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究验证了大型语言模型中存在通用的情感向量，发现不同模型（Gemma与Apertus）在情感表征的深度演化模式上表现出显著差异，且情感表征的稳定性受生成数据特征的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了验证此前在Claude Sonnet 4.5中发现的“情感向量”（即影响行为且镜像人类心理结构的情感内部表征）是否具有模型架构上的通用性，并探索不同模型在情感编码方式上的差异。

Method: 研究选取了Apertus-8B-Instruct-2509和Gemma-4-E4B-it两个开源模型，使用模型生成的两个语料库，在各层提取情感对比向量，通过计算主成分（PC）与人类情感维度（效价和唤醒度）的相关性，分析情感几何结构的分布特征。

Result: 研究成功在两个模型中复现了效价（valence）的几何结构，PC1与效价的相关性分别达到0.76和0.83，与原研究结果接近。此外，发现不同模型中效价的编码深度模式存在显著差异，且唤醒度（arousal）的编码受到生成语料库内容分布的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了情感向量在不同开源模型中具有普遍性，证明了大型语言模型内部确实存在与人类心理结构相对应的几何表征。同时，研究揭示了情感表征的形成受模型架构深度及数据分布的影响，为深入理解大模型的内部机制提供了实证基础。

Abstract: Recent work identified emotion vectors in Claude Sonnet 4.5, which are internal representations that encode emotion concepts, causally influence behavior, and exhibit geometry mirroring human psychological structure. We test the generality of these findings in two open-weight models, Apertus-8B-Instruct-2509 and Gemma-4-E4B-it, extracting emotion contrast vectors across all layers, using two model-generated corpora. We recover valence geometry for both models, with peak PC1--valence correlations of $r = 0.76$ and $r = 0.83$, approaching the $r = 0.81$ reported for Claude.Beyond replication, we observe notable differences in how valence representations emerge across model depth. In Gemma-4-E4B-it, valence is strongly encoded in early layers but collapses towards later layers, whereas Apertus-8B-Instruct-2509 exhibits the opposite pattern, with valence representations absent in early layers, but emerging at mid depths. Arousal encoding, in contrast, is sensitive to the extraction corpus: both models show stronger PC2--arousal alignment with Gemma-generated stories ($r$ up to $0.45$) than Apertus-generated ones ($r \leq 0.21$), suggesting arousal-relevant cues are unevenly distributed across generated corpora. We open-source our experiment code and dataset for reproducible investigation of emotion representations across language model architectures.

### [51] [MinGram: A Minimalist Unigram Tokenizer with High Compression and Competitive Morphological Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27019)
*Sander Land*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MinGram 是一种极简的 Unigram 分词器，通过简化训练流程（摒弃复杂的迭代和数据结构），在保持高性能压缩与优良形态学对齐的同时，显著降低了训练的计算复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Unigram 分词器虽然词表编辑灵活，但其训练过程计算繁重且复杂（如需要后缀数组和多次迭代剪枝），作者旨在设计一种训练过程更简单且高效的替代方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MinGram 的极简 Unigram 分词器，其方法包括：1. 使用 BPE 派生的种子词表；2. 采用基于最小 token 路径的 Hard EM 算法；3. 执行单次扁平化分数剪枝。该方法移除了后缀数组、前向-后向传递及迭代剪枝循环，将 token 计数作为主要优化目标，仅将 Unigram 分数作为平局决胜因素。

Result: 在六种语言的测试中，MinGram 的压缩效果优于 BPE 和标准 Unigram；在语言模型下游任务中，MinGram 表现出更好的每字节比特数（bits-per-byte）性能，同时保持了良好的形态学对齐能力。

Conclusion: MinGram 证明了通过简化训练流程，可以在保持 Unigram 分词器优良特性的同时，显著降低计算复杂度，并在压缩效率和下游语言模型性能上超越传统的 BPE 和标准 Unigram 方法。

Abstract: The Unigram tokenizer uses an elegant representation which makes it straightforward to edit vocabularies, but its training is comparatively heavy and complex. We introduce MinGram (Minimalist Unigram), which keeps the token-list representation but simplifies training using a BPE-derived seed vocabulary, Hard EM on a minimum-token path, and a single flat score-pruning step. This removes the suffix array, the forward-backward pass, and the iterative prune loop, leaving a procedure that requires little beyond tokenizer inference itself. By making token count the primary objective and using a Unigram score only as a tiebreak, MinGram keeps the compression of pure token-count methods while retaining much of the morphological alignment and downstream quality of probabilistic ones. Across six languages, MinGram compresses better than both BPE and standard Unigram, and a compression-oriented variant matches the strongest token-count compressors while retaining substantially higher morphological alignment. In controlled downstream language-model training, Unigram-family tokenizers, with MinGram among the best, consistently beat BPE in bits-per-byte.

</details>


### [52] [Improving General Role-Playing Agents via Psychology-Grounded Reasoning and Role-Aware Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27025)
*Zhenhua Xu,Dongsheng Chen,Jian Li,Yitong Lin,Zhebo Wang,Jiafu Wu,Yizhang Jin,Chengjie Wang,Meng Han,Yabiao Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文针对大模型角色扮演中缺乏深层推理与角色保真度下降的问题，提出了Psy-CoT思维链框架以增强模型内在逻辑，并开发了RAPO算法以修正强化学习中的梯度偏差，显著提升了角色扮演的准确性与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流的监督微调（SFT）方法仅停留在表面行为模仿，缺乏人类式的内在思维过程，导致模型在处理分布外（OOD）数据时泛化能力较差，且现有的强化学习训练中存在奖励模型被“破解”的问题。

Method: 1. 提出Psy-CoT框架：将角色扮演的推理过程拆解为“交互感知”、“心理共情”和“逻辑构建”三个心理学导向的思维链步骤，使模型具备动态思考能力。2. 提出RAPO（角色感知策略优化）：引入角色画像与词汇间的互信息（Mutual Information），实现非对称的梯度加权，增强角色特有词汇在正向激励中的权重，并抑制负向反馈中的干扰，解决奖励模型被过度利用的问题。

Result: 在CoSER、CharacterBench和CharacterEval等基准测试上，Psy-CoT在角色扮演保真度方面优于现有的思维链方法；RAPO策略在多个模型规模下均表现出比GRPO更优的性能。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的Psy-CoT思维链框架与RAPO策略优化方法，能够有效解决角色扮演代理在行为模仿、跨分布泛化以及奖励模型破解等方面的问题，为构建具备深层心理建模能力和高保真度的角色扮演智能体提供了有效路径。

Abstract: Building general-purpose role-playing agents that faithfully portray any character from a natural-language profile remains challenging. The dominant paradigm -- supervised fine-tuning -- encourages behavioral mimicry without deep, human-like internal thought processes, resulting in poor out-of-distribution generalization. Therefore, we propose \textbf{Psy-CoT}, a psychology-grounded chain-of-thought framework that decomposes pre-response reasoning into three role-specific steps -- \emph{Interaction Perception}, \emph{Psychological Empathy}, and \emph{Logical Construction} -- so that the model \emph{thinks dynamically} from the profile rather than merely mimicking surface patterns. While structured reasoning provides a foundation, it alone is insufficient; reinforcement learning is essential to further align the model with character fidelity. However, we observe that under LLM-based reward models, both generic phrases that hack the reward model and genuinely role-specific phrases receive identical gradient signals -- this hacking accumulates over training, misleading the model into treating both as equally optimal choices. To address this, we propose \textbf{Role-Aware Policy Optimization (RAPO)}, which uses profile--token mutual information to weight gradients asymmetrically -- amplifying role-specific tokens under positive advantage while attenuating them under negative advantage. Experiments on CoSER, CharacterBench, and CharacterEval demonstrate that Psy-CoT outperforms existing role-playing CoT methods, and RAPO consistently surpasses GRPO across multiple model scales.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了包含约 1240 个问答对的核工程基准测试数据集（NuclearQAv2），涵盖布尔、数值和语言三类问题；采用了专家编写、现有数据集整合以及大模型辅助生成相结合的混合流水线方法，并利用结构化提示词实现自动化生成与评估。

Result: 通过对多个大模型进行评估，发现模型在事实性问题上表现良好，但在定量推理和概念理解方面表现明显不足，且不同模型在各类任务上的性能差异巨大。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance across a wide range of tasks, but ensuring their reliability in highly technical domains remains a significant challenge. In nuclear engineering, problem solving often requires not only factual knowledge but also quantitative reasoning and conceptual understanding. To address the need for systematic evaluation in this domain, we introduce NuclearQAv2, a benchmark for assessing LLMs on nuclear engineering knowledge. The benchmark comprises approximately 1,240 question-answer pairs spanning three categories: boolean, numeric, and verbal. NuclearQAv2 is constructed using a hybrid pipeline that combines expert-authored questions, existing datasets, and LLM-assisted generation from domain-specific technical corpora. By leveraging structured prompting for both automated question generation and response evaluation, the proposed framework enables scalable benchmark construction and evaluation. We evaluate a diverse set of LLMs using NuclearQAv2 and observe substantial performance differences across task types. While the models generally perform well on factual questions, quantitative reasoning and conceptual understanding remain considerably more challenging. These results highlight the importance of multi-faceted evaluation frameworks and establish NuclearQAv2 as a scalable benchmark for assessing LLM capabilities in technical domains.

### [54] [Towards Explainable Adjudicative Variance: Quantifying Judicial Discretion via Gated Multi-Task Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27069)
*Stanisław Sójka,Felix Steffek,Matthias Grabmair*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的法官感知门控多任务架构，通过解耦事实与司法上下文，在法律裁决预测任务中以极低的参数成本超越了大规模生成式模型的基准，验证了结构化模型组合优于单纯的提示词工程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的法律结果预测模型难以有效区分客观案件事实与主观司法背景，且直接将法官身份与案件信息混杂在单一生成式路径中会导致信息合成效果不佳。需要一种机制来明确区分事实证据与司法裁量因素，并提高对稀有/歧义结果的预测能力。

Method: 提出了一种“法官感知门控多任务学习架构”（Judge-Aware Gated Multi-Task Learning）。该方法引入细粒度结果分类体系来监督编码器，利用结构化正则化实现语义路径解耦，并采用门控融合（Gated Fusion）机制动态调节对法官身份信息的依赖。结合LoRA适配的Gemma-4编码器，实现了对上下文信号的解耦建模。

Result: 在13,937份英国就业法庭裁决数据集上，该模型优于基于Gemma-4 26B的监督微调（SFT）基准模型。在参数量减少一个数量级的情况下，显著提升了准确性，特别是在最模糊和罕见的结果类别上表现更佳，且模型具备良好的可解释性，能有效定位法官背景驱动决策的案例。

Conclusion: 在法律结果预测任务中，针对身份条件分类，选择合适的条件接口比单纯增加模型规模更为关键。相比于提示词（prompt-based）合成，微分结构化合成（differentiable structured composition）能以更少的参数实现更高的准确性和解释性。

Abstract: Legal outcome prediction must disentangle objective case facts from adjudicative context. Merit-based rulings rely on factual evidence while technical disposals may hinge on judicial discretion. We propose a Judge-Aware Gated Multi-Task Learning architecture that explicitly models this distinction. We introduce a fine-grained outcome taxonomy to supervise the encoder, enforcing a structural regularization that disentangles distinct semantic pathways. This granular legal curriculum enables our Gated Fusion mechanism to dynamically modulate reliance on judge identity. We evaluate our approach on 13,937 UK Employment Tribunal decisions. We benchmark our design against supervised fine-tuning (SFT) of a Gemma-4 26B-A4B backbone, in which judge identity and the taxonomy are injected as prompt tokens or autoregressive output targets. The two contextual signals compose only weakly when forced through a single autoregressive channel. In contrast, coupling a LoRA-adapted Gemma-4 encoder with our gated architecture defines a new state of the art on this benchmark while requiring an order of magnitude fewer trainable parameters than the generative SFT baselines, with gains concentrated on the most ambiguous and rarest outcome classes. Beyond accuracy, the architecture is interpretable; learned judge embeddings and calibration profiles localize the cases where adjudicative context drives the prediction. These results indicate that, for identity-conditioned classification of legal outcomes, the choice of conditioning interface dominates scale: differentiable structured composition yields more accurate, more parameter-efficient models than prompt-based composition over a substantially larger backbone.

</details>


### [55] [The Riddle Riddle: Testing Flexible Reasoning in Large Language Models and Humans](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27103)
*Bella Fascendini,Kathryn McGregor,Max D. Gupta,Thomas L. Griffiths*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过“谜语-谜语”实验揭示，大语言模型在解决问题时倾向于依赖表面形式进行模式匹配，而非根据内容灵活调整推理策略，其实际推理能力远逊于人类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨大语言模型在认知任务中表现出的高准确率，究竟是源于真正的灵活推理能力，还是仅仅是对训练数据中既有模式的匹配与复现。

Method: 研究者设计了“谜语-谜语”（riddle riddle）范式，即包含谜语形式但答案仅需字面理解的问题。通过对比九种大语言模型与100名人类参与者在真实谜语与“谜语-谜语”上的表现及错误类型，分析模型是否存在灵活的策略转换。

Result: 实验发现，模型在真实谜语上的准确率远高于“谜语-谜语”（84.9% vs 50.7%），且超过90%的错误源于在字面问题中错误地应用了创造性推理；而人类表现则相反，在“谜语-谜语”上表现更好。这表明模型难以摆脱表面结构的影响。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在处理类似谜语的题目时表现出的准确性，很大程度上归因于对训练数据的模式匹配和记忆检索，而非真正的灵活推理能力。模型往往被问题的形式（表面特征）所误导，无法像人类那样根据内容需求灵活切换推理策略。

Abstract: Humans flexibly adapt their reasoning strategies to the requirements of a given problem. Large language models (LLMs) have performed well on many cognitive tasks, however, it is unclear whether this accuracy is a result of pattern matching from training data or flexible reasoning. Here, we introduce a novel paradigm to test this question: the riddle riddle paradigm. Riddle riddles are word problems written to mimic popular riddles, but altered so their answers only require literal interpretations. Identifying correct answers requires looking past the structure of each question and flexibly apply different reasoning strategies based on the content. If LLMs respond to surface features, such as form, a riddle-like structure should cause models to use an inventive reasoning strategy even when a literal interpretation suffices. Alternatively, if LLMs reason based on content, they should flexibly switch strategies when appropriate. Across two experiments with nine state-of-the-art LLMs and 100 human participants, we show humans and LLMs fail on this paradigm in opposite directions. LLMs were far more accurate on genuine riddles than on riddle riddles (84.9% vs. 50.7%); whereas humans showed the reverse effect (50.5% vs. 80.5%). Error analysis shows that 90.8% of LLM errors on riddle riddles (the condition where they show diminished performance) were due to inappropriate use of inventive reasoning while only 57.6% of human errors on genuine riddles were due to overextending literal reasoning. Thus, while both groups make mistakes, reasoning mistakes are made more often by LLMs than by humans. Overall, LLMs' strong performance on genuine riddles may reflect memory retrieval rather than flexible strategy selection, and without stimuli designed to elicit this contrast, it becomes easy to conflate LLM-generated outputs that look like reasoning with genuine reasoning.

</details>


### [56] [Forecasting With LLMs: Improved Generalization Through Feature Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27199)
*Humzah Merchant,Bradford Levy*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究利用稀疏自编码器分析大语言模型的内部机制，发现通过干预模型中的时间感知特征，可以有效地校正模型在预测任务中的前瞻偏差，使推理过程更具客观的时间逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在预测任务中虽然表现出一定能力，但常伴有“前瞻偏差”（即利用了模型训练截止日期后的未来信息）。研究旨在探究模型是依赖于特定的时间知识，还是依赖于可泛化的模式，并寻求一种方法来减轻这种偏差，使其推理过程更具历史扎根性。

Method: 1. 利用稀疏自编码器（Sparse Autoencoders）提取并解构大语言模型的内部状态；2. 定位与时间感知推理和前瞻偏差（look-ahead bias）相关的特征；3. 在不同领域应用模型，通过干预（增强或抑制）上述特征来测试其因果效应。

Result: 研究发现，通过放大模型中的时间感知特征，可以显著降低预测任务中的前瞻偏差；而对所谓的“前瞻偏差特征”进行干预则效果不明显。这证明了模型内部确实存在能够调节推理时间逻辑的可解释特征。

Conclusion: 研究表明，大语言模型中存在可解释的时间相关特征。通过稀疏自编码器识别并干预这些特征，可以在不损失通用推理能力的前提下，有效抑制大模型在预测任务中的“前瞻偏差”，从而引导模型进行更符合历史逻辑的推理。

Abstract: Successful forecasting involves identifying patterns between historical and future states of the world which generalize to future observations. We apply LLMs to a variety of forecasting tasks and inspect their internal states using sparse autoencoders to understand whether they appear to rely on time-specific pieces of knowledge versus generalizable patterns. Our analyses identify features associated with both time-aware reasoning and look-ahead-biased reasoning. We then apply the LLMs to an entirely different domain and intervene on these features. We find that amplifying time-awareness features substantially reduces look-ahead bias on forecasting prompts while preserving general reasoning performance. In contrast, steering the candidate look-ahead-bias features does not produce an effect. These results suggest that interpretable temporal features can be used to causally shift LLMs toward more historically grounded reasoning.

### [57] [Syntactic Belief Update as the Driver of Garden Path Processing Difficulty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27206)
*Alan Zhou,Miloš Stanojević,John T. Hale*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对传统词汇惊奇度模型无法解释“花园路径”句子的局限，本文提出了一种基于句法信念更新的衡量指标，该指标独立于词汇概率，能更精准地预测人类在处理此类复杂歧义句时的认知难度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的词汇惊奇度（Lexical Surprisal）模型虽在大多数情况下预测效果良好，但在解释人类处理“花园路径”句子（即因初期歧义导致理解错误并在后续词汇出现时需要修正的句子）时的处理难度时失效，因此需要一种新的替代方案来解释这种心理认知过程。

Method: 提出一种基于句法信念（Syntactic Belief）的概率模型，通过每接收一个新词后更新句法树的概率分布，并利用广义Rényi散度来衡量更新的幅度。该方法在评估处理难度时，完全独立于词汇项本身的出现概率。

Result: 实验结果表明，该模型对人类阅读“花园路径”句子的实际时间数据提供了更好的拟合度，证明了句法层面的信念更新比单纯的词汇预测更能准确反映人类处理复杂句式时的认知负荷。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入句法信念更新（Syntactic Belief Update）机制，证明了在解释“花园路径”句子的处理难度时，仅依赖词汇概率的惊奇度模型（Lexical Surprisal）存在局限。该成果为心理语言学提供了一种独立于词汇概率的纯句法解释维度，为未来研究人类句子处理机制开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Garden path sentences present a processing difficulty for humans -- the sentence prefix leads the listener towards one interpretation, until the listener hears a critical word that shows that the initial interpretation was wrong. Lexical surprisal, a measure that usually predicts sentence processing difficulty quite well, fails to provide good predictions for garden path sentences.
  We propose an alternative that actively predicts a probability distribution over syntactic trees (its syntactic belief) and updates that distribution after each new word. If a processor is led down a garden path, syntactic beliefs will be wrong and will require a large update at the critical word. The magnitude of the update is measured with a generalized Rényi divergence. Crucially, this metric is dependent on lexical items, but is fully independent of the probability of lexical items. This Syntactic Belief Update provides a better fit to the human reading time data on garden path sentences. This suggests a new research direction examining purely non-lexical alternatives to surprisal for psycholinguistics.

</details>


### [58] [Paved with True Intents: Intent-Aware Training Improves LLM Safety Classification Across Training Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27210)
*Jeremias Ferrao,Niclas Müller-Hof,Iustin Sîrbu,Traian Rebedea,Yftah Ziser*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的安全分类器往往难以准确捕捉复杂的用户意图，导致误判或漏判。作者提出，应将用户意图显式地建模为介于输入提示词和最终安全标签之间的信号，以提高分类器对隐晦或复杂恶意请求的鲁棒性。

Method: 1. 构建数据集：创建了包含1,724个复杂安全提示词的人工标注数据集AIMS，每条数据包含意图描述和有害性标签。2. 训练策略：在监督微调（SFT）、偏好学习（DPO）、推理蒸馏和强化学习（GRPO）等框架下评估了意图感知训练的效果。3. 核心机制：通过直接奖励意图忠实度以及对比意图条件蒸馏与常规推理蒸馏的效果，验证了显式建模用户意图的有效性。

Result: 1. 即使AIMS数据集规模较小，也能显著提升各类训练范式下的安全分类性能。2. 使用GRPO直接奖励意图忠实度的方法在五个外部安全基准测试中表现最佳。3. 意图感知模型在推理延迟与F1值（性能）的帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier）上具有竞争优势。

Conclusion: 研究表明，将用户意图显式建模为安全分类器中的一个信号，是一种高效且高质量的监督手段。通过意图感知训练，模型不仅能显著提升安全性，还能在推理延迟与分类准确性之间取得更好的平衡，为开发鲁棒性更强的安全分类器提供了新的路径。

Abstract: We argue that safety classifiers should model user intent as an explicit signal between the prompt and the final label. To study this, we introduce AIMS, a human-annotated dataset of 1,724 difficult safety prompts, each paired with an intent description and harm label. We use AIMS to evaluate intent-aware training across supervised fine-tuning, preference learning, reasoning distillation, and reinforcement learning. Despite its size, AIMS enables competitive safety classifiers across training regimes: DPO from model-generated intent errors improves over SFT, and intent-conditioned distillation outperforms reasoning-only distillation in most teacher-student pairs. Most notably, directly rewarding intent faithfulness with GRPO yields the strongest average performance across five external safety benchmarks, while our intent-aware models form the inference latency-F1 Pareto frontier. These results show that faithful intent modeling is a compact, high-quality supervision signal for more robust safety classifiers.

### [59] [Compositionality and the lexicon in evolutionary semantics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27228)
*Fausto Carcassi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合形式语义学与演化建模的新框架，成功揭示了量词“保守性”这一语言共性是如何通过概念简洁性与交流准确性的共同演化而形成的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语义演化模型通常假设词汇信号结构固定，或采用无法解释词汇部分的整体合成模式，缺乏对形式语义学中“通过递归合成词汇意义来构建句子意义”这一核心洞见的整合。本文旨在弥合形式语义学与演化建模之间的鸿沟，探索语义共性（特别是量词的保守性）的演化起源。

Method: 作者构建了一个联合演化框架，在该框架中，词汇意义和合成函数（composition function）在概念简洁性和交流准确性的双重选择压力下共同演化。作者通过分析帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier），考察了该框架在量词意义演化中的表现，并将结果与现有的语言学实证证据进行了对比。

Result: 研究发现，语言中最著名的语义共性——保守性（conservativity），作为一种系统层面的高效抽象在演化过程中自然涌现。该模型不仅能够解释量词的习得规律，还成功调和了实证数据与先前演化模型之间的矛盾，展示了语法结构在优化语义系统中的关键作用。

Conclusion: 本文证明了形式语义学中的句子意义合成理论可以与演化建模有效结合。研究表明，诸如保守性（conservativity）之类的语义共性并非偶然，而是系统在追求概念简洁性和交流准确性压力下的最优解（帕累托最优），为研究语义共性的起源提供了一个通用框架。

Abstract: Formal semantics has shown that sentence meanings arise by recursively composing lexical meanings, yet much of the literature on semantic universals models either lexicons with fixed signal structures or holistic composition without interpretable lexical parts. We introduce a framework that integrates this fundamental insight of formal semantics in evolutionary modeling, by allowing lexical meanings and a composition function to co-evolve under pressures for conceptual simplicity and communicative accuracy. We apply this framework to the evolution of quantificational meaning. Analyzing the Pareto frontier, we find that the most well-known semantic universal, conservativity, emerges as an efficient system-wide abstraction. The account is sensitive to syntactic structure and helps reconcile tensions between empirical evidence on quantifier learnability and prior evolutionary models. More broadly, the results demonstrate that the picture of sentential meaning developed in formal semantics can be productively combined with evolutionary modeling. The framework offers a template for studying universals that involve global compression within a grammatical category, semantic specialization of syntactic arguments, and the co-evolution of lexical and compositional meaning.

### [60] [CARVE: Content-Aware Recurrent with Value Efficiency for Chunk-Parallel Linear Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27229)
*Sayak Dutta*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 CARVE 模型，通过实现“内容感知”的记忆遗忘机制，解决了循环神经网络在训练效率和记忆控制上的核心痛点，在显著降低计算资源消耗的同时，提升了模型在各类基准测试中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的循环模型（如 GDN-2）存在“记忆盲目门控”问题，即门控机制在决定擦除什么信息时无法感知当前的记忆状态，导致参数浪费且无法应用高效的并行训练方法（WY-form 求解器）。

Method: 提出 CARVE 架构，主要改进包括：1. 将遗忘操作限制在键轴，确保其兼容高效的 WY-form 分块求解器；2. 利用已写入显存的循环输出张量作为擦除门的“内容信号”（内容感知）；3. 将每个值的写门投影简化为每个头部的单一标量（值效率）。

Result: 在 1.3B 参数规模下，CARVE 在 WikiText 困惑度上优于 GDN-2，并在常识推理和 RULER 检索任务上达到 SOTA 水平。此外，相比基线模型，CARVE 降低了 13% 的峰值内存占用，减少了 19% 的参数量，且仅有 0.4% 的吞吐量开销。

Conclusion: CARVE 通过引入“仅在键轴（key-axis）执行擦除”的原则，成功解决了现有循环模型在记忆遗忘机制上的缺陷，证明了通过内容感知门控可以实现更高效的循环训练，且在保持与原模型架构相似性的同时，显著提升了推理性能与任务表现。

Abstract: Recurrent models must forget in order to remember, yet the state of the art decides what to erase without consulting what is stored -- the gate sees only the arriving token, not the memory it is about to modify. This memory-blind gating is one of three coupled defects in the leading delta-rule architecture (GDN-2): the value-axis erase mask wastes parameters at the scale of the value projection, and -- as we prove -- mathematically prevents the WY-form triangular chunk solver that makes recurrent training competitive with Transformers.
  We introduce CARVE (Content-Aware Recurrent with Value Efficiency), which resolves all three problems through one principle: erase only on the key axis. This is provably necessary and sufficient for the WY-form solver to remain valid. Within it, CARVE reuses the recurrent output tensor -- already written to GPU memory -- as a free content signal for the erase gate, and replaces the per-value write-gate projection with a single scalar per head. At initialisation CARVE is bit-identical to GDN-2; any quality difference emerges from what the content gate learns.
  At 1.3B parameters trained on 100B tokens, CARVE achieves WikiText perplexity 15.72 (minus 0.18 vs. GDN-2, a 4.5-sigma effect), leads every recurrent baseline on nine common-sense reasoning benchmarks, and sets state of the art on every RULER retrieval probe -- at 0.4% throughput overhead, 13% lower peak memory, and 19% fewer parameters. Six formal theorems cover memory capacity, Lyapunov stability, gradient flow, expressivity separation, Pareto-optimal chunk size, and hybrid optimality.

</details>

Abstract: We present a conceptual framework for analyzing dialogue in collaborative problem-solving contexts, with an emphasis on the emerging dynamics of human-AI and multi-agent collaboration. As intelligent systems become active agents capable of autonomous reasoning and strategic cooperation, understanding the dialogic interaction during collaborative problem solving is increasingly important for optimizing and evaluating such partnerships. Our framework addresses key limitations in current analytical approaches through a hierarchical two-layer coding scheme that integrates cognitive and non-cognitive problem solving with metacognitive regulatory mechanisms. We demonstrate its effectiveness and generalizability across nine datasets spanning multiple domains, and provide insights into how humans and agents coordinate their knowledge, skills, and efforts to solve complex problems, showing in particular that metacognitive regulation can be an essential discriminator of deeper collaboration.

### [62] [LMs as Task-Specific Knowledge Bases: An Interpretability Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27237)
*Amit Elhelo,Amir Globerson,Mor Geva*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究表明，语言模型并非统一的“知识库”，其存储的事实知识与特定任务高度耦合，导致模型在处理同一事实时缺乏一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的观点将语言模型视为知识库，但知识库应具备事实的一致性（同一事实在不同查询下应返回相同结果）。本文旨在验证语言模型是否满足这一属性，并探究模型参数究竟是如何组织和存储事实知识的。

Method: 本文通过行为分析和机制分析方法进行研究。行为分析考察不同任务间事实获取的一致性；机制分析则利用参数定位技术（parameter localization）探究特定事实在不同任务中对应的参数子集；此外，还分析了思维链（CoT）推理如何通过调用跨任务参数来提升性能。

Result: 研究发现：1. 事实在不同任务间的获取往往不具备同步性；2. 同一事实在不同任务下由不同的参数子集负责；3. 思维链推理的有效性部分归功于它能够激活超出评估任务之外的特定任务参数。

Conclusion: 语言模型并不像传统的知识库那样存储统一的“事实”，而是将知识与特定任务紧密交织在一起。这种参数空间的耦合性削弱了“语言模型即知识库”的类比，并对大模型的可靠性和可控性提出了挑战。

Abstract: Language models (LMs) capture large amounts of factual knowledge applicable to a wide range of tasks, motivating the view of their parameters as a knowledge base. An important property of knowledge bases is that different queries for the same fact return consistent results, drawing on a single source of truth. We investigate whether LMs satisfy this property through behavioral and mechanistic analyses. Our results suggest that they encode knowledge in a task-specific manner. Behaviorally, facts acquired on one task frequently fail to co-emerge on others during training. Parameter localization experiments suggest a mechanistic explanation, revealing distinct parameter subsets underlying different tasks for the same fact. Finally, we show that chain-of-thought reasoning draws part of its effectiveness from engaging task-specific parameters beyond those tied to the evaluation task. Our findings suggest that what the model knows and how it is asked are intertwined in parameter space, undermining the "knowledge base" analogy and carrying implications for the reliability and controllability of factual knowledge in LMs.

</details>


### [63] [How Surprising Is Historical Italian to Language Models? Tokenization Tax, Comprehension Tax, and a Simple Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27275)
*Maria Levchenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个诊断框架来评估大语言模型处理历史文本的能力，发现虽然历史文本增加了模型的编码压力，但并未破坏模型的语义表示能力，通过简单的提示词优化即可提升处理性能，验证了LLM在数字图书馆业务中的可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决大语言模型处理历史文本时，由于正字法差异、语言演变和预训练数据覆盖度不同而导致的处理难度不明确的问题。

Method: 构建了一个包含四个维度的诊断框架（分词成本、预测不确定性/惊奇度、语义鲁棒性和上下文敏感度），并对比评估了三个不同语种与时代的文本集（17世纪意大利语、19世纪意大利语、18世纪俄语）。

Result: 研究发现：1. 历史文本会导致显著的分词成本增加（25-30%）；2. 不同语种的历史文本预测难度差异巨大；3. 尽管预测不确定性提高，但模型的向量嵌入表示依然稳健（相似度>0.85）；4. 简单的提示词工程可将历史文本的惊奇度（surprisal）降低约60%。

Conclusion: 历史文本的处理存在“编码损耗”与“语义理解”的分离。虽然历史文本增加了模型处理的负荷，但大语言模型在语义检索任务中依然表现稳健，且通过简单的上下文提示（prompt）即可显著降低生成时的不确定性，证明了其在数字图书馆场景下的应用潜力。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly critical to digital library workflows, yet their ability to process historical language remains poorly understood. Historical difficulty is typically treated as a monolithic barrier, conflating orthographic variation, linguistic distance, and pretraining exposure. In this paper, we propose a diagnostic framework that decomposes this difficulty into four distinct dimensions: tokenization cost, predictive uncertainty (surprisal), semantic robustness, and context sensitivity.
  We evaluate this framework on three datasets spanning three centuries: (1) a newly curated corpus of 17th-century Italian texts (1610-1689) digitized from original page images; (2) canonical 19th-century Italian "I Promessi Sposi" serving as a high-exposure control; and (3) 18th-century Russian civil print books as a contrastive orthographic stress test.
  Our results reveal a distinct dissociation between encoding cost and comprehension. While Russian and early modern Italian incur comparable tokenization penalties (25-30% inflation), their predictive difficulty diverges sharply. 17th-century Italian is on average 2.4 times more surprising than its modern equivalent - with academic prose reaching 3.2 times - whereas Russian shows only a modest increase. But predictive uncertainty does not imply representational degradation: embedding similarity remains robust (> 0.85) across all datasets, confirming that models can represent historical meaning even when generation is unstable.
  Finally, we demonstrate that a minimal temporal context prompt reduces historical surprisal by approximately 60%, offering a simple, model-agnostic mitigation. These findings suggest that while historical text imposes a consistent encoding tax, digital libraries can safely deploy LLMs for semantic retrieval tasks, provided that generative applications are carefully adapted.

</details>


### [64] [Multilingual Reasoning Cascades Need More Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27306)
*Arnav Mazumder,Dengjia Zhang,Shuyue Stella Li,Yulia Tsvetkov,Niyati Bafna*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对多语言推理中翻译级联导致的信息丢失问题，本研究提出了一种无需训练的干预方法：在生成最终答案时将原始问题作为上下文一并输入，显著提高了多语言任务的推理效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的“翻译-推理-再翻译”级联方法虽然在多语言推理中很常用，但存在严重的结构性信息丢失问题，导致系统无法获得文化背景、语义基准和消歧等关键信息，从而影响最终结果。

Method: 提出了一种上下文感知翻译级联（context-aware translation cascade）方法。该方法在执行推理后翻译答案的步骤中，将原始问题、英文翻译后的问题以及推理过程路径共同作为上下文输入到最终的翻译模型中。

Result: 通过对九个多语言基准测试、三种基座模型以及285种不同资源水平语言的评估发现，该方法在开放式生成任务中表现出显著的性能提升。实验证明，原始语言的问题包含了大部分对最终翻译最有益的上下文信息。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了在多语言推理级联中优化信息流的重要性，并提出了一种简单且无需训练的默认策略：在整个处理流程中保留原始问题，以有效缓解翻译过程中的信息损失和错误传播。

Abstract: Translation cascades for reasoning translate the query from another language to English, reason in English, and translate the answer back to the original language. This is a competitive approach to multilingual reasoning, but structurally lossy, since each stage discards information later stages may need, including cues for cultural grounding, register, and disambiguation. We examine the benefits of a simple and training-free intervention: a context-aware translation cascade, which additionally provides the original question, the English translated question, and the reasoning trace to the context of the final translation module. We evaluate gains across nine multilingual benchmarks including various task types, three backbone models, and 285 high-, mid-, and low-resource languages, and demonstrate strong gains for open-ended generation across models and resource regimes. We show that the original language question carries most of the beneficial context. Our study emphasizes the need to better design information flow in machine translation cascades for mitigating error propagation, and provides a simple and actionable default strategy: preserve the original user question until the end of the pipeline.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种以“底层操作机制”为核心的隐晦语言（ILE）分类法，将其与现有的四种分类法及无分类法基准进行对比，通过LLM提示工程在TikTok和Bluesky的2000条标注数据上进行性能评估。

Abstract: To avoid moderation and surveillance on social media, some users routinely invent indirect linguistic expressions (ILE) that camouflage sensitive meanings. We propose a comprehensive, mechanism-oriented taxonomy of ILE that abstracts away from communicative goals and instead categorizes the underlying operations through which meaning is encoded and recovered. We evaluate the taxonomy by incorporating it into LLM prompts and comparing it with four existing taxonomies and a no-taxonomy baseline, using 2,000 manually annotated TikTok and Bluesky posts. The proposed taxonomy attains the strongest document- and span-level performance across the three LLMs, achieving an improvement of 4.7% in accuracy and 5.4% in F1 over the best-performing benchmark. The empirical results reveal the importance of a comprehensive, mechanism-oriented taxonomy as a stable scaffold for detecting emerging coded language and a useful input to content moderation. Abstract: Verifying the eligibility of securities as collateral is a key responsibility of the German Central Bank. ### [67] [Empowering GUI Agents via Autonomous Experience Exploration and Hindsight Experience Utilization for Task Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27330)
*Tianyi Men,Zhuoran Jin,Pengfei Cao,Yubo Chen,Kang Liu,Jun Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型开源多模态大模型（MLLM）在执行网页自动化任务时，常受限于规划能力薄弱及跨网站泛化能力差的问题，亟需提升其在复杂任务中的规划表现。

Method: 1. 提出 PEEU 方法：通过自主探索环境发现经验，并利用事后经验（Hindsight Experience）合成对齐的高层训练数据；2. 提出 TDHAF 框架：从低、中、高三个粒度系统性地分析任务分解及组合泛化能力。

Result: 基于 PEEU 方法训练的 7B 模型在真实场景基准测试中达到 30.6% 的准确率，表现优于参数量更大的 Qwen2.5-VL-32B 模型。分析验证了高层任务训练对提升规划泛化能力的核心作用。

Conclusion: 通过构建“事后高层任务”并有效利用探索经验，可以显著提升小型多模态大模型（MLLM）的规划能力及跨网站泛化性能。研究表明，仅仅掌握低层原子技能不足以提升规划能力，针对高层任务的训练对于实现有效的分布外（OOD）泛化至关重要。

Abstract: Multimodal web agents can assist humans in operating repetitive GUI tasks, where effective task planning is essential for decomposing complex tasks into executable actions. While small open source MLLMs are cost efficient and privacy preserving compared with commercial large models, they suffer from weak planning and limited cross website generalization. To address these limitations, we introduce the planning experience exploration and utilization (PEEU) method, which autonomously explores environments to discover experiences and utilizes hindsight experience to synthesize strictly aligned, high level training data. To quantitatively analyze the generalization behaviors driving this performance, we propose the task decomposition hierarchical analysis framework (TDHAF) to systematically study compositional generalization across three task granularities: low, middle and high levels. Our analysis reveals that mastering low level atomic skills does not guarantee high level planning competence, while high level task training yields stronger OOD generalization. Experiments on real world benchmarks demonstrate PEEU's superior effectiveness: our 7B model achieves 30.6% accuracy, outperforming the much larger Qwen2.5-VL-32B model. These demonstrate constructing hindsight high level tasks and leveraging experiences is crucial for OOD planning abilities of small MLLMs.

### [68] [Mapping Political-Elite Networks in Europe with a Multilingual Joint Entity-Relation Extraction Pipeline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27347)
*Kirill Solovev,Jana Lasser*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种全开源、多语言的自动化流水线，能够从海量新闻文本中提取政治精英间的复杂关系并构建时间知识图谱，为大规模实证计算社会科学研究提供了一种高效且精确的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往对政治精英权力网络的研究高度依赖人工编码，或受限于简单的文本共现分析。现有大语言模型（LLM）方案多依赖私有API、缺乏多语言能力且在实体解析方面扩展性不足，迫切需要一种开源、可扩展且能处理非结构化文本的工具来构建复杂的政治知识图谱。

Method: 研究提出了一种全开源权重的多语言联合实体-关系抽取流水线。核心包括：1. 基于跨度（span-based）的命名实体识别（NER）；2. 三阶段链接级联，将实体映射至语言无关的维基数据标识符（Wikidata ID）；3. 高吞吐量、本体约束的专家混合（MoE）模型，通过引导式解码提取定向且具有符号性质（signed）的关系。

Result: 该流水线在包含3491个关系的黄金标准集上表现优异，文本准确率（严格模式为68.2%，宽松模式为93.7%）。通过奥地利和波兰的案例研究，证明了该方法能够有效重构政治实体生命周期、揭示国家企业间的利益输送网络以及极化政治环境下的冲突结构。

Conclusion: 该研究构建的模块化、多语言知识图谱提取流水线为计算社会科学提供了一种可复制、高性能的分析工具，使大规模分析政治精英的非正式关系网络成为可能，有助于深入理解公共资源的配置逻辑与政治治理结构。

Abstract: Whether political elites organise into rent-seeking coalitions that capture public resources or civic networks that sustain governance is a central question in comparative politics. Yet observing these complex, informal, and adversarial ties at scale has historically required intensive manual coding, while automated text-as-data methods have largely been limited to simple co-occurrence. Recent large language model (LLM) approaches offer a path forward but often rely on proprietary APIs, lack cross-lingual capability, and struggle with scalable entity resolution. We present a modular, fully open-weight pipeline for multilingual joint entity-relation extraction that builds signed, temporal knowledge graphs from massive unstructured news corpora. It combines span-based named-entity recognition (NER) with a three-stage linking cascade mapping mentions to language-independent Wikidata identifiers; a high-throughput, ontology-constrained mixture-of-experts model then uses guided decoding to extract directed, signed relationships grounded in a domain ontology. A full-coverage spot-check against a 3491-relation gold standard shows high textual correctness (68.2% strict to 93.7% lenient). Two large-scale case studies validate the pipeline against the public record. In Austria, it reconstructs a political party's complete lifecycle, dating internal fractures and tracking personnel into successor factions and court convictions. In a Polish corpus, it uncovers the overlapping economic and governance networks of state-enterprise patronage, alongside the structurally balanced, signed conflict network of the polarized Civic Platform (Platforma Obywatelska, PO)--Law and Justice (Prawo i Sprawiedliwość, PiS) duopoly. By bridging raw multilingual text and structured relational data, our framework provides a robust, replicable foundation for cross-national empirical computational social science.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The spatiotemporal evolution of many physical, chemical, and biological systems is described by nonlinear partial differential equations (PDEs). Recently, deep neural network-based surrogate models have gained increasing interest as efficient alternatives to computationally expensive traditional numerical solvers. In this work, we propose an attention-based, physics-guided convolutional neural network as a surrogate model to learn the microstructural evolution of such systems. We train the model to accurately predict the full time-evolution of phase separation in binary mixtures governed by the Cahn-Hilliard equation. We also show that our model accurately captures the growth of domain size and is consistent with the Lifshitz-Slyozov domain-growth law. The prediction results demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework for modeling systems with conserved kinetics and can be extended to other complex dynamical systems.

### [70] [\chisao{}: A GPU-Native Parallel Optimizer for Multimodal Black-Box Functions via Convergence-Anticonvergence Oscillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26164)
*Ira Wolfson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CHISAO 是一款基于 GPU 的原生并行优化算法，通过特有的“震荡寻优”机制，成功解决了黑盒函数多峰搜索中效率低、高维易陷入局部最优的问题，在准确度和速度上均显著优于传统串行基准算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多峰黑盒函数优化方法（如 basin-hopping, CMA-ES 等）多为串行算法，无法有效利用现代 GPU 的大规模并行计算能力，且在高维空间中容易陷入局部最优，难以高效准确地识别所有极值点。

Method: CHISAO 算法的核心在于“收敛-暂停-反转-粘滞-震荡”循环。其机制包括：利用 GPU 并行处理大规模种群；引入不对称结构移动，对已确认的峰值进行“冻结”保留；其余样本通过基于动量的反收敛和随机平滑梯度进行探索；并利用“驱逐猴子（Repulse Monkey）”和“金鸡（Golden Rooster）”两种策略进行自适应重采样以维持多样性。该算法基于有限差分获取梯度，适用于 derivative-free 场景。

Result: 在 Simon Fraser University 基准测试集的所有 42 个函数中（维度覆盖 2 到 64），CHISAO 实现了 100% 的峰值覆盖率；在 $d \ge 8$ 的高维复杂函数中，传统 CPU 基准算法性能失效，而 CHISAO 仍保持优异表现；对比传统方法，其在特定函数上实现了高达 34 倍至 39 倍的加速；在存在强噪声（$σ_{\mathrm{noise}}$ 高达 1.0）的环境下，其识别准确率仍保持在 100%。

Conclusion: CHISAO 是一种高效、鲁棒且高度并行的黑盒函数多峰寻优算法。通过结合 GPU 并行计算、震荡搜索机制及自适应重采样策略，该算法在处理高维复杂优化问题时，展现出远超传统串行算法的性能和稳定性，为大规模优化任务提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: Finding all modes of a multimodal black-box function is a fundamental challenge in optimization, Bayesian inference, and scientific computing. Existing approaches -- basin-hopping, CMA-ES, multistart gradient descent -- operate sequentially and cannot exploit the massive parallelism of modern GPU hardware. We introduce \chisao{} (\textbf{C}onvergence-\textbf{H}alt-\textbf{I}nvert-\textbf{S}tick-\textbf{A}nd-\textbf{O}scillate), a GPU-native population optimizer that runs an entire sample batch simultaneously and exploits a deliberate convergence-anticonvergence oscillation cycle to escape local traps while freezing confirmed modes. The structural move is asymmetric: samples that reach true peaks are frozen (``stuck'') and preserved, while the rest keep exploring via momentum-based anti-convergence and stochastically smoothed gradients. Adaptive reseeding via two complementary strategies (Repulse Monkey and Golden Rooster) maintains population diversity throughout. On all 42 functions of the Simon Fraser University optimization benchmark suite across dimensions $d \in \{2, 4, 8, 16, 32, 64\}$, \chisao{} achieves \textbf{100\%} mode recovery where all CPU baselines collapse at $d \geq 8$ on the hardest multimodal functions, at up to \textbf{$34\times$} speedup over basin-hopping on functions where all methods succeed (Michalewicz $d=64$) and up to \textbf{$39\times$} on unimodal functions (Rotated Hyper-Ellipsoid $d=64$, pure GPU dividend). All benchmarks evaluate the objective by value alone -- gradients come from finite differences -- so the reported speedups are a derivative-free worst case. Under substantial likelihood noise ($σ_{\mathrm{noise}}$ up to 1.0), mode detection remains 100\% reliable. The algorithm is available as a standalone open-source Python package on PyPI.

</details>


### [71] [Implementation of reinforcement learning in chemical reaction networks: application to phototaxis as curiosity-driven exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26168)
*Ruyi Tang,Grégoire Sergeant-Perthuis,David Colliaux*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过POMDP模型和化学反应动力学，提出衣藻的趋光性是一种基于信息获取的“极小认知”过程，“游动-翻滚”导航策略本质上是细胞在感知模糊环境下为了优化信息获取而进行的主动环境采样。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的单细胞藻类趋光性模型多将其描述为机械性的“游动-翻滚”反应，忽视了生物在噪声和不完整感官输入下主动采样环境以减少感知模糊性的能力，因此需要从“极小认知”的角度重新构建其导航机制。

Method: 1. 构建基于“部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程”（POMDP）的传感器运动模型，将细胞的导航过程建模为信息驱动的决策过程；2. 引入化学反应网络常微分方程（CRN-ODEs）实现该模型；3. 利用逆向强化学习（IRL）分析30条衣藻的实验运动轨迹，推断其行为目标；4. 通过随机模拟算法（SSA）对模型性能进行基准测试与验证。

Result: 研究模型成功复现了实验观测到的衣藻趋光对齐分布；证明了“翻滚”过程作为一种信息获取手段，能够通过改变细胞朝向来解析环境传感器的模糊性；验证了胞内生化网络具备支持细胞尺度自适应信息搜索行为的计算能力。

Conclusion: 本研究通过计算模型证明，单细胞生物的“游动-翻滚”行为不仅仅是简单的机械反应，更是一种主动的信息获取策略。细胞内的生物化学网络能够通过近似贝叶斯推断处理不完整信号，实现对环境的有效导航。这为从“极小认知”角度理解生物系统的自适应行为提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Living systems navigate environments using noisy and incomplete sensory signals. In unicellular algae, phototaxis is often modeled as a mechanistic run--tumble process driven by stimulus--response rules. However, such descriptions overlook how organisms actively sample their environment to reduce sensory ambiguity. From a minimal cognition perspective, we reframe this navigation as a subjective, information-driven sensorimotor process. To this end, we propose a framework linking a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) with biochemical reaction dynamics. Environmental variables are hidden, while the cell updates a minimal internal state from each observation through a memoryless Bayesian step. These internal dynamics balance orienting toward light with exploratory reorientation and can be implemented through Chemical-Reaction-Network Ordinary Differential Equations (CRN--ODEs). Our model includes a biophysical observation process for photoreception and a chemically computable polynomial bound on information gain. Using Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) on 30 experimentally recorded Chlamydomonas trajectories, we infer the behavioral objective consistent with observed phototactic motion and benchmark the resulting dynamics with standard Stochastic Simulation Algorithm (SSA) baselines. Our model reproduces the empirical alignment-to-light distribution, comparable to objective SSA baselines on this dataset. Within this framework, run--tumble alternation emerges as an information-acquisition strategy: tumbling reorients the cell to sample new sensory configurations and resolve sensor ambiguity, demonstrating how intracellular biochemical networks can support adaptive information-seeking behavior in cellular navigation.

### [73] [KG-TRACE: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Mechanistic Grounding in Antimicrobial Resistance Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26179)

Abstract: While WGS-based AMR prediction has reached high accuracy, existing models lack a mechanism to ground neural attributions in established biological pathways. Unlike existing methods that learn statistical patterns in isolation, KG-TRACE fuses genomic features and RotatE-based KG embeddings through a learned epistemic trust gate, dynamically weighting neural evidence against symbolic biological knowledge.

We demonstrate that neuro-symbolic grounding provides a verifiable audit trail for clinicians, bridging the gap between predictive accuracy and clinical trust.

### [74] [Necessary but Not Sufficient: Temperature Control and Reproducibility in LLM-as-Judge Safety Evaluations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26185)
*Hiroki Tamba*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究揭示了“大模型作为裁判”在安全评估中并非完全确定，即使设置温度为0也无法消除噪声；该发现警示开发者不应仅依赖单次运行的评估结论，必须将评估分歧指标纳入安全评估体系中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估框架中广泛使用的“LLM作为裁判”方案存在一个未经验证的假设：即通过设置温度（Temperature）为0可以实现评估的确定性。由于这些评估结果直接决定了模型的安全准入，若存在非确定性，将导致安全性评估失效，因此有必要揭示并量化这一潜在风险。

Method: 作者通过对日本AISI的开源评估代码库（aisev）进行实证测试，跨越了2个API供应商、3个模型层级和5种采样配置，共执行了690次API调用。研究对比了默认温度设置与强制贪婪解码（temperature=0, top_k=1）下的评估一致性，并分析了模型在决策边界附近的表现。

Result: 实验发现：1. 若未显式设置温度，默认的温度值（通常为1.0）导致在相同输入下的通过/失败判定出现剧烈波动，分歧率高达50%。2. 即使强制设置温度为0（贪婪解码），在测试的690次调用中，仍有1-2个处于边界的项目无法实现完全可复现。3. 随着Claude等模型逐步废弃温度参数，传统的缓解措施已失效，验证了评估过程本身存在结构性缺陷。

Conclusion: 研究指出，将大模型作为评估者（LLM-as-judge）存在显著的非确定性风险，即使在温度设置为0的情况下也无法完全避免。目前的评估框架往往忽略了这种变异性，导致评估结果可能只是噪声而非真实的安全性指标。因此，评估框架必须将“评估者分歧”作为一项核心指标纳入，并停止依赖单一的评估运行结果。

Abstract: LLM-as-judge ("grader") components are now standard in evaluation harnesses, including safety evaluations where a pass/fail verdict may gate downstream deployment decisions. A widespread assumption is that setting the grader's sampling temperature to 0 makes grading deterministic. We test this assumption against a real safety-evaluation codebase (Japan AISI's open-source aisev) and show it fails on two levels. First, the harness invokes its grader without setting temperature or seed; the underlying provider silently applies its default of 1.0, so items near the decision boundary flip pass/fail across identical runs (per-item disagreement up to ~50% over 20 runs). Second, pinning temperature=0 reduces but does not eliminate flips: across 690 API calls spanning two providers, three model tiers, and five sampling configurations, 1-2 of 7 borderline items remain non-reproducible even under forced greedy decoding (top_k=1). Claude Opus 4.7/4.8 has since deprecated temperature entirely, rendering the primary mitigation inapplicable to newer model generations. These findings expose a structural gap: evaluation harnesses that report single-run verdicts without variance or grader-disagreement metrics can present noise as a safety property. We release a reproduction harness (690 calls, 7 conditions) and recommend that harnesses treat grader disagreement as a first-class health metric alongside the scores themselves.

Method: 提出了“线索导向团伙发现（CGGD）”范式，并开发了 Clue2Group 框架。该方法首先构建紧凑的局部调查上下文以过滤噪声，利用多语义时空图神经网络（GNN）估计受限于线索的局部风险场，最后整合风险、结构和先验模式证据来重构完整的洗钱团伙。

Abstract: Money Laundering Group Discovery (MLGD) aims to identify hidden criminal groups and recover their complete structures in large-scale financial networks. Existing graph anomaly detection methods mainly produce node-level risk alerts, while global group discovery methods passively search for suspicious groups over the whole network. Both are mismatched with real Anti-money-laundering (AML) investigations, where analysts usually start from a concrete clue and gradually expand the investigation to recover the responsible group. To address this gap, we propose Clue-Guided Group Discovery (CGGD), where a laundering group is progressively recovered from an initial clue set through analyst interaction. We further propose Clue2Group, a framework that first constructs a compact local investigation context to reduce noise and preserve chain-like and cycle-like laundering structures. It then estimates a clue-conditioned local risk field with a multi-semantic local-temporal GNN, and finally integrates risk, structural, and prior-pattern evidence to recover a coherent laundering group. Experiments on two large-scale AML benchmarks show that Clue2Group provides a practical clue-driven analysis framework for AML investigations, offering a feasible step toward bridging the gap between graph-based AML research and real investigation workflows.

### [76] [Federated Hash Projected Latent Factor Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26192)

Traditional HL methods typically require users to upload personal data to a central server, which is incompatible with increasingly stringent data security regulations. Federated Learning (FL) provides a decentralized paradigm for learning globally optimal models without centralizing private data. However, most FL methods rely on transmitting large-scale real-valued gradient information, leading to high communication overhead and potential privacy risks. Integrating HL into FL is a promising solution. Nevertheless, existing HL methods suffer from limited representational capacity of binary codes, which may degrade model accuracy. To address this challenge, we propose a Federated Hash Projected Latent Factor (FHPLF) model. FHPLF introduces three key innovations: (a) replacing real-valued gradient matrices with binary gradient-like matrices, significantly reducing computation, storage, and communication costs while enhancing privacy protection; (b) leveraging Projected Hamming Distance for similarity modeling, which captures the importance of individual binary bits to improve representation capability; and (c) proposing a Secure Binary Gradient Reassembly and Privacy-Enhanced Upload (SBG-PEU) strategy to further reduce the risk of user interaction leakage during transmission. Extensive experiments on four real-world datasets demonstrate that FHPLF consistently outperforms state-of-the-art HL and FL methods, achieving a favorable trade-off among accuracy, efficiency, and privacy preservation.

### [78] [Topology-Informed Neural Networks for Flood Detection in Optical and Synthetic Aperture Radar Imagery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26204)

Method: 本文采用拓扑数据分析（TDA）方法，系统地提取了SEN12-FLOOD数据集中图像的拓扑描述符。研究将这些提取的拓扑特征作为输入，与现有的神经网络架构结合，验证了其在洪水检测任务中的有效性，并对比分析了其在提升模型可解释性方面的作用。

Result: 研究结果表明，拓扑描述符不仅在洪水检测中携带了具有实际意义的信号，而且能够作为现有深度学习模型的补充，有效提升洪水检测的整体性能及模型内部决策的可解释性。

Conclusion: 通过将拓扑描述符整合进神经网络，本文证明了拓扑数据分析（TDA）不仅能提供独立于图像像素的有效洪水信号，还能显著增强现有洪水检测系统的稳健性和可解释性，为遥感领域中安全关键的任务提供了一种有效的分析框架。

Abstract: Floods frequently impact regions around the world. Rapid and accurate flood detection is crucial for emergency response and timely mitigation of human and economic loss. The expanding availability of satellite data and advances in artificial intelligence have enhanced monitoring of environmental hazards, but many flood events remain challenging to detect because cloud cover obscures optical satellite imagery. Rambour et al. introduced the SEN12-FLOOD dataset and extracted per-image features using a ResNet-50 convolutional neural network backbone, then fed these features into a gated recurrent unit network to show that temporal information can substantially improve accuracy compared to single-image baselines. More recently, Chamatidis et al. showed that a vision transformer can achieve strong performance with popular convolutional architectures. However, these models typically function as opaque black boxes, making it difficult to interpret their decision boundaries, learned features, and internal reasoning, especially in safety-critical domains like remote sensing. In contrast, topological data analysis (TDA) provides a mathematically grounded framework for capturing global structural features of data. TDA has emerged as a powerful tool for analyzing complex imagery, especially imagery with geometrically interpretable structures, of which floods are a prime candidate. In this work, we systematically evaluate topological descriptors for flood detection using the open-source SEN12-FLOOD dataset. By extracting topological features from each image and incorporating them into neural networks, we demonstrate that topological descriptors carry meaningful flood signals independently and complement existing networks to yield more robust and interpretable flood detection systems.

### [80] [Fast LeWorldModel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26217)
*Yuntian Gao,Xiangyu Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Fast-LeWM 通过将逐步滚动改进为并行的动作前缀预测，显著提升了视觉世界模型在规划时的速度与精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LeWM 等视觉世界模型在进行规划时依赖单步自回归滚动，导致计算开销大，且随着规划视界的增加，累积的潜在空间误差会导致性能显著下降。

Method: 提出 Fast-LeWM 模型，核心思想是用“动作前缀预测”取代传统的单步自回归滚动（rollout）。通过将动作序列的各前缀进行编码，模型能并行预测不同时长的未来潜在状态，并利用最后一个前缀标记直接评估规划结果，避免了中间状态的反复计算。

Result: Fast-LeWM 在多项任务中实现了比 LeWM 更高的成功率，显著降低了规划耗时，且在长视界预测中表现出更小的潜在空间误差增长。

Conclusion: Fast-LeWM 通过引入动作前缀预测机制，成功解决了现有视觉世界模型在规划时的计算效率瓶颈与误差累积问题，证明了直接建模动作序列效果而非单步迭代是构建高效视觉世界模型的有效途径。

Abstract: Joint-Embedding Predictive Architectures (JEPAs), including recent LeWorldModel (LeWM), have become a promising foundation for reconstruction-free visual world models. For visual planning, however, LeWM evaluates candidate action sequences by repeatedly applying a local one-step latent transition model. This autoregressive rollout makes planning computationally expensive and exposes the predicted trajectory to accumulated latent errors as the horizon grows. We propose Fast LeWorldModel (Fast-LeWM), a fast latent world model that replaces repeated local rollout with action-prefix prediction. Given the current latent and a candidate action sequence, Fast-LeWM encodes its prefixes and predicts the future latents reached after executing those prefixes in parallel. By making action prefixes the basic prediction unit, Fast-LeWM directly models action effects accumulated to different extents over multiple horizons. This prefix-level supervision forces the model to learn how states continuously evolve under different action prefixes, rather than only fitting one-step state transitions. During planning, the predictor can use the last prefix token from the encoded action sequence to evaluate the corresponding future latent without explicitly rolling through each intermediate imagined state. Across multiple tasks, Fast-LeWM improves average success over LeWM while substantially reducing planning time, achieving lower open-loop latent loss whose growth becomes significantly slower as the rollout horizon increases.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种将DUI建模为混合比例估计问题的方法。具体而言，该方法通过生成合成的非成员样本，提取多样化的成员信号，从而估算候选数据集在模型训练中的参与比例，克服了传统方法对资源消耗和数据访问限制的依赖。

Abstract: How much of my data was used to train a machine learning model? Dataset Usage Inference (DUI) aims to answer this by estimating what fraction of a dataset contributed to a model's training. However, existing DUI methods rely on assumptions that rarely hold in practice: they require training expensive shadow models to imitate the target model, and they assume access to both known training samples and an in-distribution held-out set confirmed to be absent from training. These conditions make current approaches impractical for modern large models and real data ownership disputes. We introduce a practical DUI framework that removes these constraints. Our method requires neither shadow models nor real held-out data. Instead, it generates synthetic non-member samples, extracts diverse membership signals, and casts DUI as a mixture proportion estimation problem to estimate what share of the candidate dataset was used during training. Experiments on large image generative models show that our method reliably quantifies dataset usage, providing a practical tool for data owners to determine how much of their data was used to train a model.

Abstract: Symmetries are important for many deep learning tasks, ranging from applications in the sciences to medical imaging. However, there is an ongoing debate about whether to impose symmetry constraints on the neural network architecture (yielding equivariant neural networks) or learn them from augmented training data. Although equivariant networks are well-studied theoretically, much less is known about data augmentation, since analyzing augmentation requires control over the training dynamics. Inspired by recent results that show that augmented infinite deep ensembles are exactly equivariant, we study data augmentation for Bayesian neural networks (BNNs) trained with variational inference. We focus on variational distributions in the exponential family and derive conditions under which exact equivariance is reached. We furthermore obtain bounds on the equivariance error and introduce three novel symmetrization techniques which boost the effect of data augmentation in this setting. We conduct extensive numerical experiments which show that one of our symmetrization methods (orbit expansion) outperforms the baseline in both equivariance and overall performance. Our code is available at github.com/dmw1998/augment-BNNs
