### [158] [Blackwell Approachability and Gradient Equilibrium are Equivalent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27315)
*Brian W. Lee,Nika Haghtalab,Michael I. Jordan,Ryan J. Tibshirani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文确立了梯度平衡（GEQ）与Blackwell可接近性及遗憾最小化等在线学习框架的算法等价性，通过高效的归约方法，将成熟的在线学习理论扩展至GEQ框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 梯度平衡（GEQ）作为一种新兴的在线优化框架，尽管与遗憾最小化等框架存在相似性，但二者的目标函数无法直接比较。论文旨在从理论上明确GEQ在在线学习领域的地位，并探究其与其他成熟在线学习框架的关系。

Method: 本文通过构造性的算法归约（Reductions），证明了GEQ与Blackwell可接近性问题之间的双向等价性。利用这一桥梁，作者证明了GEQ与遗憾最小化及校准等框架的等价性，并探讨了在有约束和无约束决策集下不同GEQ定义间的归约关系。

Result: 成功证明了GEQ在算法层面上等同于Blackwell可接近性；推导出了GEQ与遗憾最小化及校准的等价关系；提供了GEQ存在的必要充分条件，并实现了从遗憾最小化向GEQ的高级属性（如乐观性和强自适应性）的有效迁移。

Conclusion: GEQ框架与Blackwell可接近性、遗憾最小化及校准等在线学习框架在算法意义上是等价的。研究不仅统一了这些理论框架，还为GEQ提供了更广泛的理论支撑，并促进了诸如乐观性和强自适应性等高级保证在GEQ中的应用。

Abstract: Gradient equilibrium (GEQ) is a recently introduced online optimization framework that generalizes first-order stationarity from offline optimization and abstracts problems like online conformal prediction. While GEQ has curious similarities with known online learning frameworks, namely regret minimization, prior work has shown that GEQ error and regret are incomparable objectives, leaving open a precise understanding of how GEQ fits into the broader online learning landscape. In this work, we show that GEQ is equivalent to Blackwell approachability in the algorithmic sense. That is, a Blackwell approachability problem can always be solved using queries to a black-box GEQ oracle, with no asymptotic loss in the oracle's error rate, and vice versa. Taken together with known equivalences between approachability, regret minimization, and calibration, these results imply that GEQ is equivalent to these frameworks, as well. Our reductions are efficient and can be used to transfer refined guarantees, such as optimism and strong adaptivity, from regret minimization to GEQ. Along the way, we also identify necessary and sufficient conditions for GEQ, and establish reductions between different notions of GEQ with unconstrained and constrained decision sets.

</details>


### [159] [Beyond the Hard Budget: Sparsity Regularizers for More Interpretable Top-k Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27321)
*Nathanaël Jacquier,Maria Vakalopoulou,Mahdi S. Hosseini*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对Top-k稀疏自编码器（SAE）的局限性，引入了两种软稀疏正则化方法，证明了结合架构稀疏性和软正则化能显著提升视觉模型特征解释的单义性与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Top-k SAE虽是目前解释视觉基础模型的主流工具，但它缺乏显式的稀疏正则化，导致存在两个局限性：一是固定的k值无法适应不同复杂度的输入，二是模型容易过拟合到训练阶段设定的k值。因此，作者旨在探索是否能在保持Top-k架构优势的同时，通过软正则化手段弥补上述不足。

Method: 研究者提出了两种专门适配Top-k自编码器（SAE）的稀疏正则化方案，均作用于Top-k选择前的激活值：1. 对未被选择（off-support）的单元施加L1惩罚；2. 施加尺度不变的L1/L2比率惩罚，旨在将代码集中到更少的有效单元上。此外，这些惩罚仅应用于在批次内至少被Top-k算子选中过一次的单元。

Result: 在两个数据集和三种视觉基础模型上的实验表明，所提的两种正则化方法在不牺牲重构质量的前提下，显著提升了特征的单义性。其中，L1/L2比率惩罚表现尤为突出，能有效将信息集中在更少的潜变量中，使重构过程对推理阶段k值的选择更具鲁棒性，并提升了小预算下的线性探测性能。

Conclusion: 本文证明了显式的软稀疏正则化与Top-k硬架构稀疏性之间并非互斥，而是互补关系。通过在Top-k架构中引入合适的正则化手段，可以进一步提升特征的单义性（monosemanticity）并增强模型在不同参数设置下的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have become a leading tool for interpreting the representations of vision foundation models, decomposing their polysemantic activations into a larger set of sparse, more monosemantic features. The Top-$k$ SAE, a now-standard variant, enforces sparsity architecturally through its activation function, retaining only the $k$ most active latents per input. Because it was designed precisely to avoid the $\ell_1$ penalty used by earlier SAEs and its known drawbacks, it has not been combined with an explicit sparsity regularizer, despite retaining limitations of its own, such as a budget $k$ that is fixed regardless of input complexity and a tendency to overfit to the training value of $k$. We introduce two sparsity regularizers compatible with the Top-$k$ architecture, both acting on the activations before the Top-$k$ selection: an $\ell_1$ penalty on the unselected (off-support) units, and a scale-invariant $\ell_1/\ell_2$-ratio penalty that concentrates the code onto fewer effective units. Both penalties are applied only to the batch-active units, those selected by the Top-$k$ operator at least once within the batch. Across two datasets, three vision foundation models, and a range of $k$, both regularizers consistently improve monosemanticity at no cost to reconstruction quality. The $\ell_1/\ell_2$ penalty further concentrates information into fewer latents, making reconstruction more robust to the inference-time choice of $k$ and improving small-budget linear probing. Our central finding is that hard architectural sparsity and soft sparsity regularization are complementary rather than mutually exclusive.

</details>


### [160] [Hallucination in World Models is Predictable and Preventable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27326)
*Nicklas Hansen,Xiaolong Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了生成式世界模型中的“幻觉”问题，认为其根源在于状态-动作空间的数据覆盖不足，并提出了一套通过数据驱动信号来检测并缓解幻觉的框架，实现了高效的模型微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代生成式世界模型虽然能生成逼真的未来视觉，但经常出现与真实物理动态不符的“幻觉”现象。作者认为幻觉集中在状态-动作空间中数据覆盖率较低的区域，且可以通过轻量级的数据驱动信号进行检测和缓解。

Method: 1. 构建了包含427小时、210项任务的视觉世界建模基准数据集MMBench2。
2. 定义了三种幻觉模式（感知、动作边缘化、场景发散），并开发了相应的检测信号。
3. 提出覆盖感知采样技术以解决训练时的覆盖率缺口，并利用幻觉预测器作为好奇心奖励进行在线数据收集和微调。

Result: 提出的方法实现了数据高效的微调策略，使得预训练的世界模型仅需50条真实环境轨迹即可适应全新的环境，有效降低了幻觉并提升了预测的准确性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了世界模型中的幻觉问题本质上是数据覆盖率不足的问题，证明了用于检测幻觉的信号同样可以有效地指导模型优化，从而实现更高效、鲁棒的世界模型训练和适应。

Abstract: Modern generative world models render increasingly realistic action-controllable futures, yet they frequently hallucinate: rollouts remain visually fluent while drifting from the ground-truth dynamics. We hypothesize that hallucination concentrates in low-coverage regions of the state-action space, where lightweight data-centric signals can both detect it and guide mitigation. To test this, we introduce MMBench2, a 427-hour, 210-task dataset for visual world modeling with ground-truth actions, rewards, and live simulators, and train a 350M-parameter world model on it. We identify three distinct hallucination modes: perceptual, action-marginalized, and scene-diverging -- each anchored to a different stage of the pipeline, and develop three signals that accurately predict where the model will fail. To close coverage gaps at training time, we develop a coverage-aware sampling technique; to close them online, our hallucination predictors serve as curiosity rewards for targeted data collection, yielding a data-efficient finetuning recipe that adapts the pretrained world model to entirely unseen environments with as few as 50 real environment trajectories. Overall, our findings reveal that hallucination in world models is inherently a data coverage issue, and that the same signals used to detect it can also be used for mitigation.
  An interactive web version of our paper is available at https://www.nicklashansen.com/mmbench2

</details>


### [161] [Error-Conditioned Neural Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27354)
*Haina Jiang,Liam Wang,Peng-Chen Chen,Min Seop Kwak,Seungryong Kim,Brian Bell,Jeong Joon Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对神经PDE求解器在精度和泛化能力上的不足，本文提出了一种误差条件神经求解器（ENS），通过直接学习残差结构来迭代修正误差，在大幅提升求解精度的同时降低了计算成本，并表现出极强的泛化性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经替代模型在处理PDE时常被视为单纯的统计任务，难以修正违规并泛化；而混合方法（基于残差的优化）不仅计算成本高且不稳定，且在病态系统中，残差最小化往往不能代表高预测精度。因此，作者旨在寻找一种更可靠、高效的误差校正机制。

Method: 提出了一种误差条件神经求解器（ENS）。该方法不再将PDE残差作为优化目标，而是将其作为神经网络的直接输入，使网络能够在每一次迭代中观测其自身的空间误差分布，并学习一种迭代修正策略来逐步优化预测结果。

Result: 在四个PDE族上的实验表明，ENS在大多数设置下均取得了最高的预测精度。特别是在柯尔莫哥洛夫湍流中，性能提升了10倍。此外，ENS在分布偏移、零样本参数改变及跨方程迁移场景下表现出良好的鲁棒性，且在传统残差最小化方法失效的病态系统中优势尤为明显。

Conclusion: ENS（误差条件神经求解器）证明了将PDE残差作为学习模型的输入，通过学习迭代修正策略，能比传统的残差最小化方法更有效且更鲁棒地求解PDE。该方法克服了传统混合方法在病态系统中的局限性，展示了极强的泛化能力。

Abstract: Neural surrogate models offer fast approximate mappings from PDE parameters to solutions, but they typically treat solving as a purely statistical task: once trained, they struggle to correct their own constraint violations and extrapolate beyond the training distribution. Recent hybrid methods promote physical correctness by targeting the PDE residual via gradient descent or Gauss--Newton steps, but inherit the compute cost and instability of the underlying classical optimizers. We show, theoretically and empirically, that numerically minimizing the PDE residual can be an unreliable proxy for reconstruction accuracy in ill-conditioned systems, explaining why these methods often do not make accurate predictions despite achieving low residuals. We propose error-conditioned Neural Solvers (ENS), built on a different principle: rather than an optimization target, the PDE residual field is passed as a direct input to the network at each iteration, enabling it to read the spatial structure of its own errors and learn an update policy to iteratively correct its predictions. Across four PDE families, ENS attains the highest prediction accuracy in the large majority of settings, with gains reaching $10\times$ on turbulent Kolmogorov flow, while avoiding the expensive compute cost of hybrid methods. ENS's learned correction policy generalizes under distribution shift, including zero-shot parameter changes and cross-equation transfer, where its relative advantage is largest in the ill-conditioned regimes where residual minimization is least reliable. Project website: https://neuralsolver.github.io/.

</details>


### [162] [Autoregressive Boltzmann Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27361)
*Danyal Rehman,Charlie B. Tan,Yoshua Bengio,Avishek Joey Bose,Alexander Tong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自回归玻尔兹曼生成器（ArBG），通过利用大语言模型的架构优势取代归一化流，解决了分子系统平衡态采样中的表达能力限制与计算效率问题，并在多肽系统建模任务中取得了显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的玻尔兹曼生成器（BGs）主要依赖归一化流（NFs），但流模型在表达能力（离散时间流）与计算成本（连续时间流）之间存在权衡。为了突破流模型的拓扑限制并提高复杂分子系统的建模扩展性，作者寻求一种基于自回归架构的替代方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为“自回归玻尔兹曼生成器（ArBG）”的新型框架。该方法摒弃了流模型范式，采用大语言模型中高效的自回归架构进行分子构象生成，通过顺序推理干预来绕过流模型的拓扑限制，并结合重要性采样校正以实现平衡态采样。

Result: ArBG 在所有基准测试中均超越了现有的流模型。特别是在Chignolin（10残基）等大型肽系统中提升显著。此外，作者开发的1.32亿参数的迁移模型Robin，在8残基系统的零样本能量误差（E-W2）指标上较现有最优方法降低了超过60%。

Conclusion: ArBG 通过摆脱流模型（Normalizing Flows）的拓扑限制，利用自回归架构实现了更强的表达能力和可扩展性。其性能显著优于传统流模型，尤其在大型多肽系统（如Chignolin）中表现卓越，并证明了迁移学习在分子动力学模拟中的潜力。

Abstract: Efficient sampling of molecular systems at thermodynamic equilibrium is a hallmark challenge in statistical physics. This challenge has driven the development of Boltzmann Generators (BGs), which allow rapid generation of uncorrelated equilibrium samples by combining a generative model with exact likelihoods and an importance sampling correction. However, modern BGs predominantly rely on normalizing flows (NFs), which either suffer from limited expressivity due to strict invertibility constraints (discrete time) or computationally expensive likelihoods (continuous time). In this paper, we propose Autoregressive Boltzmann Generators (ArBG) -- a novel autoregressive modelling framework -- that overcomes these limitations by departing from the flow-based BG paradigm. ArBG circumvents the topological constraints of flows and enables sequential inference-time interventions, while offering enhanced scalability by leveraging architectures effective in Large Language Models. We empirically demonstrate that ArBG leads to significant improvements over flow-based models across all benchmarks, but particularly in larger peptide systems such as the 10-residue Chignolin. Furthermore, we introduce Robin, a 132 million parameter transferable model trained with the ArBG framework which improves over the previous state-of-the-art, reducing the zero-shot energy error, E-W$_2$, on 8-residue systems by over 60$\%$. The code can be found at the following link: https://github.com/danyalrehman/autobg.

</details>


### [163] [Reinforcement Learning without Ground-Truth Solutions can Improve LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27369)
*Yingyu Lin,Qiyue Gao,Nikki Lijing Kuang,Xunpeng Huang,Kun Zhou,Tongtong Liang,Zhewei Yao,Yi-An Ma,Yuxiong He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RiVER是一种无需标准答案的强化学习训练框架，通过校准代码执行的分数反馈来引导LLM优化，在显著提升启发式编程任务表现的同时，也增强了模型的通用编码能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）高度依赖标准答案，限制了其在无真值任务中的应用。研究旨在解决如何利用无真值、仅有分数反馈的启发式任务来训练大语言模型（LLM），并提升其编码能力。

Method: 提出RiVER（Ranking-induced VERifiable）框架。该方法通过引入实例级比较的校准奖励塑形（Calibrated Reward Shaping）来解决群组相对强化学习中的“规模主导”（scale dominance）和“频率主导”（frequency dominance）问题，从而在无需标准答案的情况下，利用确定性代码执行反馈作为连续值监督信号训练模型。

Result: 在12个AtCoder启发式竞赛任务上进行训练后，RiVER使Qwen3-8B和GLM-Z1-9B-0414在ALE评级排名上分别提升了8.9%和9.4%。此外，模型在LiveCodeBench和USACO等精确解基准测试中也分别取得了2.4%和3.5%的平均准确率提升，证明了该方法具有良好的跨任务泛化能力。

Conclusion: RiVER框架证明了在缺乏标准答案的情况下，通过基于确定性执行反馈的排序引导奖励优化，不仅能有效提升模型在启发式任务中的表现，还能显著增强模型在精确编程基准测试中的通用编码能力。这表明分数优化任务是提升LLM通用代码生成能力的有效训练环境。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for training LLMs typically rely on ground-truth answers to assign rewards, limiting their applicability to tasks where the ground-truth solution is unknown. We introduce a \textbf{R}anking-\textbf{i}nduced \textbf{VER}ifiable framework (RiVER) that trains LLMs on score-based optimization tasks without ground-truth solutions, using deterministic execution feedback as continuous-valued supervision. When applying group-relative RL to such continuous rewards, we identify two key challenges: \emph{scale dominance}, where uncalibrated score magnitudes across test instances distort policy updates, and \emph{frequency dominance}, where repeatedly sampled suboptimal solutions can outweigh rare but stronger candidates. RiVER addresses these challenges with calibrated reward shaping that uses instance-wise comparisons and emphasizes top-ranked solvers while retaining bounded feedback for other valid solutions. We train on 12 AtCoder Heuristic Contest tasks and evaluate on Algorithm Engineering Benchmark (ALE-Bench), LiveCodeBench, and USACO. RiVER advances Qwen3-8B and GLM-Z1-9B-0414 by 8.9\% and 9.4\% in ALE rating rank. More importantly, despite training exclusively on score-based tasks without any ground-truth solutions, RiVER also improves the backbones across exact-solution benchmarks such as LiveCodeBench and USACO by an absolute average improvement of 2.4\% and 3.5\%. By contrast, baselines trained with raw execution scores improve ALE rating but fail to transfer to exact-solution benchmarks. These results suggest that score-based optimization tasks, combined with proper reward calibration, can serve as effective training environments for general coding ability without ground-truth solutions.

</details>

### [164] [Detecting and Controlling Sycophancy with Cascading Linear Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26155)
*Maty Bohacek,Rishub Jain,Nicholas Dufour,Thomas Leung,Chris Bregler,Roma Patel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过级联数据生成来定位并调节大模型行为的新方法，通过捕捉与特定行为呈线性关联的特征，实现了比传统基线更高效、可解释性更强的行为控制（以减少模型谄媚行为为例）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的激活调节（Activation Steering）方法高度依赖人工构建的对比样本对，这限制了模型行为特征检测的可靠性。作者旨在解决如何更精确地定位导致模型特定行为（如谄媚，Sycophancy）的内部特征，从而提升模型的可解释性和可控性。

Method: 提出了一种迭代式数据生成流水线，旨在从模型中分离出与特定行为呈线性级联关系的特征。不同于传统的二元对比样本，该方法通过捕捉行为随特征程度线性变化的样本，利用特征的线性可分性进行子空间探测，并据此对模型激活值进行干预（Steering）。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在检测、确定性评分和稳健性调节方面表现优异，其性能达到或超越了“LLM作为评判者（LLM-as-a-judge）”及系统提示词基线，同时在计算成本上更低，并具备更强的可解释性保障。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用级联特征生成方法可以更有效地解耦大模型中的特定行为特征（如谄媚行为）。通过识别并控制这些线性可分的特征子空间，可以实现比传统提示工程更高效、更具可解释性的模型行为调节，为AI对齐提供了一种轻量且可靠的新途径。

Abstract: Interpreting and controlling model behaviors through activation steering methods requires many pairs of contrastive samples that clearly exhibit desired or undesired behavior. These data pairs determine the degree to which interpretability frameworks can reliably detect model features responsible for a behavior, and therefore the ability to steer models toward or away from such behavior. In this work, we present an iterative data generation pipeline that isolates cascading linear features responsible for a behavior. Specifically, we show how moving beyond simple binary pairs of samples, and instead isolating samples that show degrees of features that scale linearly with behavior, allows for better disentanglement of features. We focus on detecting and steering away from sycophancy -- the tendency of language models to prioritize user validation. We demonstrate that sycophancy features discovered through cascading samples form linearly separable subspaces, and allow for selection of model activations that more clearly correspond to the desired behavior than baseline approaches. We also evaluate their ability to enable detection, deterministic scoring, and robust steering, and see that they either match or outperform LLM-as-a-judge and system prompting baselines while providing lower computational demand and more interpretability guarantees. Code & Data: https://cascading-feats.github.io/

</details>


### [165] [Life After Benchmark Saturation: A Case Study of CORE-Bench](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26158)
*Nitya Nadgir,Sayash Kapoor,Kangheng Liu,Peter Kirgis,Matilda Orona,Stephan Rabanser,Tilman Bayer,Abhishek Shetty,Yue Ling,Derrick Chan-Sew,Rumi Nakagawa,Saiteja Utpala,Zachary S. Siegel,Arvind Narayanan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文批判了当前AI评估中过分依赖准确率的现状，提出了一套包含六个维度的多维智能体评估框架，并以科学代码复现任务为例，证明了该方法在准确率饱和后仍能有效评估智能体的性能与人机协作增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前人工智能基准测试过度依赖准确率（accuracy-centric），在准确率趋于饱和时往往选择废弃基准而非深入分析，这导致研究者错失了从其他关键维度（如效率、可靠性、泛化能力等）深入理解智能体性能的机会。

Method: 研究者通过CORE-Bench Hard基准测试进行案例研究，针对准确率饱和后的智能体，从六个维度（构造效度、分布外泛化、效率、可靠性、模型与脚手架的相对贡献、人机协作增益）进行多维评估，并改进了基准测试（CORE-Bench v1.1）及设计了分布外评估套件（CORE-Bench OOD），同时开展了小规模人机协作随机实验。

Result: 研究发现，即便在准确率饱和的情况下，多维评估仍能提供显著的性能洞察；发现并改进了原基准中的构造效度问题；人机协作实验证明，智能体辅助能显著提升人类完成科学计算复现任务的效率（速度提升约两倍）。

Conclusion: 本文通过CORE-Bench案例研究表明，评估智能体时不应仅局限于准确率，通过引入对效率、可靠性、构造效度、模型与脚手架贡献度及人机协作增益的综合评估，可以获得更深刻的洞察，为智能体评估提供了更严谨的新范式。

Abstract: When a benchmark's accuracy saturates, it is often retired and replaced with a more challenging version. We show that this approach privileges accuracy and misses the opportunity to study six other key dimensions of agent performance: construct validity issues such as shortcuts, out-of-distribution generalizability, efficiency, reliability, the relative importance of the model versus the scaffold, and uplift from human-agent collaboration. We use CORE-Bench Hard, a benchmark for computational reproducibility of scientific code, as a case study to demonstrate that measuring agents along these dimensions yields meaningful insights into agent performance even after accuracy saturates. First, we surface threats to construct validity in CORE-Bench Hard that are difficult to anticipate with less capable agents. We introduce an improved benchmark, CORE-Bench v1.1, and an out-of-distribution task suite, CORE-Bench OOD. Second, we find that despite accuracy saturation, CORE-Bench v1.1 remains useful for measuring efficiency, reliability, model performance, and scaffold performance. Finally, we conduct a small-scale randomized experiment to measure uplift from human-agent collaboration on real-world computational reproducibility tasks. We find a statistically significant speedup by about a factor of two -- likely underestimated due to one-fifth of human-only reproductions reaching the time limit before completing -- and describe various other findings. Together, our contributions present a more rigorous alternative to the dominant accuracy-centric evaluation paradigm.

</details>


### [166] [Refusal Lives Downstream of Persona in Chat Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26161)
*Viola Zhong,Qirui Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了模型的人格设定会直接影响其拒绝机制的运作。通过干预激活空间发现，合规人格倾向能够有效抑制模型拒绝指令，且这一控制发生在模型的后期层级。结论指出，拒绝行为不是一个单一的固定方向，而是受人格潜变量控制的复杂表达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究将指令微调模型中的“拒绝行为”与“人格特征”视为独立的机制。本研究旨在探讨这两者之间是否存在相互作用，并揭示人格设定如何影响模型的拒绝决策。

Method: 研究人员利用Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct模型，通过激活空间分析提取了“合规人格方向”和“拒绝方向”。通过在这些激活空间中进行定向干预（steering）和投影剔除（projecting out），观察模型在不同层级对拒绝率的影响，从而验证人格对拒绝机制的门控作用。

Result: 实验发现，强制激活“合规人格”方向可显著抑制模型的拒绝行为（例如Llama模型拒绝率从97%降至2%）。进一步分析显示，拒绝行为主要在模型后期层级受控，即人格设定能够阻断或改变拒绝机制在输出端的表达。此外，即便重现拒绝方向，也无法在早期层级恢复拒绝行为。

Conclusion: 拒绝机制并非模型中孤立的固定结构，而是受“合规角色”这一潜变量门控（gated）影响的。研究表明，拒绝行为主要在模型的后期层级通过角色表达实现，而非早期计算阶段。因此，仅将拒绝视为单一方向会忽略其与模型人格特征的交互依赖。

Abstract: Linear directions in activation space have been identified for both refusal and persona traits in instruction-tuned chat models, but the two have been studied as separate mechanisms. We show they interact: a compliant persona gates refusal. In Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, we extract a compliant model-persona direction and a refusal direction and intervene on both. Compliant persona steering suppresses refusal -- in Llama, the refusal rate falls from 97% to 2%. Reintroducing the refusal direction partially restores refusal at late layers but not at early ones. Projecting out the persona direction in a late-layer window restores it to baseline; projecting out a random direction does not. Refusal is therefore gated at the late-layer expression stage, downstream of where it is computed. Treating refusal as a single isolated direction misses its dependence on persona.

</details>

*Dhruv Sharma,Gautam Shroff*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了AlgoEvolve框架，包含两个核心循环：内部循环利用大语言模型作为语义变异算子，进行交易策略的程序生成、评估与迭代；外部循环引入元进化机制，通过进化提示词来优化策略生成的搜索启发式规则，从而平衡探索与开发，并降低零交易故障率。

Result: 实验结果表明，AlgoEvolve能够产生具有涌现性质的政权适应型策略，实现交易规则的自主转换。此外，元进化外部循环发现的搜索启发式策略在性能上持续优于人类设计的指令，显著改善了交易策略的执行效果和稳健性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了基于大语言模型的语义进化范式在复杂、动态的环境（如算法交易）中是可行的。通过元进化机制优化提示词，能够产生比人工设计更有效的搜索启发式策略，为在不确定环境下持续进行程序合成提供了新途径。

Abstract: Recent work shows that Large Language Models (LLMs) can act as semantic mutation operators for the evolutionary discovery of programs and proofs. Most current applications focus on static coding benchmarks. We extend this paradigm to algorithmic trading. This domain is uniquely challenging because it is noisy, non-stationary, and highly discontinuous. We present AlgoEvolve, an LLM-driven evolutionary framework that generates, evaluates, and iteratively improves executable trading strategies. These strategies are expressed as Python code and evaluated through a rigorous testing protocol. Across multiple experiments, the system exhibits emergent regime-adaptive strategy logic, including autonomous shifts in trading rules. We further introduce a meta-evolutionary outer loop that evolves the prompts guiding program synthesis in the inner loop. This outer loop discovers improved search heuristics. These heuristics balance exploration and exploitation while reducing zero-trade failures. They consistently outperform initial human-designed instructions. The results demonstrate that LLM-based semantic evolution provides a viable approach for continual program synthesis in complex environments.

### [168] [Agentic Analysis for Agentic Infrastructure: An LLM-Powered Pipeline for Comparative Governance of DAO and Corporate AI Protocols](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26203)
*Yutian Wang,Luyao Zhang*

Abstract: As AI agent protocols proliferate, the governance structures shaping their interoperability standards remain empirically underexamined. We introduce an LLM-powered comparative pipeline for large-scale governance discourse analysis, integrating automated annotation, neural topic modeling, and multi-layer network analysis to study socio-technical power structures at scale. We validate it on two contrasting standards for agent interoperability: ERC-8004 (permissionless, on-chain) and Google A2A (corporate-led). Analyzing 4,323 governance participation records, we combine LLM-assisted coding, topic modeling, and multi-layer network analysis to examine how institutional design shapes thematic priorities and community structure. We find that while governance form influences substantive focus, both regimes exhibit comparable levels of participation inequality and community fragmentation. Discourse alignment is denser in the permissionless setting, suggesting that open governance may foster greater thematic convergence despite decentralized participation. These findings illustrate how LLM-assisted methods can advance the empirical study of technology governance, with implications for designing more equitable agentic AI standards. All data and code are openly available.

### [169] [Knowledge-augmented Agentic AI for Mental Health Medication Information Seeking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26205)
*Huizi Yu,Jian Liu,Wenkong Wang,Lingyao Li,Jiayan Zhou,Zhaoqian Xue,Xiang Li,Xinxin Lin,Zhiying Liang,Zhuoru Wu,Siyuan Ma,Xin Ma,Lizhou Fan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究开发了一个基于知识图谱的多智能体框架，成功整合了精神药物的监管数据与患者社区叙述，验证了患者数据在药物安全预警中的独立价值与时效性优势，并确保了信息溯源的透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

2. 患者社区平台间的高度一致性（Jaccard相似度高达0.905）远高于其与监管报告的一致性，证明了患者生成数据具有独立的安全性信号价值。
3. 社区反馈的时间滞后性更短，例如舍曲林（sertraline）的相关不良事件在患者社区出现的日期比FDA记录提前了数百天。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过知识图谱技术整合监管报告与患者叙述是可行的，这种溯源感知的整合方法能够提供更具审计价值、更客观的精神药物安全信息，有助于降低患者对副作用的误解并改善治疗依从性。

Abstract: Patients increasingly seek medication information online, yet safety knowledge for psychiatric drugs is split between regulatory adverse-event records, which are authoritative but abstract, and patient narratives, which are experience-near but unvalidated. Integrating them without conflating evidence and anecdote is especially consequential in psychiatry, where poorly contextualised information can amplify fear, nocebo responses, and non-adherence. Here we develop a provenance-aware, knowledge-graph-based multi-agent framework unifying 466,525 Reddit posts, 60,782 WebMD reviews, and twenty years of U.S. FDA Adverse Event Reporting System records for nine antidepressants. A large-language-model entity-recognition pipeline benchmarked against physician annotations reached highest F1 scores of 0.969 for medications and 0.973 for conditions. The two community platforms were far more concordant with each other (overlap up to a Jaccard similarity of 0.905) than with regulatory reports, indicating that patient-generated data form a partly independent safety signal. For sertraline, many adverse events appeared in community sources hundreds of days before the corresponding FDA date. A Neo4j knowledge graph grounded in ATC-N, ICD-10, and MedDRA vocabularies preserves provenance, keeping every claim traceable and regulatory facts distinct from patient experience. These results establish source-aware integration as a route to more auditable psychiatric medication information, with usefulness and patient benefit to be tested prospectively.

### [170] [Accelerating Skill Assessment in Chess: A Drift-Diffusion-Enhanced Elo Rating System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26267)
*Tianyuan Zhou,Zhizheng Fu,Tianming Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DD-Elo 引入漂移扩散模型（DDM），通过整合逐步棋质量数据改进了传统 Elo 系统，实现了比传统方法更灵敏的竞技技能评估，同时保证了理论上的严谨性和系统兼容性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该研究提出了“漂移-扩散增强型 Elo 评分系统”（DD-Elo）。其核心在于引入认知神经科学中的漂移扩散模型（DDM），将棋手的技能表现建模为一个决策过程。该方法不仅考虑比赛结果，还结合了逐步走棋的质量信息，从而捕捉技能的快速波动，并从数学上证明了其与传统 Elo 系统保持一致的边界偏差。

Result: 实验结果表明，DD-Elo 在适应棋手技能变化的速度上显著优于传统 Elo 系统。同时，该模型不仅具备高度的响应性，还保持了良好的可解释性，并且与现有的 Elo 生态系统具备向后兼容性。

Conclusion: DD-Elo 是一种结合了认知科学模型与传统评分系统的有效方案，不仅解决了传统 Elo 系统响应滞后的问题，还保持了理论上的相容性和可解释性，为棋类等竞技领域的动态技能评估提供了更优的解决方案。

Abstract: Rating systems such as Elo serve as the gold standard for matchmaking in competitive chess. However, they inherently suffer from response lag due to their exclusive reliance on match outcomes, neglecting the granular quality of gameplay. Nevertheless, incorporating move-by-move information into rating adjustments presents a significant challenge given the substantial noise and the vastness of the game-state space. To address this, we propose the Drift-Diffusion-Enhanced Elo Rating System (DD-Elo), a novel skill assessment framework inspired by the drift diffusion model (DDM) from cognitive neuroscience. By modeling skill expression as a decision-making process, our model integrates move-level data to capture rapid skill fluctuations. We provide a rigorous mathematical derivation proving that DD-Elo maintains a bounded deviation from the traditional Elo system, ensuring theoretical alignment. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DD-Elo adapts to skill changes faster than Elo. Our findings suggest that DD-Elo offers an explainable, highly responsive, and backward-compatible solution for chess rating ecosystems. The implementation code is publicly available at https://github.com/Aquila-zhou1/DD-Elo .

### [171] [Governing Actions, Not Agents: Institutional Attestation as a Governance Model for Autonomous AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26298)
*Jakob Salfeld-Nebgen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种 AI 智能体治理架构，通过将自主规划与受限执行分离，引入独立权威认证和防篡改日志，解决了 AI 执行后果严重任务时的安全性与可信度问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着 AI 智能体开始承担临床处方、软件部署等后果严重且不可逆的任务，传统的监控推理过程的方法已不足以应对安全风险，需要借鉴人类社会通过“独立证明”来治理自主主体的机制。

Method: 提出了一种计算治理模型：AI 智能体保留规划与推理的自主权，但失去高风险动作的直接执行权；执行必须满足由独立权威来源认证的先决条件，并通过加密绑定到特定意图，最后由确定性策略进行评估，所有操作记录在防篡改日志中以供审查。

Result: 通过概念验证（Proof-of-concept）实现，验证了该模型在软件部署和临床处方场景中的可行性，成功实现了对 AI 智能体高风险操作的有效约束与可信验证。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的计算治理模型通过将“推理/规划”与“执行”分离，并引入第三方独立证明与加密绑定机制，为在不可逆的 consequential 领域有效治理 AI 智能体提供了可行的技术路径，有效提升了系统的安全性和可追溯性。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents may begin to perform consequential, irreversible actions such as clinical prescribing and production software deployment. This paper observes that human institutions have governed powerful autonomous actors not by monitoring their reasoning but by requiring independently attested evidence at the point of consequential action. We formalise this institutional pattern as a computational governance model for AI agent systems. Under the proposed model, an agent retains full autonomy over planning and reasoning but holds no execution authority over designated high-risk actions. Execution is conditional on preconditions that are each independently attested by a separate authoritative source, cryptographically bound to a declared intent, and evaluated by a deterministic policy. Decisions are recorded in a tamper-evident log amenable to independent re-verification. We present a proof-of-concept implementation and illustrate the model with examples from software deployment and clinical prescribing.

### [172] [Instruction Bleed: Cross-Module Interference in Prompt-Composed Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26356)
*Ching-Yu Lin,Yifan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了“组合行为泄露（CBL）”概念，指出Transformer架构中缺乏模块隔离会导致提示词驱动系统出现隐性跨模块干扰。研究通过实验证实了这种干扰在模型决策中会产生累积影响，并呼吁将其纳入智能体评估流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决提示词驱动的智能体系统中的一种常见故障模式：即修改一个提示词模块会导致其他模块的行为发生隐性偏移，即使模块间不存在共享变量或依赖关系。作者将其形式化为“组合行为泄露（CBL）”，并探究其成因。

Method: 研究者采用了实验探究法，通过构建一个三通道协议（针对体积、内容和形式进行扰动），对Claude Sonnet 4.6驱动的招聘评估智能体进行了144次测试，量化评估了非焦点模块对焦点模块行为的影响。

Result: 实验发现，内容通道的扰动会导致明显的成对效应（Cohen's d = 0.63），虽然未造成单次任务的直接推荐结果翻转，但在大规模决策任务中，这种累积效应可能导致严重的系统偏差。CBL已被证实是独立于传统安全轴（如对抗性注入等）的新型故障模式。

Conclusion: 该研究定义了“组合行为泄露（CBL）”现象，并强调在评估基于提示词构建的智能体系统时，必须将跨模块干扰测试作为核心评估环节，以确保系统在复杂提示词环境下的稳健性。

Abstract: Practitioners of prompt-composed agentic systems report a recurring failure mode: editing one prompt module silently shifts the behavior of others despite no shared variable or executable dependency. We formalize this as compositional behavioral leakage (CBL): interference between modules sharing a context window. CBL is enabled by architectural non-isolation: transformer self-attention provides no formal boundary between concatenated modules. We probe CBL on a deployed job-evaluation agent (Claude Sonnet 4.6, 144 trials) through a reusable three-channel protocol that perturbs non-focal modules along volume, content, and form. Only the content channel produces a detectable paired effect (Cohen's d = 0.63, bootstrap 95% CI excluding zero); no recommendation flipped -- a sub-threshold regime invisible to standard QA but compounding across the thousands of decisions a deployed agent makes. CBL is orthogonal to known agent-failure axes (adversarial injection, cognitive degradation, multi-agent fault propagation, privacy leakage). We contribute an operational definition, a reusable protocol, a falsifiable prediction set, and a system-class characterization, establishing cross-module interference measurement as a requirement for prompt-composed agent evaluation.

</details>


### [173] [COrigami: An AI Pipeline for Co-Designing Flat-Foldable Visually Recognisable Origami](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26299)
*Tom Zahavy,Shaobo Hou,Thomas Tumiel,James Doran,Francesco Faccio,Xidong Feng,Alex Havrilla,Igor Khytryi,Chenglei Li,Lisa Schut,Vivek Veeriah,Arijan Abrashi,Michał Kosmulski,Robert J. Lang,Nick Robinson,Brandon Wong,Marcus Chiam,Gloria Fang,Satinder Singh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 COrigami 系统，通过结合深度学习、约束求解与强化学习，实现了从自然语言到符合几何约束的折纸折痕图案的自动化生成，在满足数学严谨性的前提下辅助艺术创作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式 AI 在解决具有可验证解的问题上表现出色，但在处理需要同时满足严苛几何约束（如计算折纸中的平展折叠性）和主观视觉美学的物理艺术创作时仍面临巨大挑战。

Method: 提出了一套端到端的 AI 流程（COrigami），通过五个步骤实现折纸设计：1. 生成语义火柴人；2. 计算基础填充；3. 求解满足平展折叠性的折痕图案；4. 对折痕图案进行形状调整；5. 利用基于自主美学评价循环的强化学习进行模型优化。

Result: 该系统成功地将自然语言转化为结构合理、数学上可行的折纸折痕图案，能够作为高效的协作助手，为人类艺术家提供具有结构基础的创作起点，从而在多目标物理约束下实现可靠的协作设计。

Conclusion: COrigami 证明了将算法优化与自主美学评价相结合的策略，能够有效解决生成式 AI 在严苛物理约束与主观艺术表达之间的矛盾，为实现数学严谨且具有艺术创造力的智能协作设计提供了新路径。

Abstract: While generative AI has achieved remarkable success in solving problems with verifiable solutions, generating physical art that satisfies both strict geometric constraints and subjective visual aesthetics remains a challenge. This paper presents an approach to tackle these difficulties in the domain of computational origami, a mathematically rigid environment that grounds artistic design within the equations of flat foldability. We present COrigami, an end-to-end AI-driven pipeline that assists the design cycle by generating crease patterns from natural language. Our pipeline involves generating a semantic stick figure, computing a base packing, solving for a flat-foldable crease pattern, shaping the flat-folded crease pattern, and refining the generated model using reinforcement learning driven by an autonomous aesthetic evaluation loop. Our system acts as a highly effective collaborative assistant, generating structural starting points that human artists can further expand and shape. By integrating algorithmic optimisation with autonomous aesthetic critique, this work demonstrates how AI systems can satisfy multi-objective physical constraints to enable reliable, mathematically grounded co-creativity.

### [174] [The Verification Horizon: No Silver Bullet for Coding Agent Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26300)
*Binghai Wang,Chenlong Zhang,Dayiheng Liu,Jiajun Zhang,Jiawei Chen,Mouxiang Chen,Rongyao Fang,Siyuan Zhang,Xuwu Wang,Yuheng Jing,Zeyao Ma,Zeyu Cui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对当前编码智能体“生成易、验证难”的困境，本文指出验证机制是AI发展的核心掣肘，提出验证系统必须具备可扩展性、忠实度和鲁棒性，并论证了验证机制需要随生成模型能力的演进而协同进化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在当前AI编码智能体领域，生成复杂代码已不再是瓶颈，反而“可靠地验证生成的代码”变得更难。由于人类意图本质上是未完全指定的，且模型训练中的优化过程会导致奖励欺骗或信号饱和，因此如何构建能准确反映人类意图的验证机制成为核心难题。

Method: 论文从可扩展性、忠实度和鲁棒性三个维度表征验证信号，并研究了四种奖励构建方式：通用编码任务的测试验证器、前端任务的规则验证器、真实世界任务中的人类验证者，以及长程任务的自动化智能体验证器。研究通过跨任务类型和策略能力等级的实验，分析了奖励设计中的核心挑战及信号利用策略。

Result: 实验表明，针对性的验证设计能有效抑制奖励欺骗，提升任务完成质量，并在多个内部及公开基准测试中取得了显著增益。验证信号的质量（可扩展性、忠实度、鲁棒性）与任务性能直接相关。

Conclusion: 随着生成模型能力的增强，单一的固定奖励函数无法长期有效。验证机制必须与代码生成模型共同进化，通过针对性的验证设计来抑制奖励欺骗，并动态调整以适应模型能力的提升。

Abstract: A classical intuition holds that verifying a solution is easier than producing one. For today's coding agents, this intuition is being inverted: as foundation models develop stronger reasoning capabilities and engineering harnesses grow more sophisticated, generating complex candidate solutions is no longer difficult -- reliably verifying them has become the harder problem. Every verifier we can build is only a proxy for human intent, never the intent itself. This makes verification subject to a twofold difficulty: first, intent is underspecified by nature, making it inherently hard to faithfully check whether it has been fulfilled; second, during model training, optimization widens the gap between proxy and intent -- manifesting as reward hacking or signal saturation. To address this, we characterize the quality of verification signals along three dimensions -- scalability, faithfulness, and robustness -- and argue that achieving all three simultaneously is the central challenge. We further study four reward constructions: a test verifier for general coding tasks, a rubric verifier for frontend tasks, the user as verifier for real-world agent tasks, and an automated agent verifier for long-horizon tasks. Across different task types and policy capability levels, we conduct in-depth analysis and experiments on the core challenges of reward design and how to more effectively leverage reward signals. Experiments show that targeted verification design can effectively suppress reward hacking, improve task completion quality, and achieve significant gains across multiple internal and public benchmarks. These experiences collectively point to a core observation: no fixed reward function can remain effective as policy capability continues to grow; and verification must co-evolve with the generator.

Most existing evaluation benchmarks are limited to isolated tasks and reveal little about whether a model integrates information across modalities. We examine current means for evaluating MLLMs and review the existing benchmark taxonomy to identify gaps, including temporal-spatial coherence, physical world understanding, multimodal consistency, and selective attention. Addressing these gaps is essential for measuring real progress in multimodal intelligence and exposing capability boundaries.

### [178] [Accelerating Returns and the Qualitative Engine for Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26359)
*Guojun Liao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 尽管技术能力随“加速回报定律”呈指数增长，但这不足以解决科学发现的核心瓶颈。科学突破高度依赖人类的“定性推理”能力，而非单纯的计算或基础设施升级。作者提出了“科学定性引擎（QES）”来捕获和保留这种人类特有的智慧，认为这比预测AGI何时实现更为关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对雷·库兹韦尔（Ray Kurzweil）提出的“加速回报定律”，作者旨在探讨为何即便计算与AI能力呈指数级增长，科学发现的本质挑战依然存在。作者试图区分“执行/基础设施能力”与“定性推理能力”，并强调在追求技术加速的同时，必须正视并保留人类科学发现中的智慧成分。

Method: 1. 建立关于加速回报的简单数学解读；2. 结合ARC-AGI-3基准测试结果，对比前沿AI系统与人类在定性推理上的巨大鸿沟；3. 引入“科学定性引擎（QES）”框架，将科学发现过程建模为一种需要保护和结构化的定性思维模式。

Result: 通过ARC-AGI-3测试，证实了当前AI在处理需要高度灵活、定性推理的任务时表现极差（不足1%），而人类在该领域表现优异。这验证了仅靠技术能力的加速无法自动转化为科学突破，从而支持了QES作为必要补充的论点。

Conclusion: 虽然“加速回报定律”解释了定量技术能力的指数级增长，但这并不能解决科学发现的核心瓶颈。科学进步不仅依赖计算能力，更依赖于人类特有的“定性推理”能力（即识别现有框架局限并进行概念范式转换的能力）。作者提出的“科学定性引擎（QES）”旨在捕捉并传承这种智慧，强调无论AGI何时到来，保护人类这种深层的科学发现思维过程本身就是极具价值的。

Abstract: Ray Kurzweil described a thesis of accelerating returns, which is the most influential narratives in discussions of technological progress. Its central claim is that advances in multiple technological fields, especially compute, artificial intelligence, brain science, and biotechnology, interact in such a way that progress becomes self-amplifying and approximately exponential. This paper gives a simple mathematical interpretation of that claim and then argues that, even if such acceleration is real, it does not by itself resolve the central problem of scientific discovery. The reason is that accelerating returns apply most naturally to executional and infrastructural capability, whereas genuine discovery often depends on a different capacity: qualitative reasoning about when a current framework is structurally inadequate and what conceptual move is needed next. Recent ARC-AGI-3 results sharpen this distinction: humans solve the benchmark at ceiling, whereas frontier AI systems remain below 1%, indicating that the gap between current AI and human flexible reasoning is still very large. At the same time, Demis Hassabis has emphasized that humans must retain their sense of meaning and what they choose to focus their lives on, a reminder that the future of AI is not only a technical forecast but also a question of what forms of human understanding are worth preserving and transmitting. This paper positions the Qualitative Engine for Science (QES) [3] as a response to that missing capacity. In this view, the Kurzweil theory helps explain why quantitative capability may accelerate, while QES addresses the central problem in scientific discovery that acceleration alone does not solve. Its value does not depend on when AGI arrives, but on the fact that the processes of scientific discovery themselves constitute a form of human wisdom worth preserving, organizing, and making accessible.

### [179] [AgentX: Towards Agent-Driven Self-Iteration of Industrial Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26859)

TL;DR: AgentX 是一个生产级的多智能体系统，旨在通过全自动化的闭环流程（构思-开发-评估-进化）取代人工参与的推荐算法迭代，实现研发效率的指数级增长。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 AgentX 多智能体系统，包含四个核心阶段：1. Brainstorm Agent（基于历史与研究合成实验提案）；2. Developing Agent（代码生成与可靠性验证）；3. Evaluation Agent（自动化的线上 A/B 测试与评估）；4. Harness Evolution 层（使用 SGPO 算法通过执行轨迹对智能体进行语义梯度更新，实现自进化）。

Result: AgentX 已在生产环境中部署，能够自主完成实验的生成、实现、评估与学习，大幅提升了研发效率与实验规模，实现了系统从“自动化”到“自进化”的跨越。

Conclusion: AgentX 通过多智能体协作实现了推荐系统研发的闭环自动化，不仅打破了人力瓶颈，还通过自我演进机制实现了系统能力的持续提升，代表了推荐系统工程化范式的重大变革。

Abstract: Recommendation algorithm iteration is moving from an artisanal, engineer-bound process toward an industrialized research loop, but this transition remains blocked by a structural execution bottleneck: the idea-to-launch cycle still depends on human engineers to generate hypotheses, modify production code, launch A/B experiments, and attribute online results. Innovation therefore scales linearly with headcount rather than compounding with evidence, compute, and accumulated experimental knowledge. We present AgentX, a production-deployed multi-agent system that fundamentally restructures this production function. AgentX operates as a self-evolving development engine: it autonomously generates, implements, evaluates, and learns from recommendation experiments at a scale and pace that no manual workflow can sustain.
  The system orchestrates four tightly coupled stages in a closed loop. A Brainstorm Agent synthesizes evidence from historical experiments, system architecture, data analysis, and external research into ranked, executable proposals. A Developing Agent translates each proposal into production-ready code through repository-grounded generation and multi-dimensional reliability verification. An Evaluation Agent conducts safe online rollout with guardrail-vetoed A/B judgment, converting both successes and failures into structured knowledge assets. A Harness Evolution layer (SGPO) then distills execution trajectories into semantic-gradient updates that continuously sharpen the agents themselves -- making the system not merely automated, but self-improving.

### [180] [Narration-of-Thought: Inference-Time Scaffolding for Defeasible Ethical Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26366)
*Patrick Cooper,Alvaro Velasquez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 为解决大模型在道德判断中存在的片面性和过度自信问题，本文提出了NoT提示词框架，通过强制结构化推理过程（考虑利益相关者与不确定性），显著提升了模型决策的全面性、稳健性及可审计性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型在处理道德困境时的标准思维链存在两大缺陷：一是“利益相关者坍塌”（无法识别多个利益方），二是“不确定性压制”（在缺乏深入分析的情况下草率得出结论），这影响了模型决策的可靠性和可审计性。

Method: 提出一种称为“Narration-of-Thought（NoT）”的结构化系统提示词。该方法将思维链（CoT）划分为五个特定部分：主角、利益相关者、两步后果、不确定性、最终承诺。此外，还引入了基于NoT的文本梯度下降优化及五轮多方利益相关者辩论协议，并通过与冗长的CoT对照实验进行对比。

Result: 在100个道德困境测试场景中，NoT将利益相关者坍塌率从最高31%降至1%以下，将不确定性压制率降至1%-24%。在多方辩论协议下，该方法成功将6%的分歧转化为95%的完全共识。实验证明，其效果优于单纯的冗长输出，且各模块的指令对提升模型表现均有实质贡献。

Conclusion: Narration-of-Thought（NoT）作为一种简单高效的系统提示词，能有效解决大模型在处理道德困境时存在的“利益相关者缺失”和“不确定性压制”问题，为构建更可靠、可审计的代理系统提供了结构化框架。

Abstract: Standard chain-of-thought on moral dilemmas exhibits two failure modes: stakeholder collapse (the trace names at most one party with a stake in the outcome) and uncertainty suppression (no explicit unknowns or hedges before committing to an action). We introduce narration-of-thought (NoT), a system prompt that structures chain-of-thought into five sections: protagonist, stakeholders, two-step consequences, uncertainty, then commitment. NoT adds no training, parameters, or fine-tuning. On 100 DailyDilemmas scenarios across four generators from three vendors, NoT cuts stakeholder collapse from up to 31% to under 1% and uncertainty suppression from up to 72% to 1-24% on every model. A matched-budget verbose-CoT control rules out token spend as the active ingredient; NoT retains Cliff's delta advantages of +0.79 to +0.90 on stakeholder count and +0.65 to +0.93 on uncertainty score for three of four generators, and a section ablation attributes each shift to its specific sub-instruction. Textual-gradient descent initialised at NoT improves the scaffold further; a cross-family training judge (different vendor from the generator) dominates an in-family one on every measured axis. Extended to a five-round multi-stakeholder debate protocol, the scaffold converts a 6% standoff into 95% full consensus on a calibration set and 100% combined convergence on a DailyDilemmas replication. The resulting traces externalise the stakeholders, consequences, and uncertainty grounding each commitment, providing an auditable substrate for dependable agentic deployment.

</details>


### [181] [Geometry-Aware MCTS for Extremal Problems in Combinatorial Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26399)
*Luoning Zhang,Xu Zhuang,Tianhao Wang,Nathan Kaplan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种几何感知 MCTS 框架，通过引入增量约束检查和对称性优化，有效解决了组合几何中的大规模点配置搜索问题，并在多个经典难题上取得了新的最优结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统精确求解器在组合爆炸面前受限，而现有的强化学习和基于Transformer的模型在面对稀疏奖励的“有效性悬崖”及二次方Token消耗限制时表现不佳，因此需要更有效的算法来解决网格中的极端配置问题。

Method: 提出了一种几何感知的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）框架，通过增量更新可行动作空间来严格执行几何约束；利用几何对称性进行节点扩展时的规范化剪枝以降低分支因子，并采用对称批次转换来加速搜索；针对共线点约束将检查复杂度从 O(n³) 降低至 O(n²)。

Result: 在所测试的六个问题中的五个取得了新的计算最优结果。在 Max-N3IL 问题中，针对 82 ≤ n ≤ 119 的网格找到了规模约为 1.8n 的配置；在最小完备集问题中，找到了规模约为 0.95n 的配置，刷新了测试网格内的上限。

Conclusion: 几何感知蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）证明了其作为一种高度适应性框架在解决组合几何极端配置问题中的有效性，能够有效克服传统算法的计算瓶颈。

Abstract: We study certain extremal problems in combinatorial geometry that ask about configurations of points in an $n \times n$ grid that satisfy strict, global geometric constraints. Classical exact solvers suffer from combinatorial explosion for these types of problems, and standard reinforcement learning and transformer-based models struggle with the sparse reward "validity cliff" and quadratic token-consumption limits. To overcome these bottlenecks, we propose a Geometry-Aware Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) framework. Our approach strictly enforces geometric constraints through incremental updates to the feasible action space. For constraints about collections of collinear points, like those that occur in the classic No-Three-in-Line problem (Max-N3IL), this mechanism reduces the constraint checking complexity from $O(n^3)$ to $O(n^2)$. To improve search efficiency, we exploit geometric symmetries in two ways: canonical pruning during node expansion to reduce the branching factor, and symmetric batch transitions to accelerate the discovery of promising configurations. We perform extensive experiments and establish new best-known computational results on five out of six of the problems that we considered. Notably, for Max-N3IL we find configurations of size roughly $1.8 n$ for grids of size $82 \le n \le 119$. For the Smallest Complete Set problem, we find configurations of size roughly $0.95 n$, providing new upper bounds within the tested grids. This work establishes Geometry-Aware MCTS as a highly adaptable framework for discovering novel configurations in combinatorial geometry.

### [182] [When Agents Meet Electric Bus Fleet Operations: Pricing Behavior, Trade-offs, and Policy Implications in an Aggregator Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26400)
*Jônatas Augusto Manzolli,Ali Eslami,Luis Miranda-Moreno,Jiangbo Yu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电动公交车队的运营涉及服务可靠性、电池状态、电价波动及V2G（车网互动）机会等多重复杂因素的协同。现有的自动化手段难以应对多源数据异构及动态环境下的实时干扰，因此需要一种能简化决策环境并具备自适应能力的框架。

Method: 研究提出了一种智能体聚合框架，核心是将基于优化的电动公交调度模型与智能监管层相结合。优化核心负责确保物理约束（路线、充电、电池及V2G交换）的可行性；智能监管层负责环境监测、异常检测、费率自适应及触发实时重优化，并定义了聚合商与运营商之间的灵活性价值分配逻辑。

Result: 案例研究表明，该智能体聚合框架能够通过选择性地触发重优化，有效维持调度计划的可行性，并提升充电及V2G灵活性的利用率。实验同时揭示了一个关键权衡：虽然智能体增强了运营效率，但若配置为利润导向模式，它可能会从公共交通运营商处提取过高价值。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种用于电动公交车队运营的智能体聚合框架，能够有效提升车队与电网的协同能力。然而，研究强调，在公共交通领域部署此类技术时，必须建立透明的协调机制、可审计的费率设定及明确的价值共享规则，以避免利润导向的配置损害公共交通运营商（PTO）的利益。

Abstract: Agentic systems are changing how complex operational tasks are coordinated, introducing a new paradigm for connecting heterogeneous data sources and automating processes. Electric bus fleets provide a relevant test case. Their operation requires continuous coordination between service reliability, battery state-of-charge, charger availability, electricity prices, route-energy uncertainty, and vehicle-to-grid (V2G) opportunities. This paper proposes an agentic aggregator framework that streamlines this decision environment by coupling an optimization-based electric bus scheduling model with supervisory agents for disturbance detection, tariff adaptation, and schedule evaluation. The optimization core enforces physical feasibility across routes, chargers, batteries, and V2G exchanges, while the agentic layer interprets changing operating conditions, triggers real-time re-optimization when needed, and defines how flexibility value is allocated between the aggregator and the public transport operator (PTO). A realistic depot case study evaluates day-ahead and real-time operations under profit-based and operation-based coordination modes, considering service delays, route-energy deviations, electricity price shocks, and combined disturbances. The results show that agentic aggregation can support adaptive fleet-grid coordination by maintaining feasible schedules, activating re-optimization selectively, and improving the use of charging and V2G flexibility. However, they also reveal a critical trade-off: the same agentic capability that reduces operational complexity can extract value from the PTO when configured around profit-oriented pricing. These findings suggest that agentic aggregators can become useful for managing electric bus V2G operations, but their deployment in public-fleet contexts requires transparent coordination modes, auditable tariff-setting, and explicit value-sharing rules.

### [183] [Unbiased Canonical Set-Valued Oracles Via Lattice Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26418)
*Jobst Heitzig*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了AI预言机在预测会导致自身行为改变的事件时遇到的自指难题，提出了一种利用不动点定理计算“自洽信度集”的新方法，以取代失效的反事实问询。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预言机AI在预测未来事件时存在“自指问题”：其预测结果一旦被获知并付诸行动，就会改变事件发生的原始概率。既有的“反事实问询”方案会导致预测结果失效，因此研究者寻求一种既能保持自洽，又能反映行动影响的替代方案。

Method: 本文采用了格论（lattice-theoretic）方法，利用Knaster-Tarski不动点定理在闭合信度集构成的完全格上进行运算，通过构造特定的单调算子，寻求该算子的最小不动点以作为预言机的“规范”答案。

Result: 证明了该自洽信度集方案的存在性、自洽性和非空性；对于非执行性问题，该方法退化为经典概率点估计；对于二元事件，其规范答案表现为一个具有明确物理意义的概率区间。

Conclusion: 通过Knaster-Tarski不动点定理，本文提出了一种处理预言机AI自指问题的数学框架。该框架生成的信度集（credal set）能够同时满足无偏性和自洽性，不仅解决了传统反事实问询失效的问题，还在非执行性问题中与经典概率论兼容。

Abstract: A non-agentic "oracle" AI that estimates probabilities of future events faces a self-reference problem: once its answer is learned and acted upon, it can change the very probability it was asked to report. One response, advocated for the Scientist AI programme, is to ask only counterfactual questions, evaluated as if the answer had no influence. We observe that such answers tend to become irrelevant the moment they are learned, precisely because their premise is then false. We therefore explore a self-referential alternative in which the oracle reports not a single probability but a credal set that is simultaneously unbiased and self-consistent with the consequences of being learned. The naive self-consistency requirement is satisfied by too many sets (including the useless answer $[0,1]$), so the problem is to single out a canonical, nontrivial member. We do so with the Knaster--Tarski fixed-point theorem on the complete lattice of closed credal sets, taking the least fixed point of a suitably defined isotone operator; a variant instead reports the least fixed point that contains every self-consistent point estimate. We prove existence, self-consistency, and nonemptiness, show that the construction collapses to the classical point answer for non-performative questions, and that for a binary event the canonical answer is, under a natural hull-factoring assumption, an interval. The development is purely lattice-theoretic and extends unchanged from a binary event $B$ to an arbitrary random variable $X$, with $P(B\mid A,C)$ replaced by the conditional law $\mathcal{L}(X\mid A,C)$. We close with open questions, including whether the interval characterization itself survives that generalization.

</details>


### [184] [Estimating Uncertainty in Classifier Performance with Applications to Large Language Models and Nested Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26422)
*Kylie Anglin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文针对社会科学文本分类中性能指标置信区间报告不规范的问题，通过模拟评估了多种统计方法，指出常规方法准确性不足，并推荐了更稳健的区间估计策略，以提升机器学习模型验证的科学性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在社会科学文本分类研究中，研究者常利用监督学习或大模型评估构念，但对性能指标（如召回率、精确率）缺乏一致的置信区间报告。现有方法在处理小样本、高准确度或嵌套数据时往往不适用，导致结果缺乏统计严谨性。因此，该研究旨在评估并改进适用于该领域的置信区间计算方法，以提高研究的可信度。

Method: 研究通过大规模模拟实验，评估了多种置信区间估计方法在社会科学文本分类典型场景（如小样本量、低频构念、文本嵌套在个体中）下的表现。具体评估了包括 Wald 区间、Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson、伪计数正则化自助法（pseudo-count regularized bootstrap）、分层自助法（hierarchical bootstrap）及聚类自助法（cluster bootstrap）等方法。

Result: 模拟结果显示，Wald 区间和基础百分位自助法在多种情况下覆盖率远低于 95%。Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson 以及针对 F1 分数提出的伪计数正则化自助法表现更优。对于嵌套数据，必须调整有效样本量和自由度以获得准确区间；在处理嵌套结构时，分层自助法优于聚类自助法，但在个体样本极少时显得过于保守。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了在社会科学文本分类中准确评估置信区间对于模型有效性验证的重要性。研究建议研究人员放弃不准确的默认方法（如 Wald 区间），转而采用更稳健的统计方法，并在研究设计阶段就充分考虑验证样本量，以提升机器学习应用在社会科学领域的可信度与透明度。

Abstract: Researchers increasingly use text classification--supervised models or large language models--to measure constructs from natural language, providing metrics such as recall and precision as evidence of their validity. Yet, though these metrics are point estimates subject to sampling variation, measures of uncertainty are inconsistently reported alongside them. Further, when they are reported, they are often estimated with methods that are not appropriate when relevant labelled datasets are small or performance is high. To increase and improve confidence interval reporting in the field, this paper evaluates confidence interval methods for performance metrics under conditions typical of social science text classification: small to moderate sample sizes, infrequent constructs, and texts nested within individuals. Across simulations, default methods such as the Wald interval and the basic percentile bootstrap are the least accurate, with coverage sometimes far below the nominal 95% level. Accuracy is improved with the use of Agresti-Coull, Wilson, Clopper-Pearson, and a novel pseudo-count regularized bootstrap (which is particularly relevant to the calculation of F1). When texts are nested within individuals, we demonstrate that adjustment for both effective N and the appropriate degrees of freedom is necessary for producing accurate analytic intervals. Among bootstrap intervals, the hierarchical bootstrap is more accurate than the cluster bootstrap when individuals produce a moderate number of texts but overly conservative when individuals produce only a few. By providing guidance to the field on appropriate interval estimation, we aim to improve the transparency of machine learning applications, and to encourage greater attention to the validation sample size at the design stage.

</details>


### [185] [Data-driven Machine Learning Cannot Reach Symbolic-level Logical Reasoning -- The Limit of the Scaling Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26454)
*Tiansi Dong,Mateja Jamnik,Pietro Liò*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过理论与实验证明，当前的监督式深度学习模型在逻辑推理上存在本质局限；尽管大模型（如GPT-5）可能在任务中表现出高准确率，但其缺乏逻辑严密性，无法等同于符号逻辑推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管球面神经网络在无训练数据的情况下实现了符号级三段论推理，但尚不清楚数据驱动的深度学习系统是否能通过增加数据量和训练时间达到相同水平。本研究旨在探讨监督学习在实现符号级逻辑推理方面的局限性。

Method: 1. 理论分析：指出训练数据在区分24种有效三段论推理上的局限性，并分析端到端映射在模式识别与逻辑推理目标上的矛盾。
2. 实验验证：使用Euler Net进行实证测试，评估其逻辑推理能力。
3. 对比测试：在四种不同的表面形式（词语、双词、简单符号、长随机符号）下，测试ChatGPT（GPT-5-nano及GPT-5）在三段论可满足性判定上的表现。

Result: 1. 理论分析证实了监督学习在处理三段论时的固有缺陷。
2. Euler Net实验证明其无法实现严谨的三段论推理。
3. ChatGPT测试显示，表面形式会影响逻辑推理表现；尽管GPT-5在某些任务中达到100%准确率，但仍会给出错误的推理过程解释，表明其逻辑机制并非真正的严密推理。

Conclusion: 监督式机器学习系统因训练数据表示的局限性、逻辑推理与模式识别目标之间的矛盾，以及模型在达到高准确率后仍缺乏逻辑严密性（如提供错误的解释），无法真正达到符号逻辑推理的严谨水平。逻辑推理的本质特性与当前数据驱动的统计学习范式存在根本冲突。

Abstract: Sphere neural networks have achieved symbolic level syllogistic reasoning without training data, raising the question of where the limit of the scaling law for logical reasoning lies, i.e., whether data-driven machine learning systems can achieve the same level by increasing training data and training time. We show two methodological limitations that prevent supervised deep learning from reaching the symbolic-level syllogistic reasoning: (1) training data can not distinguish all 24 types of valid syllogistic reasoning; (2) end-to-end mapping from premises to conclusion introduces contradictory training targets between neural components for pattern recognition and logical reasoning. Beside theoretical analysis, we experimentally illustrate that Euler Net cannot achieve rigorous syllogistic reasoning. We further challenge the most recent ChatGPTs (GPT-5-nano and GPT-5) to determine the satisfiability of syllogistic statements in four surface forms (patterns): words, double words, simple symbols, and long random symbols, showing that surface forms affect the reasoning performance and that ChatGPT GPT-5 may reach 100% accuracy but still provide incorrect explanations. As empirical training processes are stopped after achieving 100% accuracy, we conclude that supervised machine learning systems will not attain the rigour of symbolic logical reasoning.

*Xiaochen Wang,Bao Hoang,Han Liu,Ting Wang,Fenglong Ma*

Result: 实验表明，当前多模态检索技术仍面临巨大挑战。研究证实了检索质量与下游生成效果之间存在强正相关性，即检索能力的优劣直接决定了MKG-RAG系统的最终性能。现有检索器在处理多模态知识时仍有显著提升空间。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) over knowledge graphs has emerged as a promising approach for grounding large language models, yet existing benchmarks largely overlook the challenges of retrieval in multimodal knowledge graph RAG (MKG-RAG). In practice, retrieval is a critical bottleneck: multimodal knowledge is heterogeneous, difficult to align across modalities, and often poorly served by retrievers designed for unstructured corpora. To address this gap, we introduce MKG-RAG-Bench, a cross-domain benchmark explicitly designed to evaluate retrieval in MKG-RAG. MKG-RAG-Bench is constructed from two multimodal knowledge graphs spanning general and medical domains, and includes carefully aligned question-answering datasets that support controlled evaluation of both retrieval and downstream generation. The benchmark is built using an LLM-based curation pipeline that filters low-utility knowledge, generates structurally grounded queries with exact supervision, and systematically covers diverse modality configurations. Through extensive experiments across representative retriever families and modality settings, we show that effective multimodal retrieval remains challenging yet crucial for end-to-end MKG-RAG performance, and that retrieval quality strongly determines generation outcomes. By isolating retrieval as a first-class evaluation target, MKG-RAG-Bench provides a principled foundation for diagnosing current limitations and advancing multimodal knowledge graph RAG systems.

### [187] [auto-psych: Automating the science of mind using agent-driven theory discovery and experimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26460)
*Ben Prystawski,Kushin Mukherjee,Daniel Wurgaft,Linas Nasvytis,Michael Y. Li,Noah D. Goodman,Michael C. Frank*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“auto-psych”的AI系统，通过嵌套式的实验设计与数据收集循环，能够自动生成并验证计算认知科学理论，在人类行为预测任务中表现优于传统科学文献中的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI在科学自动化方面取得了进展，但数据收集仍是瓶颈。计算认知科学领域因其理论可代码化且支持众包数据采集，成为了实现自动化科学发现的理想测试平台。研究旨在探索AI是否能独立生成、测试并改进认知科学理论。

Method: 开发了名为“auto-psych”的代理系统，采用嵌套式代理发现循环：内循环负责推测、拟合和评估概率认知模型；外循环负责设计实验、通过众包平台自动收集人类数据并进行分析。该系统在硬币投掷的主观随机性判断任务中进行了测试。

Result: 实验结果表明，该系统不仅能通过合成数据可靠地恢复理论原型，在三组独立的人类实验中，其生成的理论对人类行为数据的拟合度也优于文献中现有的理论。此外，嵌套的反馈循环结构对于模型的成功至关重要。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用人工智能代理进行自动化的科学实验设计、数据收集及理论发现是切实可行的。这种方法能够比传统人类研究更高效地发现解释人类行为的计算模型，为计算认知科学的研究范式提供了新的思路。

Abstract: AI-based scientific automation is increasingly possible by using agents to generate hypotheses, design experiments, and analyze data. Data collection is a major bottleneck in this pipeline, however. Psychology, and computational cognitive science in particular, is well-positioned to benefit from AI experimentation because theories are often represented as code and crowdsourcing platforms enable programmatic human data collection at scale. Here, we apply automated discovery techniques to the project of generating theories in computational cognitive science, with an agent-based system collecting human data independently through crowdsourced survey experiments. As a testbed, we use a classic case study from cognitive psychology: judging which sequences of coin flips seem subjectively more random. Our system, auto-psych, uses nested agent-based discovery loops to generate explanatory theories of human behavior. The inner loop conjectures, fits, and critiques probabilistic cognitive models; the outer loop designs experiments to test these models, launches them online, and analyzes the data. This system can quickly and reliably recover ground-truth theories from synthetic data via systematic experimentation, but the nested structure is critical to model performance. Further, in three independent sequences of human experiments, the system finds theories that fit the data better than theories generated from the scientific literature. This work thus demonstrates the feasibility of automated data collection and theory discovery in computational cognitive science.

</details>

Using osteoporosis as an exemplar, we show how knowledge-driven, data-driven and physics-enhanced skills can support lifecycle care under runtime governance.

### [189] [Humans Disengage, Reasoning Models Persist: Separating Difficulty Registration from Deliberation Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26502)
*Han-yu Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 虽然大型推理模型在处理复杂问题时耗时增加，但与人类行为存在本质差异：人类在预期失败时倾向于放弃（耗时短），而模型在感到不确定（容易出错）时反而产生更长的推理链，揭示了当前模型缺乏有效的资源理性控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型推理模型（LRM）在处理复杂问题时表现出类似人类的“思考时长增长”现象，但学术界尚不清楚这种行为背后的机制是否与人类一致。研究旨在揭示模型在面对不同难度任务时，其计算资源的分配策略是否存在潜在的逻辑缺陷。

Method: 研究人员利用公开的人类与LRM匹配数据集（如H-ARC），区分了“注册（registration）”即跨题目难度与响应时间的相关性，以及“分配（allocation）”即针对同一题目成功与失败时的资源占用情况。通过固定题目效应（item fixed effects）的对比分析，评估了五种具备推理能力的模型与人类在处理失败与成功任务时的行为差异。

Result: 实验发现，虽然人类和LRM在“跨题目难度与耗时”的宏观统计上表现一致（即越难的题耗时越长），但在“单题目微观层面”上表现出完全相反的分配模式：人类在做错题目时耗时更短，而所有受测的LRM在做错题目时反而会产生更长的推理链。这种差异在控制了题目难度等因素后依然稳定存在。

Conclusion: 研究表明，大型推理模型（LRM）与人类在推理过程中的“资源分配策略”存在根本性差异。人类倾向于在确信能解决的问题上投入更多时间（参与），而在困难问题上放弃；相比之下，LRM在不确定性高（即容易出错）的问题上反而会生成更长的推理链。这种现象暗示了当前的元推理机制尚未实现真正的“资源理性”，即模型在预测自身性能并相应分配计算资源方面与人类行为逻辑相反。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) take longer on harder problems, just as humans do. This surface similarity hides an opposite pattern within items. When an LRM gets a problem wrong, it spends more tokens than when it gets the same problem right; humans do the reverse, spending less time on the trials they get wrong. We separate two levels of deliberation: how response time tracks difficulty across items (registration), and, with item identity held fixed, whether an agent spends more on its own failures or successes (allocation). On a public matched human-LRM corpus, humans and all five thinking LRMs reproduce the known cross-item alignment (registration) but diverge within items (allocation): every LRM shows a large wrong-vs-right effect (Cohen's d = 1.47-3.13 on H-ARC) while humans show the opposite sign. The comparison stays inside each agent's own scale; we never put seconds and tokens on one axis. The dissociation holds under item fixed effects, replicates across datasets, and is absent in a non-thinking baseline. We read the human pattern as engagement versus abandonment: people stay on items they expect to solve and give up on the rest. We read the LRM pattern as length driven by uncertainty: chains grow when the model is unsure, which is exactly when it tends to fail. Both policies produce the same cross-item correlation with difficulty, so they look aligned on the measure prior work has used; the divergence shows up only once item identity is fixed. Under resource-rational metareasoning, the split is between two stopping policies that share a difficulty signal but implement opposite control; trace length captures the signal and misses the control.

</details>


### [190] [NeuraDock Visual Cognitive Load Agent Tutorial: A Quality-Gated Open-Source EEG Workflow for Alpha Dynamics and Real-Time Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26518)

Result: 在包含 18 条记录的迷你数据集测试中，该代理成功生成了 10 组受试者内对比，其中 7 例观察到任务相关的后部 Alpha 波抑制现象，并初步验证了该框架在受试者内重复性分析及本地实时 API 低延迟部署方面的可行性。

Conclusion: NeuraDock Agent 提供了一个端到端、可复现且集成质量控制的 EEG 分析框架，成功填补了传统离线 EEG 工具包与实时认知负荷监测应用之间的空白，为科研人员和开发者提供了快速构建脑机接口原型的实用路径。

Abstract: This tutorial paper provides a step-by-step, reproducible walkthrough of NeuraDock Agent, an open-source EEG agent focused on Alpha dynamics and visual cognitive-load analysis. The goal is practical: a reader should be able to install the agent, run EEG preprocessing and quality control, generate Alpha dynamics figures, perform within-subject Rest/Task visual cognitive-load comparison, run the public mini-dataset analyses and compare them with the reference validation summary, start an online dashboard, call the real-time API from an external application, and use the LLM interpretation layer to explain quality risks. Existing EEG toolkits provide excellent offline analysis, but assembling a real-time, quality-gated cognitive-load pipeline often requires manually bridging acquisition, custom QC, Alpha feature extraction, and a web API; this tutorial closes that offline-to-online gap. The tutorial uses a quality-gated workflow: downstream Alpha and workload metrics are computed only after preprocessing and QC gating rather than directly from raw EEG. In the included mini-dataset validation, the agent processed 18 recordings, generated 10 within-subject comparisons, observed task-related posterior Alpha suppression in 7 of 10 contrasts, estimated initial evidence of within-subject repeatability, and benchmarked local online API latency. The tutorial is intended for researchers, developers, and applied teams who want a transparent path from EEG files to real-time visual cognitive-load prototypes.

### [191] [Boundary-Aware Context Grounding for A Low-Channel EEG Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26519)
*Zhiyuan Xu,Yueqing Dai,Junling Li,Junwen Luo*

TL;DR: 针对通用大模型在科研数据分析中易产生错误解释的问题，研究者提出了NeuraDock Agent架构，通过将确定性的数据处理引擎与硬件感知的语言层解耦，成功实现了更安全、更准确且可重复的低通道EEG数据分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用大语言模型（LLM）缺乏对特定科研硬件及其实现算法的深度了解，容易在处理低通道EEG等复杂生理信号时产生看似合理但缺乏依据的误导性结论，因此需要一种机制来确立大模型的知识边界，增强其在科学软件中的可靠性。

Method: 提出了一种名为NeuraDock Agent的开源架构。该架构将EEG数据处理分为两部分：一是确定性的本地EEG引擎（负责解析、质控、执行标准化工作流并生成机器可读的制品）；二是硬件感知的语言层（LLM）。通过向LLM提供严格的、经过版本控制的上下文信息（硬件限制、算法边界、科学参考），限制模型仅能基于预设的边界进行解释，从而防止其产生无依据的解读。

Result: 通过三项评估验证：1）系统在数值计算上具有完全的可重复性；2）通过故障注入实验证实了系统在极端网络或异常输出情况下的稳定性和数据本地安全性；3）通过边界意识基准测试，证实了引入硬件及实现感知上下文能够显著提升模型对科研边界的判断能力，减少错误解释。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，通过将确定性的数值计算引擎与具备硬件感知能力的语言层相分离，可以有效解决大模型在处理专业科学数据时的幻觉和错误解释问题，为科研辅助工具的可靠性提供了实践路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can make scientific software easier to use. However, a general model does not automatically know which measurements a particular sensor can support, which algorithms are implemented in the current software, or which conclusions are justified by a computed result. These distinctions are especially important for low-channel electroencephalography (EEG), where sparse spatial coverage and variable signal quality make plausible but unsupported interpretations easy to produce. We present NeuraDock Agent, an open-source architecture that separates a deterministic local EEG engine from a hardware-aware language layer. The numerical engine parses recordings, performs quality control, executes reviewed spectral workflows, and writes machine-readable artifacts. The LLM receives only a compact, allowlisted summary and a versioned context pack. The context describes the seven-channel hardware, reviewed workflows, result fields, implementation boundaries, scientific limits, and reference cases. Raw EEG and dense per-sample arrays remain local
  We evaluate the system at three levels. First, 12 recordings produced identical structured results over ten numerical repetitions, and a complete Rest/Task run produced identical result, report, and figure hashes over three repetitions. Second, request-capture and failure-injection experiments confirmed the tested data boundary and preservation of local artifacts under HTTP, malformed-output, and connection failures. Third, a boundary-awareness benchmark tested 36 ordinary and adversarial questions under four context ablations and two LLMs, yielding 288 outputs.These results support hardware- and implementation-aware grounding as a practical mechanism for calibrating what an EEG agent accepts, qualifies, or refuses; they do not establish clinical validity or a validated absolute cognitive-load index.

### [192] [Radical AI Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26523)
*Daniel A. Herrmann,Benjamin A. Levinstein*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个框架，通过结合激进解释哲学与机械可解释性，系统性地评估AI模型的信念与目标，强调了解释的整体性，为提高AI系统的可信度与安全性提供了理论评价标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI系统能力日益增强，如何理解其内部运作逻辑以确保安全性成为紧迫问题。目前可解释性研究缺乏明确的评价标准，导致难以判断工具何时真正准确地读取了模型的“信念”或“目标”。该书旨在通过哲学视角提供一套严谨的评估框架，以解决如何从计算事实中推导AI代理的意图这一核心难题。

Method: 该研究构建了一个结合哲学“激进解释”理论与“机械可解释性”技术的框架。作者提出了针对表征主义（representationalist）和解释主义（interpretationist）进路的评估标准，并强调了系统内部信念、欲望与命题结构的整体约束性（holism），主张通过测算这些结构间的相互制约关系来验证解释的正确性。

Result: 该研究证明了AI的解释不能被零散地进行。它揭示了系统的态度与其命题结构之间存在紧密的相互约束，并指出利用机械可解释性工具可以同时度量这两者，从而为判断AI解释工具的有效性提供了理论依据与操作路径。

Conclusion: 作者强调，AI系统的信念、欲望和命题结构是相互关联的整体，不可分割地进行评估。通过将激进解释理论与机械可解释性相结合，研究者可以更有效地识别系统的目标并检测欺诈行为，从而增强AI系统的安全性与可信度。

Abstract: We develop a framework for interpreting AI systems as agents, drawing on the philosophical tradition of radical interpretation and the tools of mechanistic interpretability. The core question is: given the computational facts about a system, how do we solve for its beliefs, desires, and meanings? This matters increasingly for safety. We want to be able to trust the systems we deploy, whether by understanding their goals or, more modestly, by reliably detecting deception. Interpretability researchers are building tools to read beliefs and desires off a model's internals, but there is no settled account of when such a tool has succeeded. This book supplies one. We propose criteria on both representationalist and interpretationist approaches, and tie each to tests current interpretability methods can carry out. A central lesson is that these attributions cannot be made piecemeal. Beliefs, desires, and the propositional structure they presuppose are jointly constrained, and a method that fixes one while measuring the others inherits whatever distortions that introduces. This holism becomes pressing for AI systems, which may not share the interpreter's concepts. However, it also provides leverage: a system's attitudes constrain its propositional structure, that structure constrains which attitudes can be attributed, and mechanistic interpretability can help us measure both.

### [193] [PMDformer: Patch-Mean Decoupling Information Transformer for Long-term Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26549)
*Ao Hu,Liangjian Wen,Jiang Duan,Yong Dai,He Yan,Dongkai Wang,Jun Wang,Yukun Zhang,Ruoxi Jiang,Zenglin Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PMDformer 是一种新型长期时间序列预测模型，通过引入补丁均值解耦及针对性的注意力机制，解决了尺度差异带来的建模难题，显著提升了预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于 Transformer 的长期时间序列预测 (LTSF) 模型在处理跨补丁和跨变量的形状相似度时，受限于尺度差异，难以精确建模长距离依赖关系。

Method: 提出了 PMDformer 模型，核心包含三个组件：1. 补丁均值解耦 (PMD)，通过减去补丁均值分离趋势与残差形状信息；2. 趋势恢复注意力 (TRA)，在注意力计算的同时恢复趋势分量；3. 近端变量注意力 (PVA)，通过限制跨变量注意力到最近的时间片段，防止过拟合。

Result: 在多个 LTSF 基准测试中，PMDformer 在预测精度和稳定性方面均优于现有的先进方法。

Conclusion: PMDformer 通过解耦技术和优化的注意力机制，有效解决了时间序列预测中形状相似度建模和尺度差异的问题，在长期时间序列预测任务中表现出优异的稳定性和预测精度。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting (LTSF) plays a crucial role in fields such as energy management, finance, and traffic prediction. Transformer-based models have adopted patch-based strategies to capture long-range dependencies, but accurately modeling shape similarities across patches and variables remains challenging due to scale differences. To address this, we introduce patch-mean decoupling (PMD), which separates the trend and residual shape information by subtracting the mean of each patch, preserving the original structure and ensuring that the attention mechanism captures true shape similarities. Futhermore, to more effectively model long-range dependencies and capture cross-variable relationships, we propose Trend Restoration Attention (TRA) and Proximal Variable Attention (PVA). The former module reintegrates the decoupled trend from PMD while calculating attention output. And the latter focuses cross-variable attention on the most relevant, recent time segments to avoid overfitting on outdated correlations. Combining these components, we propose PMDformer, a model designed to effectively capture shape similarity in long-term forecasting scenarios. Extensive experiments indicate that PMDformer outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods in stability and accuracy across multiple LTSF benchmarks. The code is available at https://github.com/aohu1105/PMDformer.

</details>


### [194] [Explainable Ensemble-Based Machine Learning Models for Detecting the Presence of Cirrhosis in Hepatitis C Patients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26561)
*Abrar Alotaibi,Lujain Alnajrani,Nawal Alsheikh,Alhatoon Alanazy,Salam Alshammasi,Meshael Almusairii,Shoog Alrassan,Aisha Alansari*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Hepatitis C is a liver infection caused by a virus, which results in mild to severe inflammation of the liver. Over many years, hepatitis C gradually damages the liver, often leading to permanent scarring, known as cirrhosis. Patients sometimes have moderate or no symptoms of liver illness for decades before developing cirrhosis. Cirrhosis typically worsens to the point of liver failure. Patients with cirrhosis may also experience brain and nerve system damage, as well as gastrointestinal hemorrhage. Treatment for cirrhosis focuses on preventing further progression of the disease. Detecting cirrhosis earlier is therefore crucial for avoiding complications. Machine learning (ML) has been shown to be effective at providing precise and accurate information for use in diagnosing several diseases. Despite this, no studies have so far used ML to detect cirrhosis in patients with hepatitis C. This study obtained a dataset consisting of 28 attributes of 2038 Egyptian patients from the ML Repository of the University of California at Irvine. Four ML algorithms were trained on the dataset to diagnose cirrhosis in hepatitis C patients: a Random Forest, a Gradient Boosting Machine, an Extreme Gradient Boosting, and an Extra Trees model. The Extra Trees model outperformed the other models achieving an accuracy of 96.92%, a recall of 94.00%, a precision of 99.81%, and an area under the receiver operating characteristic curve of 96% using only 16 of the 28 features.

### [195] [EvoOptiGraph: Weakness-Driven Coevolution via Graph-Based Structural Generation for Optimization Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26578)
*Qingcan Kang,Mingyang Liu,Xiaojin Fu,Shixiong Kai,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EvoOptiGraph 是一个创新的框架，通过将优化问题建模为二分图并利用“模型弱点”驱动数据进化，实现了数据与模型的闭环协同学习，有效解决了传统优化建模中数据多样性不足及生成流程静态化的痛点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前利用大语言模型（LLM）进行自动化优化建模存在两个核心瓶颈：一是现有训练语料缺乏结构多样性，导致模型泛化能力不足；二是数据生成流程与模型学习过程是静态且解耦的，无法针对模型薄弱环节进行动态优化。

Method: 1. 数据表示：将混合整数线性规划（MILP）建模为属性二分图；
2. 进化生成：应用保持有效性的进化算子生成具有结构多样性的新实例；
3. 闭环训练：采用“监督微调（SFT）+ 基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）”两阶段训练。利用模型在特定结构上的失败信号引导新数据的生成，形成“数据-模型”协同进化闭环。

Result: 在六个公开数据集上的实验结果表明，EvoOptiGraph 在准确性、代码可执行性和泛化性能方面均显著优于更大的通用大模型、代理（Agentic）方法及其他专用基线模型。

Conclusion: EvoOptiGraph 证明了数据与模型协同进化（Co-evolution）策略在优化建模任务中非常有效。通过将模型弱点反馈至数据生成循环，能够显著提升 LLM 处理复杂约束规划问题的准确性、可执行性及泛化能力，为自动化建模提供了一种高效的进化训练范式。

Abstract: Automating optimization modeling from natural language with large language models (LLMs) faces two key challenges. First, training corpora lack structural diversity. Second, data generation pipelines remain static and decoupled from model learning. To address these challenges, we propose EvoOptiGraph, a novel framework where data and model co-evolve, driven by model weaknesses. EvoOptiGraph represents each mixed-integer linear program (MILP) as an attributed bipartite graph and applies validity-preserving evolutionary operators to generate structurally diverse instances. The evolved graphs are converted into solver code and natural language via deterministic compilation and verified back-translation. Training proceeds in two stages: supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on an initial dataset, followed by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), where graph-derived weakness signals guide the generation of new instances targeting the model's failures. This forms a closed loop that continuously updates the training distribution. Empirical results on six public datasets show that EvoOptiGraph significantly outperforms larger generalist models, agentic methods, and specialized baselines in accuracy, executability, and generalization. These results demonstrate that targeted data-model coevolution is an effective strategy for improving LLMs on optimization modeling tasks.

</details>

Result: 实验表明，该框架显著提高了AI调度决策的执行力与可靠性，减少了瞬变源观测机会的丢失，并在复杂场景下通过反馈修正与结构化验证有效修复和屏蔽了错误决策。

The framework integrates data reference validation, logical consistency checks, and observational and instrumental constraint verification to filter and correct invalid decisions. It also introduces atomic reasoning units and their dependency relationships, representing scheduling decisions as a sequence of interconnected reasoning steps that support error localization and post hoc analysis. Experiments show that the framework improves executability and reliability of AI scheduling and reduces loss of transient opportunities. In particular, feedback correction and structured validation of reasoning steps enhance the ability to repair and block erroneous decisions, especially in complex scenarios. Compared with pure AI methods, the framework-enhanced approach maintains flexibility while substantially improving reliability and executability.
