### [200] [SKILL-DISCO: Distilling and Compiling Agent Traces into Reusable Procedural Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26669)
*Zhongxin Guo,Danrui Qi,Hanwen Gu,Peng Cheng,Yongqiang Xiong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对智能体重复解决相似任务的低效问题，本文提出了SkillDisCo框架，通过将成功轨迹蒸馏为可复用的程序化子图，显著提升了智能体的执行效率与成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体在处理相似任务时往往选择从零开始，导致不必要的推理成本和冗长的执行轨迹，且现有研究对程序化技能的适用场景及共享结构表征尚不明确。

Method: 提出SkillDisCo框架，将FSM（有限状态机）定义的场景视为图，通过对成功任务轨迹的蒸馏与编译，提取可复用的参数化控制流子图（PFSM子图），并将其转化为可调用、可执行且可验证的程序化技能。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebArena基准测试中的实验结果表明，SkillDisCo不仅显著提高了任务成功率，还减少了智能体的执行轮数，且该优势在不同模型规模下均具有通用性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，将智能体的共享经验形式化为可复用的执行结构（参数化控制流子图）是提高智能体在复杂任务中效率和成功率的有效途径。SkillDisCo框架通过从成功路径中提取结构化知识，成功弥补了从头开始解决任务的低效性，为开发更具自主性和鲁棒性的智能体提供了新范式。

Abstract: Agents often repeatedly solve similar task instances from scratch, leading to unnecessary reasoning cost and long execution traces. Prior work has explored workflow reuse and executable skill induction, but it remains unclear which task scenarios admit procedural skills and how the shared procedural structure should be represented across successful traces. We study this problem in FSM-defined scenarios, where successful traces can be viewed as paths in an unknown transition graph, and formulate procedural skills as reusable parameterized control-flow subgraphs. Based on this view, we introduce SkillDisCo, a distillation-and-compilation framework that distills reusable PFSM subgraphs from successful traces and compiles them into callable, executable, and verifiable procedural skills. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebArena show that SkillDisCo improves success rates and reduces agent turns across benchmarks and model scales, demonstrating the benefits of representing shared experience as reusable execution structures.

### [201] [NebulaExp-8B: An Empirical Post-Training Pipeline via Full-Scale Ablation Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26671)
*Qiaobo Hao,Yangqian Wu,Shunyi Wang,Zhongjian Zhang,Ziqun Li,Yayin He,Muqing Li,Chen Zhong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NebulaExp是一个针对8B规模LLM的全透明、可复现后训练流水线，通过系统性的数据处理与强化学习策略，显著优化了模型在指令遵循与复杂推理任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的后训练研究普遍缺乏数据构建细节、过滤规则及详细的训练配方，阻碍了社区的可复现性研究以及轻量化模型的优化。因此，作者旨在构建一个完全透明、基于消融实验的后训练流水线。

Method: 提出NebulaExp流水线，包含：1. 数据工程：构建3.84M条SFT样本与200K条RL候选集，运用响应蒸馏、多维交叉验证及难度分级等技术；2. 训练策略：针对指令分支采用三阶段SFT与GRPO强化学习；针对推理分支采用中等难度GRPO；3. 验证机制：引入单教师（OPD）与多教师（MOPD）蒸馏策略，减少对任务验证器的依赖。

Result: 1. 指令模型（Instruct branch）：SFT后平均基准分数从55.01提升至60.99，经GRPO强化学习进一步提升至61.85。2. 推理模型（Reasoning branch）：通过中等难度GRPO，平均推理分数从73.88提升至75.17。3. 蒸馏策略：MOPD利用仅10K样本即实现平均性能4.18分的提升，证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究为8B参数量级的LLM提供了一套完整、透明且可复现的训练配方。实验表明，通过系统化的数据工程和强化学习策略，可以显著提升模型在指令遵循、推理及通用能力上的表现，并揭示了不同能力维度间的权衡关系。

Abstract: Post-training alignment determines the reasoning and human preference following capabilities of large language models, yet most existing works withhold detailed data construction, filtering rules and training recipes, which hinders community reproducibility and lightweight model optimization. This work presents NebulaExp, a fully transparent, ablation-driven post-training pipeline built on Qwen3-8B-base, covering two orthogonal model branches: general instruct model and complex reasoning-specialized model. We curate a raw corpus of 3.84M multi-source SFT samples and a 200K verifiable RL candidate pool, and design an end-to-end data processing stack including response distillation, multi-dimensional cross-verification filtering, fine-grained difficulty grading, task classification and diversity-aware sampling. For the Instruct branch, our three-stage optimized supervised fine-tuning approach NebulaExp-Ins-SFT improves the average benchmark score from the 55.01 baseline of Qwen3-8B-nothink to 60.99. GRPO reinforcement learning then further elevates the average score to 61.85. For the Reasoning branch, medium-difficulty GRPO RL improves average reasoning score from 73.88 to 75.17. To address RL's dependency on task verifiers, we systematically investigate single-teacher and multi-teacher OPD (MOPD): utilizing merely 4K instruction-following samples and outperforms RL baseline by 3.26 points on IFEval with +4.43 average overall gain; MOPD fuses four domain-specialist teachers with merely 10K samples, lifting average performance by 4.18 over the base model. This report provides a fully reproducible empirical post-training recipe for 8B-scale LLMs, and comprehensively dissects the capability trade-offs among instruction adherence, mathematical reasoning, code generation and general knowledge.

</details>


### [202] [Do Safety Guardrails Need to Reason? LeanGuard: A Fast and Light Approach for Robust Moderation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26686)
*Dongbin Na*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 LeanGuard，证明了在大模型安全护栏任务中，复杂的思维链推理（CoT）并不一定能提升准确率或鲁棒性。通过使用轻量级编码器，研究实现了在保持性能的同时将推理计算开销降低约 100 倍，为高效的内容安全检测提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的内容安全护栏通常基于思维链（CoT）推理来判定内容，这导致模型运行缓慢且计算开销巨大。然而，这种推理机制是否真的能提升护栏的准确性仍存疑，特别是在对实时性要求极高的端侧部署场景（如机器人）中，这种沉重的机制可能并不适用。研究旨在探究安全护栏是否真的需要推理。

Method: 研究团队构建了一个受控的对比实验，在相同的语料库上同时训练轻量级双向编码器（LeanGuard）和带推理能力的解码器（Reasoning Guard）。通过仅移除推理链条而保持其他条件固定，对比两者的性能、推理计算成本及鲁棒性。LeanGuard 采用 395M 参数的标签预测编码器，仅需单次前向传播即可完成分类。

Result: 实验结果显示，LeanGuard（395M 参数）在公共基准测试中平均 F1 分数达到 82.90%，性能持平于基于更大规模解码器的推理护栏，但计算开销降低了约 100 倍。此外，LeanGuard 在应对标签噪声和保持低假阳性率下的召回表现上，均优于推理护栏，证明了其更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，对于大语言模型的内容安全护栏任务，思维链（CoT）推理并非必须，且目前常用的“推理护栏”模式在效率和鲁棒性上并不具备明显优势。LeanGuard 证明了轻量级的判别式模型在保持高准确率的同时，能带来显著的计算效率提升（约100倍），这为端侧或实时安全防护提供了更优的路径。

Abstract: In order to screen a prompt or a response, the recent guardrail methods generate a chain-of-thought (CoT) before they issue a verdict. This design follows a common belief that step-by-step reasoning improves a decision. However, CoT also makes the guard heavy and slow, because the model must generate many tokens before it decides. This may not match how guardrails are actually deployed. A guardrail sometimes should not be heavy and slow, and it often runs on-device, for example on an embodied robot. In this paper, we pose a question whether a safety guardrail really needs to reason. To answer this question, we train a lightweight bidirectional encoder and a reasoning guard on the same corpus, and we then remove only the reasoning while we keep everything else fixed. With this controlled same-base comparison, we show that the chain does not improve moderation accuracy. We name the resulting guard LeanGuard. A 395M label-only encoder reaches an average F1 of 82.90 $\pm$ 0.26 over public benchmarks. It matches a reasoning guard that is built on a much larger decoder, while it uses only a single forward pass over an input of at most 512 tokens. This is about a ~100x reduction in inference compute. We further show that this label-only encoder stays robust under training-label noise and retains far more recall at a strict false-positive rate than the reasoning guard, so a heavier reasoning guard is not the more robust choice either. Our finding suggests that the current guardrail benchmarks may not be hard enough to reward reasoning, and that the necessity of CoT for moderation is still not proven. We release all source codes and models including LeanGuard at https://github.com/ndb796/LeanGuard.

</details>

To overcome this limitation, we present LithoDreamer, the first physics-informed World Model (WM) framework for computational lithography, which formulates the ``Layout-Mask-Resist Image-After Development Image (ADI)'' pipeline as a decision-driven multi-step evolution system. LithoDreamer captures feature changes between adjacent states to model stage-specific physics-informed latent spaces, in which it controls process intervention exploration and drives subsequent state transitions. To achieve interpretable intervention optimization without continuous supervision, we propose a contrastive variational optimization paradigm that contrasts the latent differences between intervention paths with variational evolution constraints, guiding the model to generate evolutions consistent with real lithography physics. ### [205] [A Latent ODE Approach to Spatiotemporal Modeling of Cine Cardiac MRI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26718)

Abstract: Cardiac magnetic resonance imaging (CMR) captures rich spatiotemporal information about ventricular structure and motion, but conventional risk models use only a few image-derived indices from selected cardiac phases. These results suggest that continuous full-cycle modeling of ventricular motion provides informative cardiac phenotypes beyond conventional CMR summaries, while external validation in more representative patient cohorts is required before clinical risk-prediction use.

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过引入苏格拉底式推理机制（Socratic midwifery），AI系统能够实现从简单的“工作流自动化”向“基于证据的、具备认识论自主性的自我修正科学发现”跨越。这为在复杂物理环境中实现真正的科学自主探索提供了一种可行且有效的范式。

Abstract: The automation of scientific discovery has reached an inflection point. True autonomous science demands epistemic autonomy--the capacity to construct, challenge and revise physical explanations in response to evidence. Here we introduce AHOIS, a multi-agent AI scientist that embeds Socratic midwifery into closed-loop experimentation. A physics-critic agent interrogates hypotheses through causal questioning, constraint checking, counterexample generation and falsification-criteria formulation. We evaluate AHOIS on a real multimode-fibre optical platform, a high-dimensional system with complex wave transformations, indirect detection, environmental drift and multi-modal acquisition. Without prior encoding schemes, classifiers or speckle models, the system autonomously proposed and validated a random-interference encoding hypothesis, discovered task-adaptive sparse-measurement strategies, diagnosed distinct failure modes (encoding instability, fluorescence contamination and detector noise) and translated a published imaging protocol into an executable workflow on a non-original configuration. The discovered encoding yielded 16x16 measurements with effective rank 56.9 and classification accuracies of 76.97% on MNIST and 83.17% on Fashion-MNIST. Ablations show that Socratic interrogation improves physical consistency, hypothesis completeness, uncertainty calibration and experimental-plan validity. These results establish a route from workflow automation towards evidence-grounded, self-correcting autonomous discovery in complex physical environments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学发现本质上是一个在巨大状态空间中的优化问题。现有研究多关注状态空间的探索，而忽视了评估准则（即目标函数）本身也需要根据研究进展进行同步优化。因此，本文旨在解决如何让评估标准随研究深化而自动进化的难题。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“共识目标聚合”（Consensus Objective Aggregation）的元优化框架。该方法允许大语言模型（LLM）动态生成评估目标函数，并通过相关性加权投票的方式将多个目标函数进行整合，形成一个随认知深化而不断自我纠正和进化的稳定评估准则。

Result: 在3-SAT问题的算法发现任务中，应用该框架后，算法在问题规模 $N$ 上的扩展性从基准的 $\sim N^{2.51}$ 降低至 $\sim N^{1.33}$，并在最大测试算例上实现了约67倍的加速。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过将科学发现形式化为元优化（Meta-optimization），并结合共识目标聚合机制，能够有效优化评估标准，从而在算法发现等复杂科学任务中实现显著的性能提升。该框架具有普适性，为自动化的科学发现开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Scientific discovery is fundamentally an optimization problem, defined by a vast "state space" of theories and experiments, and an evaluation criterion based on quality, novelty, and validity. Large language models (LLMs) have enabled automated exploration of this space, but we argue that simultaneous modification of the evaluation criteria is equally important. Here, we propose formalizing research as meta-optimization, where the optimization objective itself is also being optimized. Our key contribution is "consensus objective aggregation," where LLM-generated objective functions are combined via correlation-weighted voting, yielding a stable, self-correcting evaluation criterion that evolves as understanding deepens. We apply this framework to algorithm discovery for 3-SAT problems based on digital MemComputing machines, reducing the baseline scaling with problem size $N$ from $\sim N^{2.51}$ to $\sim N^{1.33}$ and delivering a $\sim 67\times$ speedup on the largest instances tested. As a problem-agnostic framework, we hope this approach will considerably aid scientific discovery.

### [208] [EGG: An Expert-Guided Agent Framework for Kernel Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26758)
*Yaochen Han,Ke Fan,Hongxu Jiang,Wanqi Xu,Weiyu Xie,Runhua Zhang,Chenhui Zhu,Yixiang Zhang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了EGG（Expert-Guided Agent Framework），将算子生成分解为两个层次化阶段：1. 算法结构设计（建立基础架构）；2. 硬件级调优（执行并行映射、张量分块和内存优化）。同时，设计了阶段感知的多智能体协作机制，用于上下文管理，确保优化过程的稳定性和有效性。

Result: 在KernelBench及实际工作负载上的实验表明，EGG生成的算子平均比PyTorch快2.13倍，且性能优于现有的其他基于Agent和基于强化学习（RL）的方法。

Abstract: High-performance GPU kernels are critical for reducing the exponentially growing computational costs of large language models (LLMs), but their development heavily relies on manual tuning by domain experts. While recent advances in LLM-based approaches show promise for automating kernel generation, they still struggle to achieve both correctness and high performance. This limitation primarily arises from the lack of domain-specific optimization guidance, hindering effective exploration of the optimization space. We propose EGG, an Expert-Guided Agent Framework for Kernel Generation, which incorporates expert optimization principles to guide LLMs' decisions. Inspired by expert workflows, we decompose kernel generation into two hierarchical stages: 1) algorithmic structure design, which establishes a high-quality computational structure foundation; 2) hardware-specific tuning, which performs targeted adjustments through parallel mapping, tensor tiling, and memory optimization. This staged decomposition defines explicit optimization objectives, structuring the design space to achieve progressive refinement. To this end, a stage-aware multi-agent collaboration mechanism is designed for inter and intra-stage context management, ensuring stable optimization trajectories. Experiments on KernelBench and real-world workloads show that EGG achieves a 2.13x average speedup over PyTorch, outperforming existing agent-based and RL-based approaches.

### [209] [ResilPhase: Plug-and-Play Phase Mapping and Noise-Resilient Macro-Trajectory Extrapolation for Diffusion Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26769)
*Qicheng Zhao,Yu Li,Qi Sun,Zheyu Yan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对扩散模型（DiT）加速方案在高加速比下质量严重下降的问题，本文提出了 ResilPhase 框架。该方法通过在 ODE 空间中进行全局漂移外推，配合无导数的重心拉格朗日插值与相位映射约束，成功解决了导数噪声敏感和不稳定性难题，实现了高效且高质量的推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于“缓存后预测（cache-then-forecast）”的 DiT 加速方法在极高加速比下会导致严重的质量下降。根本原因是其基于离散外推的方案与连续扩散轨迹不匹配，且对噪声导数的依赖导致了累积空间误差和高阶不稳定性。因此，急需一种能够稳定预测模型轨迹的加速框架。

Method: 1. 宏观轨迹重构：将加速推理从特征预测转变为基于模型全局漂移（Global Drift）的状态演进，消除特征不一致性；2. 无导数重构：引入重心拉格朗日外推器（Barycentric Lagrange Extrapolator），规避了高阶时间导数噪声带来的不稳定性；3. 相位映射约束：提出有界相位映射（Bounded Phase Mapping）对预测域进行正则化，抑制外推过程中的震荡误差累积。

Result: ResilPhase 在 FLUX.1-dev 和 HunyuanVideo 等大规模模型上进行了广泛验证，实验结果表明，该框架在极高加速比下仍能保持业界领先的生成质量（fidelity），显著优于现有的同类加速方法。

Conclusion: ResilPhase 通过将加速推理重新定义为 ODE 空间中的稳健宏观轨迹外推，有效解决了现有扩散模型（DiT）加速方案中因导数不稳定性导致的质量退化问题，在保持高生成质量的同时实现了显著的推理加速，代表了扩散模型高效推理的一个重要演进方向。

Abstract: The adoption of powerful diffusion models is hindered by their significant inference latency. Recent ``cache-then-forecast'' schemes alleviate this issue by accelerating DiTs using derivative-based polynomials, but they suffer from severe quality degradation at high acceleration ratios. Our analysis reveals its root cause: the discrete extrapolation performed on representations that are misaligned with the continuous diffusion trajectory and are numerically unstable. Thus, accelerated DiTs suffer from accumulated spatial errors, noisy derivative amplification, and high-order instability. We therefore reformulate accelerated inference as stable macro-trajectory extrapolation in ordinary differential equation (ODE) space. Instead of predicting intermediate features, we align forecasting with the model's Global Drift (GD), i.e., the end-to-end state evolution, thereby eliminating feature inconsistency and memory overhead. However, even this smooth macro-trajectory remains vulnerable to the derivative fallacy: its higher-order temporal derivatives are intrinsically noisy. Thus, we introduce a derivative-free barycentric Lagrange extrapolator to effectively bypass derivative instability and approximation error. We further propose a bounded Phase Mapping that regularizes the extrapolation domain, suppressing oscillatory error growth. These elements collectively constitute ResilPhase, a noise-resilient acceleration framework. Experiments on FLUX.1-dev and HunyuanVideo demonstrate state-of-the-art fidelity under aggressive acceleration ratios.

</details>


### [210] [Memory Depth, Not Memory Access: Selective Parametric Consolidation for Long-Running Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26806)
*Haoliang Han*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了长期语言智能体的“记忆深度”问题，提出了EVAF机制，通过选择性地将关键经验固化至模型参数（LoRA），弥补了仅依靠检索系统无法长期维持目标导向行为的缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的检索系统只能在查询时获取事实，无法决定哪些经验应在工作上下文卸载后持续影响模型行为。研究者旨在解决长期运行智能体的“记忆深度”问题，即如何将目标导向的倾向性持久地固化在参数中。

Method: 提出了“循环漂移（loop-drift）协议”作为压力测试，在工作上下文卸载后测试智能体的目标保持能力；引入了EVAF（基于惊喜度和效价门控的LoRA巩固机制），通过选择性地将关键经验写入小的参数存储区来实现记忆的持久化。

Result: 实验表明，在GPT-2、TinyLlama和Mistral-7B上，检索在浅层事实回溯上表现优异，而EVAF在目标持久性和卸载后恢复方面表现更强（得分0.812-0.904），且仅需极少量的参数写入（每200个事件仅2-3次）。同时证明了选择与执行的解耦及模型依赖性。

Conclusion: 选择性参数巩固（如EVAF机制）能提供区别于检索机制的“记忆深度”，对于实现长期语言智能体的目标持久性至关重要。研究表明，记忆的筛选（selection）与执行（actuation）是两个可独立控制的维度，且这种机制在处理长期干扰和任务恢复时优于纯粹的检索系统。

Abstract: Long-running language agents need more than memory access. Retrieval systems can fetch past facts at query time, but they do not decide which experiences should continue to shape behavior after the working context is unloaded. We study this separate problem as memory depth: durable goal-conditioned tendencies written into a small parametric store. We introduce the loop-drift protocol, a controlled stress test in which the retrieval index remains intact while working context is unloaded and goal-conditioned behavior must persist under long-loop interference. We evaluate EVAF, a surprise- and valence-gated LoRA consolidation mechanism. Across GPT-2 and TinyLlama, retrieval is strongest on shallow factual recall (short-fact accuracy 0.956--0.973), while EVAF is strongest on goal persistence and post-unload recovery (0.812--0.904) with only 2--3 parametric writes per 200 events. Mechanism controls show that selective consolidation factorizes into two controllable dimensions: selection and actuation. Matched random gates isolate selection beyond sparse writing; fixed-inner controls across GPT-2, TinyLlama, and Mistral-7B show that inner-loop write strength is model-dependent; and a Mistral-7B matched-gate inversion reveals asymmetric selection-actuation coupling under miscalibrated actuation. Public Memora event streams serve as an external diagnostic, exposing stale-memory invalidation as an unresolved boundary. Within this probe, selective parametric consolidation supplies memory depth distinct from and complementary to retrieval access.

</details>


### [211] [KARLA: Knowledge-base Augmented Retrieval for Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26807)
*Francois Crespin,Fabian M. Suchanek,Nils Holzenberger*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究提出了一种通过训练模型生成特定触发标记来自动查询知识库的方法，实现了大语言模型事实知识的实时获取、动态更新与可溯源性，在提高事实准确度的同时降低了对超大规模模型参数的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大语言模型存在的事实幻觉问题，并克服其知识更新困难、缺乏可解释性以及大模型资源消耗过大等局限。

Method: 提出了一种让大语言模型（LLM）在生成token过程中自动从知识库（KB）检索事实的方法。核心机制是训练模型生成特殊的触发标记（special tokens），由这些标记发起对知识库的查询，从而将外部事实实时整合到模型输出中。

Result: 实验结果显示，该方法在短文本和长文本生成任务中均显著提升了事实准确性。此外，它支持通过修改知识库内容直接更新模型输出，无需重新训练模型参数，且能让较小的模型达到与大型模型相当的事实准确度。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过在生成过程中引入外部知识库查询机制，可以有效提升大语言模型的生成事实性，同时实现知识的动态更新与溯源，为构建更可信、更高效的知识密集型应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: We propose a new method that allows an LLM to automatically pull in factual knowledge from a knowledge base during token generation. This means that (1)~factual knowledge in the LLM output can be updated without retraining the LLM, (2)~facts in the LLM output can be traced to the knowledge base for transparency and explainability, and (3)~smaller models can achieve the same factual accuracy as larger models. Our core idea is to train the model to produce special tokens that trigger a query to the knowledge base. Our experiments show that our method improves factual grounding in both short and long-form generation, and allows factual revisions to take effect through KB edits rather than parameter updates.

</details>


### [212] [Computational Analysis of Heart Rate Variability in Healthy Adults](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26816)
*María J. Lado,Arturo J. Méndez,Leandro Rodriguez-Liñares,Baltasar García Pérez-Schofield,Pedro Cuesta-Morales,Brais Iglesias-Otero,Xose A. Vila*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究评估了健康人群HRV指标的统计特性，指出HRV指标存在冗余与跨研究不一致问题，筛选出一套更具代表性且稳健的HRV评估指标，为临床和科研应用提供了标准化参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 心率变异性（HRV）是评估心脏生理状态的关键指标，但目前针对健康人群的HRV参数研究尚不充分，且缺乏统一的行业“黄金标准”。为了提升HRV在临床诊断和科学研究中的实用价值，迫切需要对各项指标进行系统性评估与筛选。

Method: 研究人员对40名健康成年人（30-50岁，男女各半）进行了心率变异性（HRV）数据采集。利用信号处理与计算分析方法，从时域、频域和非线性三个维度对HRV指标进行了分析，重点评估了数据的正态性、稳定性、相关性、可重复性及一致性，并与Fantasia数据库进行了对比验证。

Result: 研究发现：1. 大多数时域和非线性指标呈正态分布，且存在性别差异；2. HF相关指标稳定性较差；3. HF相关指标间存在高相关性，表明存在冗余；4. 大多数指标与Fantasia数据库相比误差小于10%，但女性SD2和SDNN误差超过15%；5. 频域指标变异性高，跨研究比较难度大，而时域和非线性指标变异性较低。

Conclusion: 该研究通过对健康成年人HRV指标的系统评估，筛选出ApEn、IRRR、HRVi、SD2、MADRR和rMSSD作为最具代表性的指标。这些指标不仅能有效反映心脏自主神经功能，还能提高临床研究的可重复性与临床效用。研究建议在未来的HRV研究中精简指标，避免冗余，并强调了频域指标在跨研究比较时的局限性。

Abstract: Heart Rate Variability (HRV) analysis is a key indicator of cardiac physiological state and aids in disease diagnosis. However, research on HRV parameters in healthy individuals remains limited, and no gold standard exists. This study evaluates HRV indices in 40 healthy adults (20 men, 20 women, aged 30-50) to improve HRV's clinical utility. Using computational methods for signal processing and data analysis, time, frequency, and nonlinear indices were analyzed to address five questions: (1) normality, (2) stability, (3) correlation, (4) reproducibility, and (5) consistency. Key findings: (1) Time-domain and nonlinear indices, particularly global and LF (low frequency), follow normal distributions, with gender differences noted. (2) Most indices are stable except HF (high frequency)-related ones. (3) High correlations in HF-related indices suggest redundancy, indicating only one is necessary in studies. (4) Comparisons with the Fantasia database revealed less than 10% error for most indices, except SD2 and SDNN in women (greater than 15%). (5) Time-domain and nonlinear indices show low inter-study variability, while frequency-domain indices exhibit high variability, limiting cross-study comparisons. The selected indices-ApEn and IRRR (global variability), HRVi and SD2 (LF), and MADRR or rMSSD (HF)-are best suited for accurately representing HRV components and enhancing its clinical and research relevance.

### [213] [The Capability Frontier: Benchmarks Miss 82% of Model Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26836)
*Bradley Fowler,Ryan Smith,Daniel Thi Graviet,William Myers,Joshua Greaves,Narmeen Fatimah Oozeer,Antía García,Philip Quirke,Amirali Abdullah,Fazl Barez,Shriyash Kaustubh Upadhyay*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 传统单一LLM评估方法低估了模型在实际异构任务中的能力。本研究通过引入“能力边界”方法，证明了利用多模型协同与采样筛选，能够在显著降低计算成本的同时，大幅提升系统整体的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基准测试通常仅报告单一模型单次运行的准确率，这种做法在处理异构数据分布时无法全面反映LLM的实际能力。不同模型在不同领域存在专长，且通过采样筛选可以获得性能提升，因此有必要构建一种更准确反映真实性能上限的评估框架。

Method: 研究团队引入了“能力边界”（Capability Frontier）概念，这是一种基于帕累托前沿的评估方法。该方法在给定成本约束下，通过在多个模型间进行最优选择（模拟Oracle路由）以及对多重采样结果进行筛选，从而对性能上限进行量化。此外，研究还利用受控概率模拟分析了查询主题熵与性能差距之间的关系。

Result: 与单模型评估相比，使用“能力边界”方法后，错误率降低了54%；若同时纠正单次运行的偏差，性能提升达82%。在保持SOTA准确率的同时，成本可降低85%。此外，研究发现查询主题的熵越高，多模型路由相对于单模型最优解的性能优势越明显。

Conclusion: 现有的基准测试低估了大语言模型在异构数据分布下的真实能力。通过采用“能力边界”评估方法，即利用模型间的互补性及多样本筛选，可以在大幅降低成本的前提下显著提升性能。未来的评估体系和部署策略应从单一模型评价转向多模型协同的视角。

Abstract: Existing benchmarks typically report accuracy for a single model on a single run. This systematically understates real-world LLM capabilities, particularly under heterogeneous data distributions: (i) different models get different questions correct according to their specializations, and (ii) given a budget, multiple generations can be sampled and selectively retained. To quantify this gap, we introduce the Capability Frontier: a Pareto frontier over a set of models that characterizes the best achievable performance at each cost level under optimal selection across models and generations (i.e., via an oracle). Our construction corrects for two opposing biases: underestimation from single-model evaluation and overestimation from taking maxima over noisy samples. We study 21 LLMs across 16 widely used benchmarks spanning coding, reasoning, medicine, factuality, instruction following, and agentic tasks, comparing Capability Frontier performance at matched cost to each benchmark's top-performing model. Correcting for single-model evaluation yields a 54% error rate reduction; additionally correcting for single runs yields an 82% improvement, with SOTA accuracy matched at 85% cost reduction. Complementing these empirical results, we use controlled probabilistic simulations to show that higher query topic entropy produces a near-monotonic increase in the performance gap between oracle routing and the best single model. Our findings suggest collective LLM capabilities are substantially underestimated, with implications for evaluation and deployment in data-heterogeneous, multi-domain settings.

</details>

*Janik Bischoff,Anne Meyer,Uta Mohring,Fabian Dunke,Maximilian Barlang,Özge Nur Subas,Hadi Kutabi,Stefan Nickel,Kai Furmans*

TL;DR: 针对仓储订单履行中决策解耦导致的算法选择难问题，本文提出了CASOP框架，通过模块化组件自动合成与评估针对特定环境的优化算法流水线，并在大规模测试中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本文提出的CASOP框架为仓储订单履行提供了一种系统化的方法，能够根据特定的仓储环境自动构建和评估算法流水线。该框架不仅弥补了现有研究在算法配置和组合方面的空白，还为研究人员和从业者提供了一种高效的决策支持工具，促进了仓储自动化与优化的发展。

Abstract: Order fulfillment in manual picker-to-goods warehouses involves interconnected decisions such as item assignment, order batching, and picker routing. While integrated models capture interactions between these decisions, practical warehouse systems often require decomposed approaches due to organizational boundaries, differing responsibilities, or limited data availability. Existing studies primarily evaluate algorithms for isolated subproblems or fixed subproblem combinations for specific warehouse settings, but lack a general mechanism to determine applicable algorithm configurations, compose them into valid solution pipelines, and assess their performance.
  With Context-Aware Synthesis of Optimization Pipelines (CASOP), we propose a framework for constructing and evaluating context-specific optimization pipelines and apply these to order fulfillment. The framework comprises: (1) a modular repository of algorithms for common order fulfillment problems; (2) semantic data and algorithm cards to describe warehouse context and algorithm requirements; (3) a taxonomy that structures order fulfillment problems into relevant subproblems; (4) a pipeline synthesizer that identifies applicable algorithms for a given warehouse context and composes all valid optimization pipelines; and (5) a pipeline evaluator that assesses all resulting pipelines. We demonstrate the framework on 7 benchmark instance sets covering four problem classes, resulting in 1,063,044 valid pipelines. The framework supports researchers and practitioners in designing, automatically synthesizing, and selecting valid, high-performing algorithmic pipelines for warehouse operations. The software is open-source and available at https://github.com/kit-dsm/ware_ops_pipes and https://github.com/kit-dsm/ware_ops_algos.
  Keywords: Warehouse optimization, Algorithm selection, Pipeline synthesis, Order fulfillment

Abstract: The interpretation phase of life cycle assessment often lacks structured mechanisms for translating quantified improvement opportunities addressing environmental hotspots into actionable strategic pathways under technological, social, and policy uncertainty. The approach presented can support more disciplined translation of impact results into strategic pathways and opens up new avenues for the use of advanced AI tools in LCA studies, particularly those focused on technologies that could be deployed at scale. This proof-of-concept demonstrates how AI-assisted, evidence-grounded interpretation can support implementation-oriented decision-making beyond conventional LCA studies.

### [216] [TAVR-VLM: Risk-Conditioned Causal Grounding for Hallucination-Resistant Report Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26874)
*Zhixiang Lu,Xiwei Liu,Sifan Song,Changkai Ji,Anh Nguyen,Jionglong Su,Imran Razzak,Jinfeng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对TAVR手术规划中多模态大模型的诊断幻觉问题，研究提出TAVR-VLM框架，通过引入因果接地注意力机制（R-CGA）实现视觉与文本的精确对应，在显著降低模型幻觉的同时提升了医疗决策的准确性与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大模型（MLLMs）在经导管主动脉瓣置换术（TAVR）规划中存在严重的诊断幻觉问题，缺乏必要的解剖学基础（grounding），难以满足高风险医疗场景下的安全性要求。

Method: 提出了TAVR-VLM框架，核心在于引入“风险条件因果接地注意力机制”（R-CGA）。该方法通过将多模态输入压缩为因果风险瓶颈，生成全局风险掩码，并在生成过程中实施支持投影的因果一致性目标，强制模型在特定解剖区域内进行文字生成，从而实现“风险→区域→词汇”的结构化接地。

Result: 在包含1,482名患者的M3TAVR数据集上，TAVR-VLM达到了0.896的AUROC指标，CIDEr评分提升至0.936，并将幻觉率显著降低至8.1%，确立了该领域的新技术先进水平（SOTA）。

Conclusion: TAVR-VLM通过R-CGA架构成功将因果推理引入多模态大模型，显著提升了TAVR手术规划中诊断结果的可解释性与可靠性，为高风险医疗场景下的AI应用提供了有效的幻觉抑制方案。

Abstract: Transcatheter Aortic Valve Replacement (TAVR) planning requires meticulous multimodal reasoning. However, adapting Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) to this high-stakes domain is severely impeded by diagnostic hallucinations, where generated text lacks anatomical grounding. To address this, TAVR-VLM is introduced: a novel framework featuring Risk-Conditioned Causal Grounding Attention (R-CGA) that instantiates a model-internal ``Risk $\rightarrow$ Region $\rightarrow$ Word'' structural grounding pathway. R-CGA compresses multimodal inputs into a causal risk bottleneck, purifying dense visual features into a global risk mask. During autoregressive generation, a support-projected causal consistency objective constrains token-level grounding within the risk-defined support mask. Evaluated on $\text{M}^3\text{TAVR}$, a comprehensive 1,482-patient cohort, TAVR-VLM establishes a new state-of-the-art. It achieves an AUROC of 0.896, boosts CIDEr to 0.936, and drastically reduces the hallucination rate to 8.1\%, thereby improving interpretability for evidence-based surgical AI.

### [217] [A Pipeline for Generating Longitudinal Synthetic Clinical Notes Using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26879)
*William Poulett*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对医疗数据隐私限制难题，本文提出了一种基于LLM的模块化流水线，用于生成具有纵向一致性和临床真实感的合成病历数据集，旨在推动临床AI工具的安全研发与评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗领域中临床数据因高度敏感性而难以获取，阻碍了临床AI系统的研发与评估。为了在规避患者隐私风险的同时支持AI研发，该工作旨在构建一种能够模拟真实医疗记录、具有纵向一致性且多样化的合成临床笔记数据集。

Method: 提出了一种模块化的合成临床笔记生成流水线。该方法整合了三个核心环节：1. 结构化患者信息生成；2. 半结构化患者病程模拟；3. 基于大语言模型（LLM）的非结构化临床笔记生成。此外，还引入了基于LLM的验证与增强机制，以确保生成内容的内部一致性、真实性及多样性。

Result: 成功构建并发布了一个包含70名合成患者的数据集，每名患者拥有20至50份涵盖完整住院过程的临床笔记。该数据集具备多层级的验证标准，能够满足从总结工具到决策支持系统等多种临床AI任务的研发与评估需求。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用大语言模型构建模块化流水线生成高质量合成临床笔记的可行性。这种方法能够在保护患者隐私的前提下，为医疗AI系统的开发、测试和评估提供有效的数据支持，从而缓解了临床数据获取受限的难题。

Abstract: Synthetic data is increasingly used to enable the development and evaluation of AI systems in domains where access to real-world data is restricted. In healthcare, clinical documentation presents particular challenges due to its sensitivity. This work introduces a synthetic clinical notes pipeline and dataset designed to support the development of clinical AI tools while avoiding the privacy risks associated with real patient data. The dataset is generated using a modular pipeline that combines structured patient generation, semi-structured patient journey simulation, and unstructured clinical note generation using large language models. The pipeline is designed to prioritise internal consistency across longitudinal patient records, while also capturing variation in writing style, note structure, and clinical detail. Additional mechanisms, including LLM-based validation and augmentation steps, are used to improve faithfulness, realism, and diversity of the generated notes. We release a dataset of 70 synthetic patients, each associated with 20-50 clinical notes spanning a full hospital journey. The dataset is provided at multiple levels of validation, enabling users to balance realism and scalability depending on their use case. This dataset supports the development, testing, and evaluation of clinical AI systems, including summarisation tools, coding models, and decision support systems, without reliance on real patient data.

</details>


### [218] [Generative Retrieval via Diffusion Transformer with Metric-Ordered Sequence Training and Hybrid-Policy Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26899)
*Chenghao Liu,Yu Zhang,Zhongtao Jiang,Kun Xu,Zhenwei An,Renzhi Wang,Zhao Wang,Jiachen Zhang,Yuxiao Zhang,Kun Xu,Songfang Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为MO-DiT+HPPO的生成式检索框架，旨在解决“模式保持属性检索”难题。通过度量排序预训练和参考锚点偏好优化，该模型能够在维持种子集特定模式的前提下，精准地检索出具有特定目标属性的物品。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际生产环境中，用户往往需要检索既符合细粒度模式（由种子集表达）又具备特定属性的物品。传统的基于嵌入的检索方法难以兼顾这两者：简单地对种子集取平均值虽能保持模式，但容易限制在低属性区域；而全局属性检索则会导致模型偏离原始模式。本文旨在形式化并解决这一“模式保持属性检索”问题。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为MO-DiT+HPPO的连续生成式检索框架。该方法包含以下关键技术：1. 度量排序持续预训练（Metric-ordered CPT）：将稀疏的在线标签转化为从低属性密度到高属性密度的有序轨迹，使模型学习跨领域的度量改进方向。2. HPPO（混合候选池参考锚点偏好优化）：通过标注混合候选池并应用参考锚点偏好优化，实现生成查询分布与在线目标的对齐。3. 帕累托对过滤（Pareto pair filter）：确保在提升属性度量的同时不降低模式纯度。

Result: 实验表明，MO-DiT+HPPO框架在四个属性域的物品和模式保留协议下均取得了优异表现。相比预训练的生成式检索器，该模型在八个领域划分中的七个实现了显著的属性交叉指标提升，并在最困难的划分中取得了相当的表现，验证了该方法的有效性和稳健性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的MO-DiT+HPPO框架有效地解决了模式保持与属性检索之间的矛盾。通过度量排序训练和参考锚点偏好优化，模型能够在不损失模式纯度的前提下显著提升目标属性的检索精度，为复杂的生产环境检索任务提供了一种稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: Embedding-based retrieval ranks items by their similarity to a query in a shared vector space and usually aims to return the highest-scoring items. In many production settings this is not what is wanted: given a seed set that expresses a fine-grained pattern, one needs more items that both satisfy a target attribute and stay within that pattern. We formalize this as pattern-preserving attribute retrieval. The two goals pull against each other: averaging the seeds preserves the pattern but stays in a low-attribute region, while global attribute retrieval drifts to unrelated patterns. We approach the task with continuous generative retrieval, where a model reads a sequence of item embeddings and generates query embeddings for nearest-neighbor search. We propose MO-DiT+HPPO, a staged framework with raw-sequence pretraining, multi-domain metric-ordered continuation pretraining, tail-centroid fine-tuning, and HPPO. Metric-ordered training turns sparse online retrieval labels into in-pattern trajectories ordered from low to high predicted attribute density, teaching one model the metric-improvement direction across domains. HPPO aligns the generated query distribution with the true online objective by labeling a hybrid candidate pool with the online intersection metric and applying reference-anchored preference optimization. A Pareto pair filter keeps only winner pairs that do not lower same-pattern purity, raising the attribute metric without sacrificing the pattern. Across four attribute domains under item- and pattern-holdout protocols, metric-ordered DiT improves the intersection metric over a pretrained generative retriever, and HPPO improves it further, with significant gains on seven of eight domain-split cells and a marginal tie on the hardest split. Metric-predictor validation, order ablations, CPT/SFT comparisons, and a candidate-policy ablation show where the gains come from.

</details>


### [219] [Learning to Recover Task Experts from a Multi-Task Merged Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26902)
*Jinwook Jung,Taegyu Kim,Kumju Jo,Sungyong Baik*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ReTeX 是一种新型多任务模型合并框架，它将模型合并带来的干扰建模为可补偿的参数偏移，仅需单一合并检查点即可高精度恢复多任务性能，并支持对未知任务的自适应处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多任务模型合并方法存在权衡难题：静态合并虽然轻量但会导致严重的参数干扰；动态合并虽然效果好但通常需要存储和加载冗余的专家组件，推理成本昂贵。本文旨在寻找一种仅通过单一合并模型即可恢复各任务专家性能的高效方法。

Method: 1. 参数建模：将合并过程中的参数干扰建模为仿射变换，并将其近似为可预测的加性偏移量（Additive Offsets）；
2. 框架设计：提出了 ReTeX 框架，通过预测这些偏移量来从单一合并检查点中“恢复”任务专家性能；
3. 无需路由的识别：利用 SVD 子空间签名（Subspace Signatures）进行任务识别，根据输入在子空间的投影残差选择最优专家，无需额外训练大型路由网络。

Result: 在视觉和 NLP 领域中，ReTeX 能够恢复超过 95% 的原始任务专家性能；显著提升了模型对未知任务的泛化能力，并能通过自适应内插专家知识有效处理分布外（OOD）任务。

Conclusion: ReTeX 证明了通过预测参数偏移量来消除模型合并中的干扰是可行的。该方法不仅能高效恢复单个任务专家的性能，还展现了对未知分布（OOD）任务的自适应知识内插能力，为轻量化、高性能的多任务模型合并提供了一个有效范式。

Abstract: Multi-task model merging aims to consolidate several task-specific experts into a unified model, yet static merging consistently suffers from parameter interference. While dynamic merging models aim to bridge this gap, many works rely on the costly storage and loading of redundant expert components at inference. In this work, from the perspective of task expert, we view parameter interference as parameter perturbation introduced to each expert during merging process. We show that such parameter perturbations can be modeled as affine transformation, which can be approximated as additive offsets. Motivated by these, we propose Recover Task eXpert (ReTeX), a framework that predicts those offsets, in order to undo parameter interference and recover task-expert performance from a single merged checkpoint. To recover the appropriate expert when task identity is unknown, we introduce a router-free task identifier based on SVD subspace signatures computed offline before inference. At inference, the identifier selects the task whose subspace yields the smallest projection residual for a given input. As a result, ReTeX recovers over 95% of individual-expert performance in both vision and NLP domains, while significantly improving generalization to unseen tasks. Crucially, we also show that the parameter offset prediction leads to emergent adaptive interpolation of expert knowledge for out-of-distribution (OOD) tasks. ReTeX adaptively interpolates seen expert knowledge to handle unseen tasks. Our code is available at https://github.com/BAIKLAB/ReTeX

</details>


### [220] [Diagnosing Task Insensitivity in Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26918)
*Jingyu Liu,Xiaopeng Wu,Kehan Chen,Chuan Yu,Yong Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大型语言模型作为智能体时存在“任务不敏感”问题，即倾向于执行旧任务的动作而非理解新指令。为此，作者提出了任务扰动对比正则化方法，通过增强模型对指令的依赖，显著提升了模型在分布外任务中的泛化表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型作为长序列智能体时，在面对分布外（OOD）任务时表现出明显的泛化能力不足。核心原因在于模型存在“任务不敏感”问题：即模型倾向于应用训练中习得的模式，即使面对语义已改变的指令，仍会机械地执行与原任务相关的动作，这源于优化过程中对局部观测的“捷径偏差”。

Method: 研究人员分析了模型注意力机制的漂移现象，发现模型倾向于忽略任务指令而过度依赖局部观测（捷径偏差）。基于此，作者提出了一种轻量级的对比正则化方法——任务扰动NLL优化（Task-Perturbed NLL Optimization），通过明确强制模型输出与当前任务指令强相关的动作，来纠正模型对任务的“不敏感”问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，该干预措施有效地改善了模型对任务指令的感知能力，纠正了注意力向局部观测漂移的问题。与基准模型相比，经过任务扰动优化后的模型在面对分布外任务时表现出更强的泛化性能和更稳定的决策表现。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种名为“任务扰动负对数似然优化”（Task-Perturbed NLL Optimization）的方法。通过引入对比正则化机制，该方法成功提升了语言模型代理对任务指令的敏感度，减少了对局部观测的过度依赖，从而显著增强了模型在分布外（OOD）环境下的泛化能力和任务执行的稳定性。

Abstract: Large language models can serve as capable long-horizon agents, but their out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization remains weak. We identify a key source of this failure as task insensitivity: when faced with similar but distinct tasks, models might apply patterns learned during training and fail to solve the task at hand. We show that models often continue with actions aligned with the original task even when the instruction is semantically corrupted and cannot be directly answered. We further find that, when we replace the task description in a trained prompt with another similar but distinct task, the model may still output the same action. This behavior is accompanied by a consistent training-time attention drift away from task tokens and toward local observations, suggesting an optimization bias toward shortcuts. To mitigate this problem, we propose Task-Perturbed NLL Optimization, a lightweight contrastive regularizer that explicitly encourages action dependence on the task instruction. Extensive evaluations show that our intervention improves task sensitivity and OOD generalization while preserving more stable attention to task tokens.

</details>


### [221] [Where Do CoT Training Gains Land in LLM based Agents?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26935)
*Jingyu Liu,Zhiwen Wang,Yuxin Jing,Huanyu Zhou,Yong Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了思维链（CoT）训练在语言模型中的本质：它主要提升了模型直接预测动作的能力，而非通过推理修正决策的能力。因此，作者提出通过选择性遮蔽动作标签来减少模型对特定预测的过拟合，从而提升泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明语言模型的思维链（CoT）推理往往缺乏忠实度，可能属于事后推理（post-hoc reasoning）。作者试图探究CoT训练的核心贡献：模型究竟是学会了通过推理改变决策，还是仅仅提高了基于提示词直接预测动作的能力。

Method: 通过对比“提示词动作”（直接预测）与“思维链动作”（基于推理的预测）在不同训练检查点（checkpoints）的质量表现，评估CoT训练的实际作用。进一步分析模型在交互过程中对思维链的依赖程度变化，并提出通过选择性遮蔽部分训练样本中的动作标记（action-token）来进行干预，以验证模型泛化性能。

Result: 研究发现，随着训练进行，“提示词动作”质量显著提升；而“思维链动作”相比“提示词动作”的相对优势并未随训练增加，这表明CoT训练并没有显著增强推理对决策的驱动作用。此外，模型在后期检查点更少根据思维链内容修改决策，显示出更强的直接预测倾向。实验证明，对动作标签进行选择性遮蔽可以显著提高模型的域外泛化表现。

Conclusion: 思维链（CoT）训练主要提升了模型在无需推理情况下的直接预测能力（prompt actions），而非增强了推理对决策的修正作用。研究发现随着训练深入，模型对提示词的依赖度反而增加，对思维链的修正依赖减弱。通过对部分样本屏蔽动作标签的训练干预，可以有效提升模型的域外泛化能力。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning is widely used in language-model agents, but prior work has shown that verbalized CoT is not always faithful and may instead reflect post-hoc reasoning, which means the model already knows the answer before reasoning. We therefore ask what CoT training is actually improving: is the model getting better at changing its action through generated reasoning, or is it getting better at predicting the action directly from the prompt? We study this question by comparing \emph{prompt actions} (predicting action without CoT) with CoT actions (predicting action with CoT). Across checkpoints, prompt-action quality improves substantially. While interacting with the environment, the relative advantage of CoT actions over prompt actions remains similar, showing that CoT training does not widen the advantage of CoT reasoning, and it helps to improve the quality of prompt actions. We further find that later checkpoints are less likely to revise the action in response to CoT, suggesting greater reliance on the prompt. Motivated by these patterns, we selectively mask action-token supervision on a fraction of training examples. This intervention improves out-of-domain generalization.

</details>


### [222] [Look-Before-Move: Narrative-Grounded World Visual Attention in Dynamic 3D Story Worlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26964)
*Jiaming Bian,Bingliang Li,Yuehao Wu,Pichao Wang,Zhi Wang,Hailan Ma,Huadong Mo,Zhenhong Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Look-Before-Move框架，通过将视觉观察规划与相机运动执行解耦，使具身智能能够在动态3D环境中根据叙事意图主动决定观察内容，从而实现更具叙事感和连贯性的自主相机运动规划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具身智能和世界模型领域，现有的视觉感知多局限于被动解释观测结果。本文旨在解决如何在动态3D场景中通过主动规划相机视角（即决定观察什么、如何构图以及如何随叙事意图转移注意力），从而实现更高效、更符合叙事的自主视觉获取。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Look-Before-Move”的相机规划框架，包含三个核心步骤：1. 构建语义观察契约（Semantic Observation Contract），将导演意图转化为可执行的视觉约束；2. 执行蒙特卡洛视点搜索（Monte Carlo Viewpoint Search），以寻找符合叙事且几何上可行的视角；3. 应用语义轨迹定位（Semantic Trajectory Grounding），将选定视点连接成连续、避障且时间上连贯的相机运动。

Result: 实验结果表明，与代表性基线相比，该框架在主体感知、意图一致性和轨迹质量方面均有显著提升。此外，作者还构建了一个包含50个故事、457个场景和1585个镜头的动态3D故事世界基准（Story World Benchmark）。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了在生成相机运动前先组织视觉注意力对于提升具身智能在动态3D环境中的感知能力、叙事一致性和运动轨迹质量至关重要。Look-Before-Move框架为解决复杂的具身视觉规划问题提供了一种有效的新范式。

Abstract: As embodied AI and world models increasingly operate in dynamic 3D environments, visual perception must move beyond passively interpreting given observations toward actively deciding what to observe. We study this problem through camera planning in dynamic 3D story worlds, where the camera must not only generate smooth motion, but also decide what visual evidence should be acquired before it moves. We formulate this capability as Narrative-Grounded World Visual Attention, where the camera acts as an embodied observer that determines what to observe, how to compose the observation, and how to shift attention over time under narrative intent and physical 3D constraints. To realize this capability, we propose Look-Before-Move, a camera planning framework that separates observation specification from motion execution. It first builds a Semantic Observation Contract to convert directorial intent into executable visual constraints, then performs Monte Carlo Viewpoint Search to find narrative-compliant and geometrically feasible viewpoints, and finally applies Semantic Trajectory Grounding to connect selected viewpoints into continuous, collision-aware, and temporally coherent camera motion. We further construct a dynamic 3D Story World Benchmark based on StoryBlender, covering 50 stories, 457 scenes, and 1585 shots with animated characters, semantic scene configurations, and executable 3D environments. Experiments show that our framework improves subject perception, intent consistency, and trajectory quality over representative baselines, demonstrating the importance of organizing visual attention before generating camera motion.

</details>


### [223] [Einstein World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26969)
*Munachiso Samuel Nwadike,Zangir Iklassov,Ali Mekky,Zayd M. Kawakibi Zuhri,Kentaro Inui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出“爱因斯坦世界模型（EWM）”，通过允许LLM在推理过程中调用视觉模拟来生成可审查的假设，从而增强模型在处理反事实推理和复杂思想实验时的逻辑能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出“爱因斯坦世界模型（EWM）”架构，将“视觉-时间演进（visual-temporal rollouts）”直接嵌入推理路径中。模型通过调用专用的世界模块（world-module）对特定场景进行短期的视觉模拟，生成的输出被视为可审查的假设（inspectable hypothesis），进而辅助大模型进行后续逻辑推理。

Result: EWM成功将大模型的工具调用能力扩展至“视觉思想实验”领域。实验表明，通过在推理链中引入可检查的视觉滚动输出，模型能够更好地处理需要空间、时间和逻辑模拟的任务，从而突破纯文本推理的局限性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种将视觉想象引入大模型推理流程的新范式，表明通过辅助视觉环境模拟（World-module），大模型能够有效处理超出纯文本能力的复杂推理任务，为增强LLM的认知与规划能力提供了新思路。

Abstract: Does intelligence require the ability to reason about phenomena beyond direct experience? It is natural to suspect that some complex thought cannot be captured through language alone. However, of particular concern to this work, is whether visualising counterfactual events can complement language as a mechanism for complex thought. We ask whether LLMs can be trained to utilise such visualisation mechanisms, in a way that benefits their reasoning abilities. Motivated by this question, we propose Einstein World Models. EWMs are a blueprint for LLM-based reasoning systems that place visual-temporal rollouts inside the reasoning trace, allowing them to reason in ways that text alone may not support well. In an EWM, the LLM calls a world-module (not to be confused with a world model), to produce short rollouts of scenes under consideration. The returned rollout is treated not as the answer, but as an inspectable hypothesis that can support later reasoning. Einstein World Models extend the capability of LLMs for tool calling (such as web search or code execution), into the domain of visual thought experiments.

### [224] [Adaptive Utility driven Resource Orchestration for Resilient AI (AURORA-AI)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27005)
*Rahul Umesh Mhapsekar,Ilias Cherkaoui,Lizy Abraham,Indrakshi Dey*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对AI系统在非平稳环境下的性能衰退问题，本文提出了 AURORA-AI 框架，通过融合控制理论与公平感知效用最大化策略，实现了对资源的高效、动态编排，显著提升了系统的韧性与公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代AI系统常部署于计算、人口统计和操作条件不断变化的非平稳环境中，传统的静态资源分配策略会导致模型预测性能下降，并损害公平性和可解释性等以人为本的属性。

Method: 提出 AURORA-AI 框架，该框架集成了哈密顿-雅可比-贝尔曼（HJB）反馈控制、基于李雅普诺夫（Lyapunov）的稳定性监测以及公平感知复合效用函数，构建了一个闭环策略，用于在非平稳环境下动态重新分配异构AI模型的计算资源。

Result: 在包含人口偏差冲击、概念漂移和极端突发事件的模拟测试中，AURORA-AI 表现优异：相较于静态基准和 PPO 算法，其在黑天鹅事件后的恢复速度最快；显著提升了 Alpha 分位数和超分位数性能（分别提升 29% 和 25%）；有效降低了人口统计均等差距，并增加了李雅普诺夫稳定运行步骤的比例。

Conclusion: 基于稳定性理论的公平感知自适应编排是一种实用且具有理论支撑的方法，能够有效促进韧性、以人为本的AI部署。

Abstract: Modern AI systems are increasingly deployed under non-stationary computational, demographic, and operational conditions in which static resource allocation strategies degrade both predictive performance and human-centric properties such as fairness and explainability. This paper presents AURORA-AI, an Adaptive Utility-driven Resource Orchestration framework for Resilient AI that unifies Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman feedback control, Lyapunov-based stability monitoring, and a fairness-aware composite utility into a single closed-loop policy.The framework continuously redistributes computational budget across a population of heterogeneous AI models so that the global utility, defined jointly over predictive performance, demographic parity, cost, latency, robustness, and interpretability, remains maximised under disruption. The framework is evaluated in a stress-rich discrete-time simulation that concurrently injects demographic bias shocks, gradual concept drift, and abrupt black-swan disruptions, and is compared against five established controllers including Static, Round Robin, Greedy, LinUCB, and a deep reinforcement-learning agent based on Proximal Policy Optimisation. AURORA-AI achieves immediate recovery from the black-swan event compared to eighty-eight time steps for the Static baseline and twenty-two for Proximal Policy Optimisation, lifts the alpha-quantile and the super-quantile by twenty-nine and twenty-five percent respectively, simultaneously reduces the mean and maximum demographic parity gap, and increases the fraction of Lyapunov-stable operating steps. These results indicate that fairness-aware adaptive orchestration grounded in stability theory is a practical and theoretically motivated path toward resilient human-centric AI deployment.

</details>


### [225] [Semantic Early-Stopping for Iterative LLM Agent Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27009)
*Sahil Shrivastava*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于语义嵌入相似度的多智能体LLM循环早停机制，在无需牺牲回答质量的前提下，通过减少冗余迭代显著降低了token消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体LLM循环（如写作者-评论者模式）通常依赖固定的迭代上限（max_iterations）来终止，这种方法不仅在简单任务上浪费计算资源，在复杂任务上也容易导致截断，缺乏根据任务进度动态调整的能力。因此，研究旨在提出一种具备语义感知能力的早停机制。

Method: 1. 提出基于嵌入相似度（余弦距离）和质量评估的语义早停机制。
2. 建立确定性终止的理论框架，并通过机器验证其合理性。
3. 设计了一种“审判者高效”（judge-efficient）评估协议，通过缓存轨迹和解耦操作/评估token，实现低成本的公平对比。
4. 在HotpotQA数据集上进行多跳检索增强问答的实证研究。

Result: 1. 语义早停机制在HotpotQA测试集上将操作token成本降低了38%，且保持了与固定迭代法相当的回答质量。
2. 证明了单纯依赖质量门控（quality-gated）的方法由于评估开销过大而不可行。
3. 实验发现“预言机”（Oracle）选择最佳轮次的方法显著优于现有所有策略，表明核心挑战已从“何时停止”转变为“如何挑选最佳回答”。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，简单的语义停止准则（基于嵌入距离）在维持性能的同时能显著降低多智能体LLM系统的计算成本。然而，研究也指出，目前的评估范式（何时停止）已逐渐触及瓶颈，未来的挑战在于如何更高效地从已生成的序列中自动选出“最佳回答”。

Abstract: Multi-agent large language model (LLM) loops, for example a Writer that drafts and a Critic that revises, are almost always terminated by a fixed iteration cap (max_iterations). This is a syntactic kill-switch: it is blind to whether the answer is still improving, so it over-spends tokens on easy inputs and truncates hard ones. We study semantic early-stopping: the loop halts when consecutive draft embeddings stop changing in meaning (cosine distance with a patience window) and the answer's measured quality stops improving. Our work makes three contributions. First, an honest theoretical footing: we prove deterministic termination and well-definedness and machine-check these claims, while treating the convergence of the distance sequence as an empirically tested conjecture rather than a (previously over-claimed) Banach contraction. Second, a judge-efficient evaluation protocol: we generate each question's full trajectory once, replay every stopping policy over the identical drafts, and cache every LLM-judge call, yielding a strictly paired efficiency-versus-quality comparison at low cost; we further separate operational tokens (charged to a policy) from evaluation tokens (a measurement instrument). Third, an empirical study on multi-hop retrieval-augmented question answering (HotpotQA). On the 60-question test split, a judge-free semantic stopper reduces operational tokens by 38% relative to max_iterations at parity quality (Delta-IS = -0.004, p = 0.81), whereas the full quality-gated variant is counter-productive because its per-round judging dominates cost. An oracle that selects the best round attains +0.115 Information Score over every practical policy (p ~ 4e-11), reframing the problem from "when to stop" (easy) to "which round is best" (open).

</details>


### [226] [How to evaluate clustering with ground truth?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27061)
*Pasi Fränti*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文梳理了聚类外部评价指标，针对不同评估需求（质心级、逐点级、点对点等）推荐了CI、PSI及ACC等指标，旨在帮助研究者更科学地评估聚类效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有基准真值（Ground Truth）的聚类任务中，缺乏对各类外部有效性指标的系统梳理与评估准则，导致研究者在指标选择上存在困惑。

Method: 通过系统综述常见外部有效性指标，重点对比分析了基于集合匹配的评估方法，并针对不同应用场景（聚类级与逐点级）提出了针对性的评价指标建议。

Result: 研究明确了不同评估指标的适用边界：CI指标具有高可解释性；PSI指标解决了聚类规模差异带来的偏见；ACC等指标适用于点对点权重一致的评估需求。

Conclusion: 本文建议在聚类评估中，若追求直观且可解释的聚类级指标，应优先选择质心指标（CI）；若需精细的逐点评估，PSI指标在处理聚类规模偏差方面更具优势，而ACC等指标则适用于要求所有数据点权重均等的场景。

Abstract: External indexes can be used for cluster evaluation when ground truth is available. We review the most common external validity indexes focusing on set-matching-based measures. We recommend centroid index (CI), because it is an intuitive cluster-level measure with an explainable result. If we need a more fine-tuned, point-level measure, there are more choices. Pair-set index (PSI) provides a normalized score which is not biased by cluster sizes. If all points should matter equally, then clustering accuracy (ACC) or any other set-matching measure is suitable.

</details>


### [227] [Joint Learning of Experiential Rules and Policies for Large Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27136)
*Shicheng Ye,Chao Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了JERP框架，通过将交互经验同时转化为辅助决策的提示规则和模型更新的依据，实现了LLM智能体经验利用与策略演进的深度融合，显著提升了其在复杂环境下的任务完成能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在处理多步交互任务时，将经验作为外部自然语言规则存储与通过参数更新优化策略这两种方式存在局限性：前者难以与策略演进同步，后者在稀疏奖励环境下对局部错误的纠正能力有限。为此，研究旨在结合这两者的优势，实现经验规则与策略的协同演进。

Method: 提出了JERP（Joint Learning of Experiential Rules and Policies）框架。该方法在交互过程中维护一个长期经验规则库，并在决策时检索相关规则作为上下文提示；在单次交互结束后，利用轨迹数据同时进行策略优化和规则库修订，通过对比当前轨迹与成功参考轨迹来实现规则的更新。

Result: 在AlfWorld和WebShop任务上的实验表明，JERP框架能有效提升LLM智能体在复杂交互任务中的决策性能，证明了该方法在利用交互经验方面的优越性。

Conclusion: JERP框架通过联合学习经验规则与策略，成功解决了多步交互环境中经验利用的割裂问题，证明了规则库与模型参数同步演进对于提升智能体决策性能的关键作用。

Abstract: For LLM agents in multi-step interactive environments, a key challenge is to make effective use of accumulated interaction experience. Existing work has typically separated two uses of such experience: keeping it outside the model as natural-language rules for later prompting, or using trajectories and feedback to update the model parameters. The former is easy to interpret but can fall out of sync with the evolving policy; the latter improves the policy more broadly but provides only limited correction for local mistakes in sparse-reward settings. We present Joint Learning of Experiential Rules and Policies for LLM Agents (JERP), which updates a long-term experiential-rule pool and the policy from the same interaction trajectories. At decision time, JERP retrieves task-relevant rules and conditions the agent on them together with the interaction history. After each episode, it uses the collected trajectories both to optimize the policy and to revise the rule pool by comparing current rollouts with reference successful trajectories. This coupling keeps the rule pool aligned with the evolving policy while allowing stable and effective behaviors to be gradually absorbed into the model itself. Experiments on AlfWorld and WebShop show that JERP yields consistent gains in decision performance for complex interactive tasks.

</details>


### [228] [OpenRCA 2.0: From Outcome Labels to Causal Process Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27154)
*Aoyang Fang,Yifan Yang,Jin'ao Shang,Qisheng Lu,Junjielung Xu,Rui Wang,Songhan Zhang,Yuzhong Zhang,Boxi Yu,Pinjia He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出了现有根因分析评估的局限性，并提出了带有因果路径标注的OpenRCA 2.0基准。研究表明，当前大模型虽能勉强识别根因，但在严谨的因果链推理逻辑上仍存在显著缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有根因分析（RCA）数据集仅标注根因本身，忽略了从根因到故障现象的传播路径，导致LLM任务退化为简单的模式匹配，无法准确评估其深层推理能力。

Method: 提出了PAVE（一种基于故障注入的逐步标记协议），通过“前向验证”机制（从原因到结果的逻辑推理）而非传统的反向推导，构建了OpenRCA 2.0基准数据集，包含500个带有因果传播路径标注的跨系统实例。

Result: 在对11个前沿大模型进行测试后发现，仅有20.7%的模型能准确识别根因。研究还发现，虽然76.0%的模型能识别出部分根因服务，但仅有61.5%能通过合乎逻辑的因果路径将其与现象关联，证明了现有仅关注结果的评估方式无法发现智能体的逻辑“幻觉”。

Conclusion: 传统的仅关注结果的评估方法掩盖了LLM在根因分析中的逻辑缺陷。引入基于因果传播路径的评估对于构建可信的LLM智能体至关重要，能够揭示智能体在因果链条推理上的深层不足。

Abstract: Root cause analysis (RCA) poses a holistic test of LLM agentic capabilities, such as long-context understanding, multi-step reasoning, and tool use. However, existing datasets suffer from a fundamental gap: they label only the root cause, not the propagation path connecting it to the observed symptom, which largely simplifies the task to naive pattern matching. To support rigorous evaluation, we introduce PAVE, a step-wise labeling protocol that leverages known interventions from fault injection to reconstruct causal propagation paths. The mechanism is forward verification: reasoning from cause to effect rather than inferring backward from symptoms. Applying PAVE yields OpenRCA 2.0 (500 instances), the first cross-system RCA benchmark with step-wise causal annotations for LLM agents. Across 11 frontier LLMs, recovering the exact root-cause set succeeds in only 20.7% of cases on average. To locate where this difficulty lies, we relax the criterion and find what we call the ungrounded diagnosis: agents identify at least one correct root-cause service in 76.0% of cases, but ground that service in a verified causal propagation path to the observed symptom in only 61.5%. Outcome-only evaluation hides this failure mode; step-wise causal ground truth is the missing piece for trustworthy LLM-based RCA agents.

### [229] [TOPS: First-Principles Visual Token Pruning via Constructing Token Optimal Preservation Sets for Efficient MLLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27161)
*Tinghao Wang,Yichen Guo,Rui Huang,Zheng Lu,Qizhe Zhang,Chenxi Li,Yuan Zhang,Jiajun Cao,Zhirong Shen,Yaosong Du,Guangyan Gan,Wenya Wang,Lin William Cong,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对多模态大模型（MLLM）计算开销过大的问题，本文提出了一种名为TOPS的视觉标记剪枝方法。通过信息论定义任务相关性、信息覆盖和语义多样性三大原则，实现了在大幅降低标记数量的同时保持模型性能，甚至在部分情况下减轻了幻觉问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM在处理视觉任务时，因视觉标记数量过多导致计算开销巨大。现有的剪枝方法存在缺陷：基于注意力机制的方法容易保留冗余标记，基于多样性的方法往往忽略用户指令，且缺乏统一的理论指导。因此，作者旨在从第一性原理出发，为视觉标记剪枝构建一个科学的理论框架。

Method: 研究从第一性原理出发，利用信息论分析推导出有效的标记选择需遵循的三大核心原则：任务相关性（Task Relevance）、信息覆盖率（Information Coverage）和语义多样性（Semantic Diversity）。基于此，作者提出了一个无需训练且模型无关的剪枝模块TOPS。该模块通过综合考量这三个原则，在不依赖额外训练的情况下，动态筛选出最关键的视觉标记。

Result: 在7种主流MLLM骨干网络和14个基准测试上的实验表明，TOPS在各种剪枝设置下均优于现有方法。特别是在LLaVA-NeXT模型上，TOPS在剔除77.8%视觉标记的情况下，7B和13B模型的性能分别保持在100%和100.6%，有效证明了该方法在压缩模型规模同时兼顾性能表现的优越性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过构建“标记最优保留集”（TOPS）框架，证实了基于信息论原理的视觉标记剪枝能够有效剔除冗余信息。实验结果表明，该方法不仅能显著提升MLLM的推理效率，还能在压缩模型的同时保持甚至提升性能（如减少幻觉现象），为轻量化多模态大模型的研发提供了新范式。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have achieved strong multimodal reasoning capabilities, but their efficiency is limited by the large number of visual tokens, which introduces substantial computational overhead. Visual token pruning offers a natural solution, yet existing methods are imperfect: attention-based criteria tend to retain redundant tokens, while diversity-based criteria are often agnostic to user instructions. Even methods that combine multiple criteria still lack a principled formulation of the intrinsic objective of token pruning. In this paper, we revisit visual token pruning from a first-principles perspective and formulate it as constructing Token Optimal Preservation Sets. Through a top-down information-theoretic analysis, we identify three fundamental principles for effective token selection: Task Relevance, Information Coverage, and Semantic Diversity. Based on these principles, we propose TOPS, a training-free and model-agnostic pruning module that can be applied to various MLLMs. Extensive experiments on 7 MLLM backbones and 14 benchmarks demonstrate that TOPS outperforms prior methods under diverse pruning settings. Notably, on LLaVA-NeXT, TOPS removes 77.8% of visual tokens while preserving 100.0% and 100.6% performance on its 7B and 13B models, respectively, suggesting that pruning redundant visual tokens can sometimes mitigate hallucination and inspire future lightweight MLLM design.

</details>


### [230] [A Process Harness for Uplifting Legacy Workflows to Agentic BPM: Design and Realization in CUGA FLO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27188)
*Fabiana Fournier,Lior Limonad*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“流程线束”（Process Harness）机制，通过TDF模型在传统确定性工作流引擎之上叠加智能体层，从而在保持业务合规性的前提下，赋予流程推理、自适应及 oversight 等智能化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 引入“流程线束”（Process Harness）概念，在不替换底层引擎的前提下，在工作流周围构建受策略控制的智能体层；2. 开发“任务-决策-流程”（TDF）模型，定义数据模式及执行语义；3. 设计三种智能体（TaskAgent、DecisionAgent、FlowAgent）及基于FRAME策略的治理机制；4. 实现原型系统CUGA FLO并在贷款审批工作流中进行验证。

Abstract: We introduce the process harness, a new mechanism for uplifting legacy workflows into Agentic Business Process Management (Agentic BPM) without replacing the underlying workflow engine. A process harness places a policy-governed agentic layer around a deterministic workflow engine, intercepting designated control points to contribute reasoning, adaptation, and oversight while the engine retains structural authority over the process. To define the process harness rigorously, we develop the Task-Decision-Flow (TDF) model, specifying both its data schema and its execution semantics. TDF decomposes LLM reasoning across three policy-governed agent types: a TaskAgent for knowledge-intensive task execution, a DecisionAgent for per-case gateway routing, and a FlowAgent that governs runtime flow adaptation through a principled hook mechanism. Each agent reasons within an explicit policy drawn from the process FRAME, the aggregate policy set governing all LLM calls in the system. We then present CUGA FLO as the design and implementation realization of the TDF model, and demonstrate it on a loan approval workflow that exercises all three agent types and hook-driven regulatory override. The process harness uniquely reconciles imperative requirements, realized through deterministic workflow execution that enforces structural compliance, with normative requirements, realized through policy-framed agentic autonomy invoked at designated control points wherever the process demands it.

### [231] [Vulnerability of Natural Language Classifiers to Evolutionary Generated Adversarial Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27215)
*Manjinder Singh,Alexander E. I. Brownlee,Mohamed Elawady*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 GAversary 的新型黑盒对抗攻击方法，通过结合遗传算法与 GloVe 词向量，显著提升了针对自然语言处理（NLP）模型的攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习模型（尤其是 NLP 模型）对对抗性输入具有脆弱性，而现有的许多攻击方法依赖于对模型内部结构的了解或在攻击效果上存在局限，研究者旨在开发一种更高效、具备通用性的黑盒攻击框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GAversary 的混合遗传算法。该方法将目标模型视为黑盒，仅利用模型输出的逻辑值（logit）作为引导；在变异操作中，利用 GloVe 词向量进行词替换推荐，以增强对抗样本的语义相似性。

Result: GAversary 在多个基准数据集上的测试表现优于 BAE 和 A2T 方法。在最佳测试案例中，将目标模型准确率从 76.8% 降至 5.8%（相比 BAE 的 27.6% 具有显著优势）；尽管在扰动词数、语义相似度和运行时间上较对比方法有所牺牲，但其攻击成功率明显提升。

Conclusion: GAversary 是一种高效的黑盒对抗攻击方法，通过引入基于 GloVe 的遗传算法，能够显著降低 NLP 模型的预测准确率，虽然在扰动词数和语义相似度上存在一定权衡，但其攻击强度远超现有主流基准方法。

Abstract: Deep learning models have achieved impressive performance across various fields but remain vulnerable to adversarial inputs, particularly in NLP, where such attacks can have significant real-world consequences. Adversarial attacks often involve small, semantically similar token replacements to fool NLP models, and recent methods have become more precise by targeting specific vulnerable words, often by exploiting some level of access to the model's internal structure. This paper proposes GAversary, a hybrid Genetic Algorithm (GA) to generate adversarial attacks on natural language models. The GA is able to treat the target model as a black box, requiring only the logit value output by the model to guide the search. GAversary differs from GAs previously proposed for this problem by using GloVe embeddings to propose word replacements (the mutation operator) to improve the semantic similarity of the adversarial examples. GAversary is applied to several benchmark data sets and well-known target models. GAversary is able to substantially reduce the target model's accuracy on test data compared to the BAE and A2T attacks compared against (in the best case, reducing a 76.8% accuracy to 5.8%, compared to BAE's 27.6%). The trade-off is that GAversary perturbs just under twice as many words as the other two methods, with a slightly lower semantic similarity to the original text and around a 5% increase in run-time.

</details>


### [232] [Ask, Don't Judge: Binary Questions for Interpretable LLM Evaluation and Self-Improvement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27226)
*Sangwoo Cho,Kushal Chawla,Pengshan Cai,Zefang Liu,Chenyang Zhu,Shi-Xiong Zhang,Sambit Sahu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BINEVAL 是一种新型的、免训练的大模型评估框架，它通过将评估任务分解为可解释的二元判定问题，解决了传统评估方法透明度低和难以诊断的痛点，在提升评估准确性的同时，为提示词的改进提供了直接的诊断依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型评估方法存在瓶颈：人工评估成本高且缓慢；基于词汇的度量指标与人类评价相关性差；整体式（holistic）大模型评审员给出的评分往往缺乏透明度且难以调试。因此，需要一种既精确又具有可解释性的评估框架。

Method: 提出了 BINEVAL 框架：利用元提示词（meta-prompt）将评估标准拆解为细粒度的原子级二元问题（Binary Questions）；由大模型独立回答这些问题；通过聚合这些回答得出具有解释性的多维度评分，并据此进行反馈。

Result: 在 SummEval、Topical-Chat 和 QAGS 等基准测试中，BINEVAL 的表现优于 UniEval 和 G-Eval；在事实一致性方面效果显著；不仅与人类评价的相关性更高，还能更好匹配人类评分分布，避免了传统大模型评审的“天花板效应”，并支持提示词的迭代优化。

Conclusion: BINEVAL 框架证明了通过将复杂评估任务分解为原子级的二元判定，能够有效解决大模型评估中透明度不足和诊断困难的问题。该方法不仅在评估性能上与现有基准持平或超越，还为大模型的迭代优化提供了可解释的反馈机制。

Abstract: Evaluating LLM outputs remains a major bottleneck in NLP: human evaluation is expensive and slow, lexical metrics correlate poorly with human judgments on open-ended generation, and holistic LLM judges often produce opaque scores that are hard to debug. We propose BINEVAL, a framework that decomposes evaluation criteria into atomic binary questions and aggregates the resulting verdicts into interpretable, multi-dimensional scores. Given a task prompt, a meta-prompt generates fine-grained evaluation questions, and an LLM answers them independently for each output, yielding transparent question-level feedback together with calibrated overall scores. This decomposition makes evaluation easier to inspect, easier to diagnose, and directly usable for prompt improvement. Across SummEval, Topical-Chat, and QAGS, BINEVAL matches or outperforms strong baselines including UniEval and G-Eval, with especially strong results on factual consistency benchmarks such as QAGS. Beyond competitive correlation with human judgments, BINEVAL better matches human score distributions and avoids the ceiling effects common in prior LLM judges, leading to better discrimination between borderline and clearly flawed outputs. We further show that the same question-level feedback supports iterative prompt optimization, improving evaluator prompts on summarization and generation prompts on IFBench under both self-update and cross-model update settings. Overall, BINEVAL provides a task-agnostic, training-free, and interpretable evaluation framework that combines strong empirical performance with practical diagnostic and optimization value.

</details>


### [233] [EO-WM: A Physically Informed World Model for Probabilistic Earth Observation Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27277)
*Junwei Luo,Shuai Yuan,Zhenya Yang,Yansheng Li,Zhe Liu,Hengshuang Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为EO-WM的视频扩散Transformer模型，通过引入物理知情的调节机制，显著提升了地球观测预测模型在极端天气条件下的响应保真度和预测准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的地球观测预测方法存在局限性：确定性模型无法处理预测的不确定性，而基于扩散的模型往往忽略了天气因素的物理本质。此外，现有基准测试过于关注重构精度，缺乏对模型是否能准确响应天气变化（如极端气候压力）的评估。

Method: 提出了一种基于视频扩散Transformer的框架（EO-WM），核心创新点在于一种物理知情的调节机制：将气象强迫分解为气候基准、天气异常和累积物理压力三个维度，通过独立的路径进行特征处理，并累积异常强迫以捕捉持续性的环境压力影响。此外，还构建了两个针对性诊断基准：极端夏季基准和季节匹配对基准。

Result: 在植被指数（NDVI）下降幅度的预测中，误差相对降低了5.63%，方向命中率提升了7.80%，且在保持标准像素级指标竞争力的同时，在极端气候下的预测行为表现出显著的优越性。

Conclusion: EO-WM通过引入物理先验和解耦的气象调节机制，有效地解决了地球观测（EO）预测中对极端天气响应不足的问题，为环境监测和灾害预警提供了更可靠的预测模型。

Abstract: Earth Observation (EO) forecasting aims to predict future Earth surface dynamics from satellite observations under changing meteorological conditions. In this paper, we view this task as a partially observed, weather-driven world modeling problem, in which weather acts as a conditioning signal, while forecasting remains uncertain due to sparse observations and unobserved land-surface states. However, existing methods do not fully capture this setting: deterministic models collapse uncertainty into a single future prediction, while diffusion-based methods typically treat weather variables as undifferentiated conditioning signals, and existing benchmarks focus mainly on reconstruction accuracy rather than whether forecasts respond correctly to changed weather forcing.We introduce EO-WM, a video diffusion transformer for multispectral EO forecasting. EO-WM incorporates a physically informed conditioning framework that represents meteorological forcing through a climatological baseline, weather anomalies, and cumulative physical stress signals. Specifically, it separates baseline and anomaly through distinct conditioning pathways, and accumulates anomalous forcing over time to capture sustained heat and drought stress. To evaluate weather-response behavior beyond standard metrics, we introduce two diagnostic benchmarks: an Extreme Summer Benchmark for severity-aware prediction of vegetation degradation under extreme weather, and a Seasonal Matched-Pair Benchmark for testing response fidelity under changed weather forcing. Experiments show that EO-WM reduces the error in predicted Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) decline amplitude by a relative 5.63% and improves directional hit rate by a relative 7.80%, while remaining competitive on standard pixel-level metrics. The benchmarks and model will be made open-source at https://github.com/Luo-Z13/EO-WM.

### [234] [Simulation-based inference for rapid Bayesian parameter estimation in epidemiological models: a comparison with MCMC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27286)
*Alina Bazarova,Johann Fredrik Jadebeck,Henrik Zunker,Carolina J. Klett-Tammen,Torben Heinsohn,Wolfgang Wiechert,Katharina Noeh,Stefan Kesselheim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过对比实验表明，相比于传统的MCMC，使用神经网络的基于仿真的推理（SBI）能在大规模流行病学模型校准中实现数倍至百倍的计算提速，且能保持高精度的后验估计，为实时流行病预测提供了高效的技术路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机械论流行病学模型在传染病预测中应用广泛，但使用传统的MCMC进行贝叶斯校准时，在高维非线性系统或需要近实时分析的情境下，计算成本极高。因此，研究团队旨在探索SBI作为一种更快速、可扩展的替代方案。

Method: 研究采用了基于神经网络后验估计（Neural Posterior Estimation）的SBI方法，针对机械论SECIR模型进行校准。作者利用2020年德国COVID-19重症监护（ICU）占用数据，在31天和201天的不同推理窗口下，将SBI与传统的马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法进行了比较。评价指标包括Wasserstein距离、KL散度以及后验预测检查。

Result: 实验结果显示，SBI与MCMC在后验分布和预测轨迹上具有高度一致性。在计算性能方面，SBI表现出巨大的优势：在31天的推理问题上，SBI将计算时间从约1000秒缩短至60-70秒；在更复杂的201天推理任务中，SBI仅需约157秒，而MCMC则需要超过19000秒。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了基于仿真的推理（SBI）在机械论流行病学模型校准中是一种高效且可扩展的替代方案。相比于传统的MCMC方法，SBI能够显著降低计算成本，同时保持高度的后验估计准确性，非常适合需要快速响应的实时流行病预测和决策支持。

Abstract: Mechanistic epidemiological models are widely used to support infectious disease forecasting and public-health decision making. Bayesian calibration of such models is commonly performed using Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC), which can become computationally expensive for high-dimensional nonlinear systems and repeated near-real-time analyses. Here, we investigate simulation-based inference (SBI) using neural posterior estimation as a scalable alternative for Bayesian calibration of a mechanistic SECIR epidemiological model using COVID-19 intensive care unit (ICU) occupancy data from Germany during 2020. We compared SBI and MCMC across multiple epidemic phases using both 31-day inference windows and a substantially more challenging 201-day reconstruction problem involving multiple transmission change points. Posterior agreement was evaluated quantitatively using Wasserstein distances and Kullback-Leibler divergences together with posterior predictive checks. Across the 31-day windows, SBI recovered posterior distributions in strong agreement with MCMC while accurately reproducing observed ICU trajectories. In the 201-day setting, SBI preserved the dominant posterior structure despite increased uncertainty. SBI, by combining CPU and GPU resources, substantially reduced computational runtime compared with MCMC, which was restricted to running on CPUs. Whereas MCMC required approximately 1000 seconds for the 31-day inference problems, SBI achieved comparable posterior and predictive performance in approximately 60-70 seconds on a single GPU. For the 201-day inference problem, SBI required an average of 157 seconds, while the MCMC runs took over 19,000 seconds. Our results demonstrate that SBI provides a rapid and computationally efficient framework for Bayesian calibration of mechanistic epidemiological models, supporting repeated near-real-time inference and rapid outbreak analysis.

### [235] [Prompt Injection in Automated Résumé Screening with Large Language Models: Single and Multi-Injection Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27287)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型被广泛应用于简历筛选，候选人存在利用提示工程手段对算法进行策略性操纵的动机，研究旨在揭示这种“提示注入”攻击的有效性、局限性及其对招聘公平性的影响。

Method: 通过受控实验的方法，研究了在简历中添加“提示注入”（即旨在影响模型评估而非增加实质资质的自荐文本）对候选人排名结果的影响，并分析了在不同候选人质量分布（同质与异质）及不同注入普及率下的系统表现。

Result: 实验表明，在候选人质量同质且注入行为稀少时，提示注入能可靠提升排名；但随着注入者比例增加，其效力会迅速衰减并最终失效。在质量异质的情况下，注入虽然整体效果有限，但仍可能导致低质量候选人意外超越高质量候选人，引发公平性风险。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在自动化招聘筛选中存在明显的“提示注入”漏洞。当操纵行为较少且候选人水平相近时，该行为效果最显著，但随普及率上升而失效；同时，它可能导致低质量候选人获得不公平的竞争优势，给招聘系统的公正性带来挑战。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to screen and rank job applicants, creating incentives for candidates to strategically manipulate algorithmic hiring systems. We study prompt injection in automated résumé screening, defined as subtle self-promotional text that introduces no new qualifications but is designed to influence LLM evaluations. Using controlled experiments, we show that prompt injection reliably improves applicant rankings when résumé quality is homogeneous and few candidates inject. However, its effectiveness rapidly diminishes as more candidates inject, collapsing when manipulation becomes widespread. When candidate quality is heterogeneous, prompt injection is less effective on average, but can occasionally allow lower-quality candidates to outrank higher-quality ones, raising fairness concerns. Overall, LLM-based screening is most vulnerable when manipulation is rare and candidate quality differences are small. Code and resources are publicly available at: https://github.com/preetb1199/Prompt_Injection_ACL26

### [236] [When Does Combining Language Models Help? A Co-Failure Ceiling on Routing, Voting, and Mixture-of-Agents Across 67 Frontier Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27288)
*Josef Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了多模型大语言模型系统的准确率上限受限于“共同错误率”（beta），证明了仅通过增加模型数量而非提升错误互补性，很难显著超越单个最优模型的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常关注多模型大语言模型系统（如Agent混合、路由等）在提升准确率方面的能力，但缺乏对这类系统性能上限的理论界定。作者旨在探讨为何这些系统在某些情况下提升有限，并揭示了传统诊断指标（如成对误差相关性）无法准确识别系统性能瓶颈的问题。

Method: 研究团队分析了来自21个供应商的67个大模型在数学和代码任务上的表现，引入了“共同错误率（beta）”作为评估指标，并对比了常用的“平均成对误差相关性（rho）”。同时，利用Clopper-Pearson界限为模型组合的潜在增益提供了有限样本证书，并使用四分相关校准的单因子模型及高斯Copula模型进行实证分析。

Result: 实验显示，现有的统计模型严重低估了“共同错误率”：在数学任务中观测到的beta值为0.052，远高于高斯Copula模型预测的0.023。研究还发现，共同错误往往源于问题形式而非知识本身。在可验证任务中，单纯组合模型带来的增益极小，性能提升主要依赖于模型在不同问题上出现互补性错误的能力。

Conclusion: 多模型系统（如路由、投票、级联）的性能上限受到“共同错误率”（beta）的严格制约。研究表明，仅通过增加模型数量来提升性能的效果有限，真正关键在于模型间的错误多样性，而非仅仅依靠模型组合的统计相关性。在没有强查询级路由信号的情况下，组合模型往往难以超越性能最优的单个模型。

Abstract: Multi-model LLM systems such as routing, voting, cascades, fusion, and mixture-of-agents are used to beat single-model accuracy. We show that their gain is capped by a quantity the field rarely reports. For any policy whose output is one member model answer, accuracy cannot exceed one minus beta, where beta is the rate at which every model is wrong on the same query. In contrast, the usual diagnostic, average pairwise error correlation rho, cannot identify beta: error laws with identical marginals and pairwise correlations can have different all-wrong rates. A Clopper-Pearson bound on beta gives a finite-sample certificate on the largest gain any router, vote, or cascade could deliver before training a router.
  Across 67 models from 21 providers, a tetrachoric-calibrated single-factor model still underprices the all-wrong tail: on open-ended mathematics, observed beta is 0.052 versus 0.023 under the full 67-model Gaussian copula, about 2.5 times underpricing, with 90 percent CI 1.7 to 3.4 and k equals 17. The effect recurs on execution-graded code, where beta is 0.079. Re-asking the same GPQA-Diamond questions in free-response rather than multiple-choice form reopens the tail, with beta 0.127 and a five-judge panel with kappa 0.73 to 0.92, locating co-failure in answer format rather than subject. At matched quality, low-rho heterogeneous ensembles beat high-rho Self-MoA, but on checkable tasks in our pool, combining models rarely beats the single best model without a strong query-level routing signal. Gains come from models failing on different questions, not from adding more models.

</details>

Abstract: Digital twins have emerged as a promising paradigm for personalized healthcare, enabling modeling of individual behavior and health trajectories. In this work, we propose a language-based digital twin framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to mimic the conversational behavior of elderly individuals by incorporating stylometric cues and contextual metadata. To evaluate fidelity and cognitive consistency, we introduce a multi-head conditional variational autoencoder (cVAE) that jointly measures reconstruction quality and predicts cognitive scores. Experiments on the I-CONECT dataset show that the digital twin preserves identity-specific characteristics and achieves reconstruction and MoCA prediction errors comparable to real data, while outperforming baseline GPT-generated responses. These results highlight the potential of language-based digital twins as a scalable and non-invasive approach for personalized and continuous cognitive health monitoring.
